Remember this: whatever you have, you use it or you lose it!

一种想要打破它的强烈欲望！你当然知道，没有人可以被催眠的另一个人没有自愿被催眠。这种意愿通常表现为对生活漠不关心，缺乏抱负，恐惧，目标不明确，以及许多其他形式。大自然不需要征得一个人的同意就可以把他置于催眠的节奏之下。它只需要发现他毫无防备，通过任何形式的忽视使用他自己的心灵。记住: 无论你拥有什么，你要么使用它，要么失去它！

All successful attempts to break the habit of drifting must be done before nature makes the habit permanent, through hypnotic rhythm.

所有打破漂流习惯的成功尝试都必须在大自然通过催眠的节奏使这个习惯永久化之前完成。

Q As I understand you, hypnotic rhythm is a natural law through which nature fixes the vibration of all environments. Is that true?

正如我所理解的，催眠节律是一个自然法则，通过它，大自然固定了所有环境的振动。是真的吗？

A Yes, nature uses hypnotic rhythm to make one’s dominating thoughts and one’s thought-habits permanent. That is why poverty is disease. Nature makes it so by fixing permanently the thought-habits of all who accept poverty as an unavoidable circumstance.

答: 是的，大自然使用催眠的节奏使一个人的主导思想和思维习惯永久存在。这就是为什么贫穷是疾病。所有接受贫穷是不可避免的环境的人的思维习惯都被永久地固定下来，大自然就是这样做的。

Through this same law of hypnotic rhythm, nature will also fix permanently positive thoughts of opulence and prosperity.

通过这同样的催眠律，大自然也将永久地固定富裕和繁荣的积极思想。

Perhaps you will better understand the working principle of hypnotic rhythm if I tell you its nature is to fix permanently all habits whether they are mental or physical. If your mind fears poverty, your mind will attract poverty. If your mind demands opulence and expects it, your mind will attract the physical and financial equivalents of opulence. This is in accordance with an immutable law of nature.

如果我告诉你催眠节奏的本质是永久地固定所有的习惯，不管它们是精神上的还是身体上的，也许你会更好地理解它的工作原理。如果你的头脑害怕贫穷，你的头脑就会吸引贫穷。如果你的头脑要求富裕，并期望它，你的头脑将吸引物质和财政等价物的富裕。这符合一个不可改变的自然法则。

Hill first wrote about the Law of Attraction in the March 1919 issue of his Golden Rule magazine. Within the last decade, this immutable law of nature has been popularized around the world by the resounding success of the book and movie The Secret.

1919年3月，Hill 在他的《黄金法则》杂志上首次写到了吸引力法则(新思维)。在过去的十年里，这个不可改变的自然法则已经因为《秘密》这本书和电影的巨大成功而在世界范围内普及开来。

Q Did the writer of that sentence in the Bible, “Whatsoever a man soweth, that shall he also reap,” have in mind this law of nature?

问: 《圣经》中那句话“人所种的，就是他所收的”的作者有没有记住这个自然法则？

A He could have nothing else in mind. The statement is true. You can see evidence of its truth in all human relationships.

A 他脑子里不可能有别的东西。这句话是真的。你可以在所有的人际关系中看到它的真实性。

Q And that is why the man who forms the habit of drifting through life must accept whatever life hands him. Is that correct?

这就是为什么养成漂泊生活习惯的人必须接受生活赋予他的任何东西。是这样吗？

A That is absolutely correct. Life pays the drifter its own price, on its own terms. The non-drifter makes life pay on his own terms.

A 完全正确。生活为流浪汉付出了自己的代价，以自己的方式。非流浪汉用自己的方式让生活付出代价。

Q Doesn’t the question of morals enter into what one gets from life?

难道道道德问题不会影响一个人从生活中得到什么吗？

A To be sure, but only for the reason that one’s morals have an influence on one’s thoughts. No one can collect what he wants from life merely by being good, if that is what you want to know.

可以肯定，但仅仅是因为一个人的道德对他的思想有影响。如果你想知道的话，没有人可以仅仅通过做一个好人就能从生活中得到他想要的东西。

Q No, I guess not. I see what you mean. We are all where we are and what we are because of our own deeds.

问: 不，我想不会。我明白你的意思。因为我们自己的所作所为，我们才能有今天的成就。

A No, not exactly. You are where you are and what you are because of your thoughts and your deeds.

A 不，不完全是这样。因为你的思想和行为，你才能有今天的成就和成就。

Q Then there is no such reality as luck, is there?

那么，根本就没有运气这回事，不是吗？

A Emphatically no. Circumstances which people do not understand are classified under the heading of luck. Back of every reality is a cause. Often the cause is so far removed from the effect that the circumstance can be explained only by attributing it to the operation of luck. Nature knows no such law as luck. It is a man-made hypothesis with which he explains away things he does not understand. The terms “luck” and “miracle” are twin sisters. Neither of them has any real existence except in the imaginations of people. Both are used to explain that which people do not understand. Remember this: everything having a real existence is capable of proof. Keep this one truth in mind and you will become a sounder thinker.

A 断然否定。人们不理解的情况被归类为运气。每一个现实背后都有一个原因。原因往往与结果相去甚远，以至于环境只能通过将其归因于运气而得到解释。自然界没有运气这样的法则。这是一个人为的假设，他用这个假设来解释他不懂的东西。“运气”和“奇迹”这两个词是孪生姐妹。除了在人们的想象中，他们都没有真正的存在。两者都是用来解释人们不理解的东西。记住这一点: 任何真实存在的事物都有证明的能力。记住这一点，你就会成为一个健全的思考者。

Q Which is more important, one’s thoughts or one’s deeds?

问: 一个人的想法和行为哪个更重要？

A All deeds follow thoughts. There can be no deeds without their having first been patterned in thought. Moreover, all thoughts have a tendency to clothe themselves in their physical counterpart. One’s dominating thoughts, that is, the thoughts one mixes with the emotions, desire, hope, faith, fear, hate, greed, enthusiasm, not only have a tendency to clothe themselves in their physical equivalent, but they are bound to do so.

一切行动都跟随着思想。如果没有事先在思想上的模式化，就不可能有事迹。此外，所有的思想都倾向于给自己的物理对应物披上外衣。一个人的主导思想，也就是说，这些思想混合着情感、欲望、希望、信仰、恐惧、憎恨、贪婪、热情，不仅有一种给自己穿上等同的衣服的倾向，而且它们必然会这样做。

Q That reminds me to ask you to tell me more about yourself. Where, in addition to the minds of people, do you dwell and operate?

问: 这提醒我让你告诉我更多关于你自己的事情。除了人们的思想之外，你在哪里居住和运作？

A I operate wherever there is something I can control and appropriate. I have already told you I am the negative portion of the electron of matter.

A 我在任何我可以控制和适当的地方工作。我已经告诉过你们，我是物质电子的负部分。

• I am the explosion in lightning.

•我是闪电中的爆炸。

• I am the pain in disease and physical suffering.

•我是疾病带来的痛苦和身体上的折磨。

• I am the unseen general in warfare.

•我是战争中看不见的将军。

• I am the unknown commissioner of poverty and famine.

•我是贫穷和饥荒问题的无名专员。

• I am the executioner extraordinaire at death.

•我是死亡的杰出刽子手。

• I am the inspirer of lust after the flesh.

•我是肉欲的激发者。

• I am the creator of jealousy and envy and greed.

•我是嫉妒、嫉妒和贪婪的创造者。

• I am the instigator of fear.

•我是恐惧的煽动者。

• I am the genius who converts the achievements of men of science into instruments of death.

•我是把科学家的成就转化为死亡工具的天才。

• I am the destroyer of harmony in all manner of human relationships.

•我是各种人际关系中和谐的破坏者。

• I am the antithesis of justice.

•我是正义的对立面。

• I am the driving force in all immorality.

•我是所有不道德行为的驱动力。

• I am the stalemate of all good.

•我是所有好事的僵局。

• I am anxiety, suspense, superstition, and insanity.

•我是焦虑、悬念、迷信和疯狂。

• I am the destroyer of hope and faith.

•我是希望和信仰的破坏者。

• I am the inspirer of destructive gossip and scandal.

•我是破坏性八卦和丑闻的制造者。

• I am the discourager of free and independent thought.

•我不鼓励自由和独立的思想。

• In brief, I am the creator of all forms of human misery, the instigator of discouragement and disappointment.

•简言之，我是所有形式的人类痛苦的创造者，是沮丧和失望的煽动者。

Q And you do not call that cold and cruel?

问: 你不认为那是冷酷和残忍吗？

A I call that definite and dependable.

A 我称之为明确而可靠。

The world depression broke up the habits of men everywhere and redistributed the sources of opportunity in all walks of life on an unprecedented scale.

世界大萧条打破了世界各地人们的习惯，以前所未有的规模重新分配了各行各业的机会来源。

The drifter’s pet alibi, with which he tries to explain away his undesirable position, is his cry that the world has run dry of opportunities.

那个流浪汉最喜欢的借口，就是他大声疾呼，说这个世界已经没有机会了，他试图用这个借口来解释自己不受欢迎的处境。

Non-drifters do not wait for opportunity to be placed in their way. They create opportunity to fit their desires and demands of life!

非漂流者不会等待机会被放置在他们的方式。他们创造机会来满足自己的欲望和生活需求！

Hill speaks of the great opportunities that arose during the Great Depression and the fortunes that were made by those who seized those opportunities. I believe that Hill would say the same thing in our own day . . . many opportunities exist today because of the economic turmoil. Will you seize one and create your own opportunity to fit your desires and demands of life?

希尔谈到了大萧条时期出现的巨大机遇，以及那些抓住这些机遇的人所创造的财富。我相信希尔在我们这个时代也会说同样的话... ... 由于经济动荡，今天存在着许多机会。你会抓住一个机会，创造自己的机会来满足自己的欲望和生活的要求吗？

Q Are non-drifters smart enough to avoid the influence of hypnotic rhythm?

非漂移者是否足够聪明以避免催眠节奏的影响？

A No one is smart enough to dodge the influence of hypnotic rhythm. One could just as easily avoid the influence of the law of gravity. The law of hypnotic rhythm fixes permanently the dominating thoughts of men, whether they be drifters or non-drifters.

没有人聪明到可以躲避催眠节奏的影响。人们可以很容易地避免万有引力定律的影响。催眠律法永久地固定了人们的主导思想，无论他们是流浪者还是非流浪者。

There is no reason why a non-drifter would want to avoid the influence of hypnotic rhythm, because that law is favorable to him. It helps him convert his dominating aims, plans, and purposes into their physical replicas. It fixes his habits of thought and makes them permanent.

没有理由说一个非漂泊者会想要避免催眠节律的影响，因为这个规律对他是有利的。这有助于他将自己的主导目标、计划和目的转化为他们的物理副本。它固定了他的思维习惯，并使之永久化。

Only the drifter would wish to dodge the influence of hypnotic rhythm.

只有流浪汉才希望躲避催眠节奏的影响。

Q For the better portion of my adult life I have been a drifter. How did I manage to escape being swept into the whirlpool of hypnotic rhythm?

问: 在我成年生活的大部分时间里，我一直是个流浪汉。我是如何设法逃脱被催眠节奏的漩涡的？

A You haven’t escaped. The major portion of your dominating thoughts and desires, since you reached adulthood, has been a well-defined, definite desire to understand all the potentialities of the mind.

A 你没有逃脱。自从你成年以来，你主导思想和欲望的主要部分，就是一种明确的、明确的渴望去理解心灵的所有潜力。

You may have drifted on thoughts of lesser importance, but you did not drift in connection with this desire. Because you did not drift, you are now recording a document which gives you exactly what your dominating thoughts demanded of life.

你可能漂浮在一些不那么重要的想法上，但是你并没有随着这个欲望而漂浮。因为你没有随波逐流，所以你现在正在记录一份文件，这份文件恰恰给了你主导思想对生活的要求。

Q Why doesn’t your opposition use hypnotic rhythm to make permanent one’s higher thoughts and nobler deeds? Why does your opposition permit you to use this stupendous force as a means of entangling people in a web of evil spun by their own thoughts and deeds? Why does your opposition not outwit you by binding people with thoughts which build and lift them above your influence?

问: 为什么你的对手不使用催眠的节奏来使一个人的更高级的思想和更高尚的行为永久化？为什么你的反对派允许你使用这种巨大的力量作为一种手段，把人们卷入由他们自己的思想和行为所编织的邪恶网络中？为什么你的反对者没有用思想捆绑人们，让他们超越你的影响力，从而胜过你呢？

A The law of hypnotic rhythm is available to all who will use it. I make use of it more effectively than does my opposition because I offer people more attractive bribes to think my sort of thoughts and indulge in my sort of deeds.

A 催眠节律对所有愿意使用它的人都是有效的。我比我的反对者更有效地利用它，因为我向人们提供更有吸引力的贿赂，让他们思考我的想法，沉迷于我的行为。

Q In other words, you control people by making negative thinking and destructive deeds pleasing to them. Is that correct?

换句话说，你通过消极的想法和破坏性的行为取悦他人来控制他人，对吗？

A That is the idea, exactly!

A 就是这个意思，没错！





Chapter Seven

SEEDS OF FEAR

第七章恐惧的种子

Q I HAVE OFTEN WONDERED WHY your opposition—what we earthbound call God—does not annihilate you? Can you tell me why?

问: 我经常想知道为什么你的反对ーー我们俗称为上帝ーー没有消灭你? 你能告诉我为什么吗？

A Because the power is as much mine as his. It is as available to me as to him. That is what I have been trying to get over to you. The highest power in the universe can be used for constructive purposes, through what you call God, or it can be used for negative purposes, through what you call the Devil. And something more important still, it can be used by any human being just as effectively as by God or the Devil.

A 因为权力是我的，也是他的。这对我和他一样重要。这就是我一直试图让你明白的。宇宙中最高的力量可以被用于建设性的目的，通过你所谓的上帝，或者它可以被用于消极的目的，通过你所谓的魔鬼。更重要的是，它可以被任何人有效地使用，就像被上帝或魔鬼使用一样。

Q You make a far-reaching claim. Can you prove your claim?

你提出了一个影响深远的要求。你能证明你的要求吗？

A Yes, but it would be better if you proved it for yourself. The Devil’s word is not worth much among you earthbound sinners. Neither is God’s word. You fear the Devil and refuse to trust your God; therefore you have but one source available through which you may appropriate the benefit of universal power, and that is by trusting and using your own power of thought. This is the direct road to the universal storehouse of Infinite Intelligence. There is no other road available to any human being.

A 是的，但是如果你自己能证明的话会更好。魔鬼的话在你们这些尘世的罪人中是没有价值的。神的话也不是。你害怕魔鬼，拒绝相信你的上帝; 因此，你只有一个来源，通过这个来源，你可以获得普遍力量的好处，那就是相信和使用你自己的思想力量。这是通往无限智慧这个宇宙宝库的直接道路。对任何人来说，没有别的路可走。

Q Why have we earthbound not found the road to Infinite Intelligence sooner?

问: 为什么我们这些凡夫俗子没有早点找到通往无限智慧的道路？

A Because I have intercepted you and led you off the path by planting in your minds thoughts which destroy your power to use your minds constructively. I have made it attractive to you to use the Power of Infinite Intelligence to attain negative ends, through greed, avarice, lust, envy, and hatred. Remember, your mind attracts that which your mind dwells upon. To divert you away from my opposition, I had only to feed you on thoughts helpful to my cause.

因为我已经拦截了你们，并且通过在你们的头脑中植入那些摧毁你们建设性地使用你们头脑的能力的思想，把你们带离了道路。通过贪婪、贪婪、欲望、嫉妒和仇恨，我已经让你们觉得用无限智慧的力量达到消极的目的是有吸引力的。记住，你的思想吸引着你的思想。为了转移你对我反对意见的注意力，我只需要告诉你一些对我的事业有帮助的想法就行了。

Q If I understand what you are saying, you are admitting that no human being need fear the Devil or worry about how to flatter God!

问: 如果我明白你的意思，你就是在承认没有人需要害怕魔鬼或者担心如何奉承上帝！

A That is it precisely. This admission may put a crimp in my style, but I have this satisfaction of knowing it may also slow down my opposition by sending people direct to the source of all power.

A 正是如此。这种承认可能会妨碍我的风格，但我有这种满足感，因为我知道它也可能减缓我的反对，因为它可以把人们直接送到所有力量的源头。

Here, as in some other points during the dialogue, Hill gets explicitly theological. Using the Devil as a foil and letting words come out of the mouth of the symbol of evil, Napoleon Hill can lay out his thoughts and feelings about God—Infinite Intelligence—as the ultimate source for his overall philosophy of success.

在这里，正如在对话中的其他一些观点，希尔得到了明确的神学。拿破仑 · 希尔以魔鬼为衬托，让邪恶的象征说出话来，可以展示他对上帝ーー无限智慧ーー的思想和感情，这是他整个成功哲学的根本来源。

Q In other words, if you cannot control people through negative bribes or fear, then you wish to kick over the entire apple cart and show people how to go directly to God? Are you, by any chance, in politics too? Your technique seems frightfully familiar.

换句话说，如果你不能通过负面的贿赂或恐惧来控制人们，那么你希望踢翻整个苹果车，告诉人们如何直接去找上帝？你有没有可能也参与政治？你的技巧似乎非常熟悉。

A Am I in politics? If I am not in politics, who do you believe starts depressions and forces people into wars? Surely you would not lay this at the door of my opposition? As I have already told you, I have allies in all walks of life, to help me in connection with all human relationships.

A 我从政了吗？如果我不从政，你认为是谁引发了萧条，迫使人们陷入战争？你肯定不会把这件事告诉我的反对者吧？正如我已经告诉过你们的，我在各行各业都有盟友，在所有人类关系中帮助我。

Q Why don’t you take over the churches and use them outright in your cause?

问: 你为什么不接管教会，直接把它们用在你的事业上呢？

A Do you think I am a fool? Who would keep alive the fear of the Devil if I subdued the churches? Who would serve as a decoy to attract the attention of people while I manipulate their minds if I did not have some agency through which to sow the seeds of fear and doubt? The cleverest thing I do is to use the allies of my opposition to keep the fear of hell burning in the minds of people. As long as people fear something, no matter what, I will keep a grip on them.

A 你认为我是傻瓜吗？如果我征服了众教会，谁还能保持对魔鬼的恐惧呢？如果我没有某种机构来播下恐惧和怀疑的种子，当我操纵人们的思想时，谁会充当诱饵来吸引人们的注意力呢？我所做的最聪明的事情就是利用我的反对者的同盟，让人们不再惧怕地狱。只要人们害怕什么，不管是什么，我都会紧紧抓住他们。

Q I am beginning to see your scheme. You use the churches to plant the seed of fear and uncertainty and indefiniteness in the minds of people. These negative states of mind cause people to form the habit of drifting. This habit crystallizes into permanency through the law of hypnotic rhythm; then the victim is helpless to help himself, is that right? Hypnotic rhythm, then, is something to be watched and respected?

我开始看出你的计划了。你利用教会在人们的心中播下恐惧、不确定和不确定的种子。这些消极的心理状态导致人们形成漂泊的习惯。这个习惯通过催眠的律法变成了永久性的; 那么受害者是无助于自救的，对吗？那么，催眠的节奏是需要观察和尊重的东西吗？

A A better way of stating the truth is that hypnotic rhythm is something to be studied, understood, and voluntarily applied to attain definite desired ends.

一个更好的说明真相的方法是，催眠节律是一种需要研究、理解和自愿应用的东西，以达到确定的预期目的。

Q If the force of hypnotic rhythm is not voluntarily applied to attain definite ends, may it be a great danger?

如果催眠节律的力量不是自愿地用于达到确定的目的，它会是一个巨大的危险吗？

A Yes, and for the reason that it operates automatically. If it is not consciously applied to attain a desired end, it can, and it will, operate to attain undesired ends.

A 是的，因为它是自动运行的。如果不是有意识地应用它来达到一个预期的目的，它就能够，而且它将会，操作来达到不预期的目的。

Take the simple illustration of climate, for example. Anyone can see and understand that nature forces every living thing and every element of matter to adjust itself to her climates. In the tropics she creates trees which bear fruit and reproduce themselves. She forces the trees to adjust themselves to her scorching sun! She forces them to put out leaves suitable for protection against the rays of the sun. These same trees could not survive if removed to the arctic regions where nature has established an entirely different climate.

举个简单的气候例子。任何人都可以看到并理解，自然迫使每一种生物和每一种物质元素调整自己以适应它的气候。在热带地区，她创造了结果和繁殖自己的树木。她强迫树木适应灼热的阳光！她强迫他们放出适合遮挡阳光的树叶。如果把这些树移到北极地区，这些树就不能生存，因为那里的自然环境已经形成了完全不同的气候。

In the colder climate she creates trees which are adjusted to survive and to reproduce themselves, but they could not survive if transplanted in the tropical regions. In the same manner, nature clothes her animals, giving to those in each different climate a covering suited to their comfort and survival in that climate.

在较冷的气候条件下，她创造的树木适应了生存和繁殖，但是如果移植到热带地区，它们就无法生存。同样地，大自然给她的动物穿上衣服，给那些生活在不同气候下的动物穿上适合它们舒适和生存的衣服。

In a similar manner, nature forces upon the minds of men the influences of their environment, which are stronger than the individual’s own thoughts. Children are forced to take on the nature of all influences of those around them unless their own thoughts are stronger than the influences.

同样地，大自然强加在人类头脑上的环境的影响比个人自己的思想更强大。孩子们被迫接受周围人的影响，除非他们自己的思想比周围人的影响更强大。

Nature sets up a definite rhythm for every environment, and everything within the range of that rhythm is forced to conform to it. Man, alone, has the power to establish his own rhythm of thought providing he exercises this privilege before hypnotic rhythm has forced upon him the influences of his environment.

大自然为每个环境设定了一个明确的节奏，在这个节奏范围内的一切都被迫顺应它。只有在催眠的节奏强加于人的环境影响之前，人才有能力建立自己的思维节奏，只要他行使这种特权。

Every home, every place of business, every town and village and every street and community center has its own definite, discernible rhythm. If you wish to know what a difference there is in the rhythms of streets, take a walk up Fifth Avenue, in New York, and then down a street in the slums! All forms of rhythm become permanent with time.

每个家庭，每个商业场所，每个城镇和村庄，每条街道和社区中心都有自己明确的、可辨别的节奏。如果你想知道街道的节奏有什么不同，可以沿着纽约第五大道散步，然后沿着贫民窟的街道走！所有形式的节奏都会随着时间而变得永恒。

Q Does each individual have his own rhythm of thought?

每个人都有自己的思维节奏吗？

A Yes. That is precisely the major difference between individuals. The person who thinks in terms of power, success, opulence, sets up a rhythm which attracts these desirable possessions. The person who thinks in terms of misery, failure, defeat, discouragement, and poverty attracts these undesirable influences. This explains why both success and failure are the result of habit. Habit establishes one’s rhythm of thought, and that rhythm attracts the object of one’s dominating thoughts.

A 是的。这正是个体之间的主要差异。一个以权力、成功、财富为考虑因素的人，会建立一种节奏，吸引这些理想的财富。那些以痛苦、失败、挫败、沮丧和贫穷来思考的人会受到这些不良影响。这就解释了为什么成功和失败都是习惯的结果。习惯建立了一个人的思维节奏，这种节奏吸引了一个人主导思想的对象。

Q Hypnotic rhythm is something resembling a magnet which attracts things for which it has a magnetic affinity. Is that correct?

催眠节奏就像一块磁铁，吸引着具有磁性亲和力的东西。是这样吗？

A Yes, that is correct. That is why the poverty-stricken herd themselves into the same communities. It explains that old saying, “Misery loves company.” It also explains why people who begin to succeed in any undertaking find that success multiplies, with less effort, as time goes on.

A 是的，没错。这就是为什么贫困的人们会聚集在同一个社区。它解释了那句老话，“同病相怜。”这也解释了为什么那些开始在任何事业上取得成功的人会发现，随着时间的推移，成功会以更少的努力而倍增。

All successful people use hypnotic rhythm, either consciously or unconsciously, by expecting and demanding success. The demand becomes a habit, hypnotic rhythm takes over the habit, and the law of harmonious attraction translates it into its physical equivalent.

所有成功的人都有意无意地使用催眠的节奏来期待和要求成功。需求变成了一种习惯，催眠的节奏取代了习惯，和谐的吸引力法则将其转化为身体上的等价物。

Q In other words, if I know what I want from life, demand it and back my demand by a willingness to pay life’s price for what I want, and refuse to accept any substitutes, the law of hypnotic rhythm takes over my desire and helps, by natural and logical means, to transmute it into its physical counterpart. Is that true?

换句话说，如果我知道自己想从生活中得到什么，我愿意为自己想要的付出生命的代价，并拒绝接受任何替代品，那么催眠节奏法则就会接管我的欲望，并通过自然和合乎逻辑的方式，帮助我将它转化为身体上的对应物。是真的吗？

A That describes the way the law works.

A 描述了法律的运作方式。

Q Science has established irrefutable evidence that people are what they are because of heredity and environment. They bring over with them at birth a combination of all the physical qualities of all their numberless ancestors. After they arrive here, they reach the age of self-consciousness and from there on they shape their own personalities and more or less fix their own earthly destinations as the result of the environmental influences to which they are subjected, especially the influences which control them during early childhood. These two facts have been so well established there is no room for any intelligent person to question them. How can hypnotic rhythm change the nature of a physical body which is a combination of thousands of ancestors who have lived and died before one is born? How can hypnotic rhythm change the influence of one’s environment? People who are born in poverty and ignorance have a strong tendency to remain poverty-stricken and ignorant all through life. What, if anything, can hypnotic rhythm do about this?

科学已经确立了无可辩驳的证据，证明人是因为遗传和环境而成为现在的样子。他们一出生就带来了他们无数祖先的所有物质特性的组合。在他们到达这里之后，他们达到了私我意识的年龄，从那里他们塑造了自己的个性，或多或少地由于他们所受到的环境影响，特别是控制他们在幼年时期的影响，他们固定了自己的尘世目的地。这两个事实是如此确凿，以至于任何聪明人都没有机会去质疑它们。催眠的节奏是如何改变一个物质身体的本质的呢? 这个物质身体是成千上万在你出生之前已经生存和死亡的祖先的结合体？催眠节律如何改变环境的影响？出身贫寒、无知的人，一辈子都处于贫困和无知状态的倾向很强。催眠的节奏对此有什么作用呢？

A Hypnotic rhythm cannot change the nature of the physical body one inherits at birth, but it can and it does modify, change, control, and make permanent one’s environmental influences.

催眠的节奏不能改变一个人在出生时所继承的物质身体的本质，但是它可以并且确实改变、改变、控制，并且使一个人的环境影响永久化。

Q If I understand what you mean, a human being is forced by nature to take on and become a part of the environment he chooses or the environment that may be forced upon him?

问: 如果我明白你的意思，一个人是被自然所迫，成为他所选择的环境或者可能被强加于他的环境的一部分？

A That is correct, but there are ways and means by which an individual may resist the influences of an environment he does not wish to accept, and also a method of procedure by which one may reverse the application of hypnotic rhythm from negative to positive ends.

答: 这是正确的，但是有一些方法和手段，个人可以抵制他不愿接受的环境的影响，也有一种程序方法，通过这种方法，人们可以扭转催眠节奏从消极到积极的应用。

Q Do you mean that there is a definite method by which hypnotic rhythm can be made to serve instead of destroy one?

你的意思是说有一种明确的方法可以使催眠节律服务而不是摧毁一个人？

A I mean just that.

A 我就是这个意思。

Q Tell me how this astounding end may be attained.

问: 请告诉我这一令人震惊的结果将如何实现。

A For my description to be of any practical value, it will be necessarily lengthy because it will have to cover seven principles of psychology which must be understood and applied by all who use hypnotic rhythm to aid them in forcing life to yield that which they want.

要使我的描述具有任何实际价值，它必须是冗长的，因为它必须涵盖心理学的七个原则，这些原则必须被所有使用催眠节奏来帮助他们迫使生活屈服于他们想要的东西的人所理解和应用。

Q Then break your description into seven parts, each giving a detailed analysis of one of the seven principles, with simple instructions for its practical application.

问: 然后把你的描述分成七个部分，每个部分对七个原则中的一个进行详细的分析，并简单说明其实际应用。

I have always been fascinated with how Hill’s mind works. After building a case for impending doom, he now reveals the lifeline for anyone seeking success. This is a critical turning point. As you read further, will his “seven principles” capture your imagination, as they did mine?

我一直着迷于希尔的大脑是如何工作的。在为即将到来的厄运做好准备之后，他现在揭示了任何寻求成功的人的生命线。这是一个关键的转折点。当你进一步阅读时，他的“七项原则”是否会像我的那样激发你的想象力？





Chapter Eight

DEFINITENESS OF PURPOSE

第八章明确目标

Q YOUR MAJESTY WILL NOW PROCEED to unfold the secrets of the seven principles through which human beings may force life to provide them with spiritual, mental, and physical freedom.

陛下现在将开始揭示人类可能强迫生命提供给他们精神、心理和身体自由的七个原则的秘密。

In the rest of the book, Hill discusses these seven principles to attain spiritual, mental, and physical freedom:

在本书的其余部分，希尔讨论了获得精神、心理和身体自由的七个原则:

1. Definiteness of purpose

1. 明确目标

2. Mastery over self

2. 掌控自我

3. Learning from adversity

3. 从逆境中学习

4. Controlling environmental influence (associations)

4. 控制环境影响(协会)

5. Time (giving permanency to positive, rather than negative thought-habits and developing wisdom)

5. 时间(给予积极而不是消极的思维习惯以永久性，培养智慧)

6. Harmony (acting with definiteness of purpose to become the dominating influence in your own mental, spiritual, and physical environment)

(英译汉)和谐(带着明确的目标行动，在你自己的精神、精神和物理环境中成为主导影响力)

7. Caution (thinking through your plan before you act)

7. 谨慎(在行动之前仔细考虑你的计划)

Do not be sparing in your description of these principles. I want a complete illustration of how the principles may be used by anyone who chooses to use them. Tell us all you know about the principle of definiteness of purpose.

不要吝惜你对这些原则的描述。我想要一个完整的例子来说明这些原则可能被任何选择使用它们的人所使用。告诉我们你所知道的关于明确目标的原则。

The interrogator gains some momentum here and goes for the jugular. Do we have the courage, at moments of opportunity, to act as aggressively and with definiteness of purpose?

审讯人员在这里获得了一些动力，直击要害。我们是否有勇气，在有机会的时候，以一种积极的态度和明确的目标行事？

A If you go through with this mad idea of publishing my confession, you will open the gates of hell and turn loose all the precious souls I have collected back down through the ages. You will deprive me of souls yet unborn. You will release from my bondage millions now living. Stop, I beg of you.

如果你坚持这个疯狂的想法，发表我的忏悔，你将打开地狱之门，释放我从古至今收集的所有珍贵的灵魂。你会剥夺我未出生的灵魂。你将从我的束缚中解放出现在活着的数百万人。住手，我求求你。

Q Open up. Let’s hear what you have to say about the principle of definiteness of purpose.

让我们听听你对于明确目标的原则有什么要说的。

A You are pouring water on the fires of hell, but the responsibility is yours, not mine. I may as well tell you that any human being who can be definite in his aims and plans can make life hand over whatever is wanted.

A 你在地狱之火上浇水，但责任是你的，不是我的。我不妨告诉你，任何一个人，只要他的目标和计划是明确的，他就可以把生活交给任何他想要的东西。

Q That is a broad claim, Your Majesty. Do you wish to tone it down a bit?

问: 这是一个很宽泛的说法，陛下，您是否愿意把声音降低一点？

A Tone it down? No, I wish to tone it up. When you hear what I now have to say, you will understand why the principle of definiteness is so important. My opposition uses a clever little trick to cheat me of my control over people. The opposition knows that definiteness of purpose closes the door of one’s mind so tightly against me that I cannot break through unless I can induce one to form the habit of drifting.

调低音量？不，我希望它变得更加柔和。当你听到我现在要说的话，你就会明白为什么明确性原则如此重要。我的反对者使用了一个聪明的小伎俩来欺骗我对人民的控制。反对派知道，明确目标关闭了一个人的心灵之门，使我无法突破，除非我能引导一个人形成随波逐流的习惯。

Q Why doesn’t your opposition give your secret to all people by telling them to avoid you through definiteness of purpose? You have already admitted that two out of every hundred people belong to your opposition.

问: 为什么你的反对者不把你的秘密告诉所有人，告诉他们通过明确的目的避开你？你已经承认，每百人中有两人属于你的反对派。

A Because I am more clever than my opposition. I draw people away from definiteness with my promises. You see, I control more people than my opposition because I am a better salesman and a better showman. I attract people by feeding them liberally of the thought-habits in which they like to indulge.

A 因为我比我的对手更聪明。我用我的承诺把人们从确定性中拉开。你看，我控制的人比我的对手多，因为我是一个更好的推销员和表演者。我吸引人们的方法是，随意地告诉他们他们喜欢沉迷的思维习惯。

Q Is definiteness of purpose something with which one must be born or may it be acquired?

明确的目标是一个人必须出生的东西，还是可以获得的东西？

A Everyone, as I have told you before, is born with the privilege of being definite, but 98 out of every 100 people lose this privilege by sleeping on it. The privilege of definiteness can be maintained only by adopting it as a policy by which one is guided in all the affairs of life.

答: 正如我以前告诉过你的，每个人生来就具有明确的特权，但是每100个人中有98个人会因为睡在上面而失去这种特权。明确性的特权只有通过把它作为一项政策来保持，在生活的所有事务中都以它为指导。

Q Oh, I see! One takes advantage of the principle of definiteness just as one may build a strong physical body—through constant, systematic use. Is that it?

哦，我明白了！一个人利用明确性原则，就像一个人可以通过不断的、系统的运用来建立一个强壮的身体一样。是这样吗？

A You have stated the truth clearly and accurately.

A 你已经清楚而准确地陈述了事实。

Q Now I think we are getting somewhere, Your Majesty. We have at long last found the starting point from which all who become self-determining in life must take off.

现在我想我们有进展了，陛下。我们终于找到了一个起点，所有在生活中变得自主的人都必须从这个起点起飞。

We have discovered, from your astounding confession, that your greatest asset is man’s lack of caution, which enables you to lead him into the jungle of indefiniteness through simple bribes.

从你令人震惊的坦白中，我们已经发现，你最大的资产是人的不谨慎，这使你能够通过简单的贿赂把他带入不确定的丛林。

We have learned, beyond the question of doubt, that anyone who adopts definiteness of purpose as a policy and uses it in all of his daily experiences cannot be induced to form the habit of drifting. Without the aid of the drifting habit you are powerless to attract people through promises. Is this correct?

毫无疑问，我们已经认识到，任何把明确目标作为一种政策并在其所有日常经验中使用它的人，都不可能被诱导形成漂泊的习惯。没有漂泊习惯的帮助，你无法通过承诺来吸引别人。是这样吗？

A I couldn’t have stated the truth more clearly myself.

A 我自己已经说得再清楚不过了。

Q Go ahead, now, and describe how people neglect their privilege of being free and self-determining through indefiniteness and drifting.

继续，现在，描述一下人们是如何因为不确定和漂泊而忽视了自由和自主的特权。

A I have already made brief reference to this principle, but I will now go into more minute details as to how the principle works.

A 我已经简单地提到了这个原则，但是我现在要详细说明这个原则是如何起作用的。

I shall have to begin at the time of birth. When a child is born, it brings with it nothing but a physical body representing the evolutionary results of millions of years of ancestry.

我必须从出生时就开始。当一个孩子出生时，除了一个代表数百万年祖先进化结果的物质身体，它什么也没有带来。

Its mind is a total blank. When the child reaches the age of consciousness and begins to recognize the objects of its surroundings, it begins, also, to imitate others.

它的大脑完全是一片空白。当孩子到了有意识的年龄，开始认识周围事物的时候，他也开始模仿别人。

Imitation becomes a fixed habit. Naturally the child imitates, first of all, its parents! Then it begins to imitate its other relatives and daily associates, including its religious instructors and schoolteachers.

模仿成为一种固定的习惯。孩子自然会模仿，首先，他的父母！然后它开始模仿它的其他亲戚和日常伙伴，包括它的宗教教师和学校教师。

The imitation extends not merely to physical expression, but also to thought expression. If a child’s parents fear me and express that fear within range of the child’s hearing, the child picks up the fear through the habit of imitation and stores it away as a part of its subconscious stock of beliefs.

模仿不仅延伸到物理表达，也延伸到思想表达。如果一个孩子的父母害怕我，并在孩子听到的范围内表达这种恐惧，孩子就会通过模仿的习惯拾起这种恐惧，并把它作为潜意识信念的一部分储存起来。

If the child’s religious instructor expresses any form of fear of me (and they all do, in one form or another), that fear is added to the similar fear passed to the child by its parents, and the two forms of negative limitation are stored away in the subconscious mind to be drawn upon and used by me later in life.

如果孩子的宗教导师表现出对我的任何形式的恐惧(他们都表现出这种或那种形式的恐惧) ，那么这种恐惧就会增加到孩子的父母传递给孩子的类似的恐惧中，而这两种形式的消极限制就会储存在潜意识中，供我以后的生活中使用。

In a similar way the child learns, by imitation, to limit its power of thought by filling its mind with envy, hatred, greed, lust, revenge, and all the other negative impulses of thought which destroy all possibility of definiteness.

同样地，孩子通过模仿学习，通过用嫉妒、仇恨、贪婪、欲望、复仇和其他所有消极的思想冲动填满自己的头脑来限制自己的思想力量，这些冲动破坏了一切确定性的可能性。

Meanwhile I move in and induce the child to drift until I bind its mind through hypnotic rhythm.

与此同时，我走进去，引导孩子漂移，直到我通过催眠的节奏来约束他的思想。

Q Am I to understand from your remarks that you have to gain control of people while they are very young or lose your opportunity at them altogether?

问: 我是否可以从你的话中理解，你必须在人们还很年轻的时候控制他们，或者完全失去控制他们的机会？

A I prefer to claim them before they come into possession of their own minds. Once any person learns the power of his own thoughts, he becomes positive and difficult to subdue. As a matter of fact, I cannot control any human being who discovers and uses the principle of definiteness.

A 我宁愿在他们拥有自己的思想之前就认领他们。一旦任何人学会了自己思想的力量，他就变得积极而难以制服。事实上，我无法控制任何一个发现并运用确定性原则的人。

Q Is the habit of definiteness a permanent protection against your control?

明确性的习惯是否是对你的控制的永久保护？

A No, not by any means. Definiteness closes the door of one’s mind to me only as long as that person follows the principle as a matter of policy. Once any person hesitates, procrastinates, or becomes indefinite about anything, he is just one step removed from my control.

A 不，绝对不行。只有当一个人在政策上遵循原则时，明确性才会对我关上心灵的大门。一旦有人犹豫不决，拖拖拉拉，或者对任何事情变得含糊不清，他就离我的控制只有一步之遥。

Says the Devil: “Once any person hesitates, procrastinates, or becomes indefinite about anything, he is just one step removed from my control.”

魔鬼说: “一旦任何人犹豫，拖延，或变得不确定的东西，他只是一个步骤从我的控制。”

The metaphysical and spiritual aspects of the author’s philosophy are on display in these responses by the Devil. What he calls “definiteness” is today often called “intention” or being “goal-driven” or “purpose-driven.”

作者哲学的形而上学和精神层面都在魔鬼的这些回应中得到了展示。他所谓的“明确性”在今天通常被称为“意图”或“目标驱动”或“目的驱动”

Q What has definiteness to do with one’s material circumstances? I want to know if one may acquire power through definiteness of purpose without inviting destruction through the law of compensation.

明确性与一个人的物质环境有什么关系？我想知道一个人是否可以通过明确的目的而获得权力，而不必通过补偿法则招致毁灭。

A Your question limits my illustrations because there are so few people in the world who understand, and there have been so few in the past who understood, how to use definiteness of purpose without attracting to themselves the negative application of the law of compensation.

你的问题限制了我的例证，因为世界上很少有人能够理解，过去也很少有人能够理解，如何使用明确的目标，而不会引起补偿法则的负面应用。

Here you are forcing me to disclose one of my most prized tricks. I am bound to tell you that I eventually reclaim for my cause all who escape me temporarily through definiteness of purpose. The reclamation is made by filling the mind with greed for power and the love of egotistical expression, until the individual falls into the habit of violating the rights of others. Then I step in with the law of compensation and reclaim my victim.

在这里你强迫我说出我最珍贵的把戏之一。我必须告诉你们，我最终会为我的事业收回所有那些因为明确的目标而暂时逃离我的人。这种改造是通过对权力的贪婪和对自我表达的热爱来填充头脑，直到个人陷入侵犯他人权利的习惯。然后，我按照赔偿法则介入，收回我的受害者。

Q So I see from your admission that definiteness of purpose may be dangerous in proportion to its possibility as a power. Is that true?

问: 所以我从你的承认中看到，明确的目标可能是危险的，与它作为一种力量的可能性成比例。是真的吗？

A Yes, and what is more important, every principle of good carries with it the seed of an equivalent danger.

A 是的，而且更重要的是，每一条善良的原则都伴随着同样危险的种子。

Q That is hard to believe. What danger, for example, can there be in the habit of love of truth?

这很难相信。例如，热爱真理的习惯会有什么危险呢？

A The danger lies in the word “habit.” All habits, save only that of the love of definiteness of purpose, may lead to the habit of drifting. Love for truth, unless it assumes the proportion of definite pursuit of truth, may become similar to all other good intentions. You know, of course, what I do with good intentions.

A 危险在于“习惯”这个词所有的习惯，除了那些热爱明确目标的习惯，都可能导致漂泊不定的习惯。对真理的爱，除非它假定对真理的明确追求的比例，否则可能变得类似于所有其他善意。当然，你知道我是出于好意才这么做的。

“All habits, save only that of the love of definiteness of purpose, may lead to the habit of drifting.”

“所有的习惯，除了热爱目标的明确性，都可能导致漂泊的习惯。”

Q Is love for one’s relatives also dangerous?

对亲人的爱也是危险的吗？

A The love for anything or anyone, save only the love of definiteness of purpose, may become dangerous. Love is a state of mind which beclouds reason, saps will power, and blinds one to facts and truth.

对任何事或任何人的爱，除了对明确目标的爱，可能会变得危险。爱是一种精神状态，它使理智蒙蔽，削弱意志力，使人看不见事实和真理。

Everyone who becomes self-determining and gains spiritual freedom to think his own thoughts must examine carefully every emotion that seems even remotely related to love.

每一个变得自我决定和获得精神自由来思考自己的想法的人都必须仔细检查每一种似乎与爱有一点点关系的情感。

You may be surprised to know that love is one of my most effective baits. With it I lead into the habit of drifting those whom I could attract with nothing else.

你可能会惊讶地发现，爱情是我最有效的诱饵之一。有了它，我就养成了一种习惯，就是对那些我无法用别的东西去吸引的人随波逐流。

That is why I have placed it at the head of my list of bribes. Show me what any person loves most and I will have my cue as to how that person can be induced to drift until I bind him with hypnotic rhythm.

这就是为什么我把它放在贿赂清单的首位。告诉我一个人最喜欢的是什么，我就能知道这个人是如何被诱导漂移的，直到我用催眠的节奏把他捆绑起来。

Love and fear, combined, give me the most effective weapons with which I induce people to drift. One is as helpful to me as the other. Both have the effect of causing people to neglect to develop definiteness in the use of their own minds. Give me control over a person’s fears and tell me what he loves most and you may as well mark that person down as my slave. Both love and fear are emotional forces of such stupendous potency that either may completely set aside the power of will and the power of reason. Without will and reason there is nothing left to support definiteness of purpose.

爱和恐惧结合在一起，给了我最有效的武器，我用这些武器引导人们随波逐流。其中一个对我和另一个一样有帮助。两者都会导致人们在使用自己的思想时忽略发展明确性。让我控制一个人的恐惧，告诉我他最喜欢什么，你也可以把那个人当成我的奴隶。爱和恐惧都是如此巨大力量的情感力量，任何一方都可能完全放弃意志的力量和理性的力量。没有意志和理性，就没有什么能够支持明确的目标。

Q But, Your Majesty, life would not be worth living if people never felt the emotion of love.

但是，陛下，如果人们没有感受到爱的情感，生命就不值得活下去。

A Ah! You are right as far as your reasoning goes, but you neglected to add that love should be under one’s definite control at all times.

A 啊！你的推理是正确的，但是你忘了说爱情应该在任何时候都受到一个人的明确控制。

Of course, love is a desirable state of mind, but it also is a palliative which may be used to limit or destroy reason and will power, both of which rate above love in importance to human beings who want freedom and self-determination.

当然，爱是一种可取的精神状态，但它也是一种缓和剂，可能被用来限制或摧毁理性和意志力，这两者对于想要自由和自决的人来说都比爱重要。

Q I understand from what you say that people who gain power must harden their emotions, master fear, and subdue love. Is that correct?

问: 我从你的话中了解到，获得权力的人必须强化他们的情感，控制恐惧，征服爱。是这样吗？

A People who gain and maintain power must become definite in all their thoughts and all their deeds. If that is what you call hard, then they must become hard.

一个获得并保持权力的民族，必须在他们的一切思想和行为上变得明确。如果这就是你所说的艰难，那么它们必须变得艰难。

Q Let us look into the sources of advantage of definiteness in the everyday affairs of life. Which is more apt to succeed, a weak plan applied with definiteness, or a sound strong plan indefinitely applied?

问: 让我们来看看明确性在日常生活中的优势来源。哪一个更容易成功，一个明确应用的弱计划，还是一个可靠的强计划无限期应用？

A Weak plans have a way of becoming strong if definitely applied.

如果一定要实施的话，一个薄弱的计划会变得强大。

Q You mean that any plan definitely put into continuous action in pursuit of a definite purpose may be successful even if it is not the best plan?

你的意思是，为了追求一个明确的目标，任何明确地付诸于持续行动的计划即使不是最好的计划，也可能是成功的？

A Yes, I mean just that. Definiteness of purpose plus definiteness of plan by which the purpose is to be achieved generally succeeds, no matter how weak the plan may be. The major difference between a sound and an unsound plan is that the sound plan, if definitely applied, may be carried out more quickly than an unsound plan.

A 是的，我就是这个意思。目标的明确性加上计划的明确性，目标的实现一般来说是成功的，不管计划可能多么薄弱。一个合理的计划和一个不合理的计划的主要区别在于，一个合理的计划，如果一定要执行，可能比一个不合理的计划执行得更快。

Q In other words, if one cannot be always right one can and should be always definite? Is that what you are trying to get across to me?

换句话说，如果一个人不能总是正确的，那么他能够也应该总是明确的吗？这就是你想让我明白的吗？

A That is the idea. People who are definite in both their plans and their purposes never accept temporary defeat as being more than an urge to greater effort. You can see for yourself that this sort of policy is bound to win if it is followed with definiteness.

A 这就是我的想法。那些既有明确的计划又有明确的目标的人从来不认为暂时的失败只是一种更大努力的冲动。你可以亲眼看到，如果有明确的遵循，这种政策一定会取得成功。

Q Can a person who moves with definiteness of both plan and purpose be always sure of success?

一个既有计划又有目标的人是否总能确保成功？

A No. The best of plans sometimes misfire, but the person who moves with definiteness recognizes the difference between temporary defeat and failure. When plans fail he substitutes others but he does not change his purpose. He perseveres. Eventually he finds a plan that succeeds.

A 没有。最好的计划有时会失败，但是明确行动的人会认识到暂时的失败和失败之间的区别。当计划失败时，他替换其他人，但他不改变自己的目标。他坚持着。最终他找到了一个成功的计划。

“The person who moves with definiteness recognizes the difference between temporary defeat and failure. When plans fail he substitutes others but he does not change his purpose. He perseveres.”

“明确行动的人认识到暂时失败和失败的区别。当计划失败时，他替换其他人，但他不改变自己的目标。他坚持不懈。”

Q Will a plan based upon immoral or unjust ends succeed as quickly as one motivated by a keen sense of justice and morality?

问: 一个基于不道德或不公正目标的计划能否像一个基于强烈的正义感和道德感的计划那样迅速取得成功？

A Through the operation of the law of compensation, everyone reaps that which he sows. Plans based on unjust or immoral motives may bring temporary success, but enduring success must take into consideration the fourth dimension, time.

通过补偿法的运作，每个人都收获了他播种的东西。基于不公正或不道德动机的计划可能会带来暂时的成功，但持久的成功必须考虑到第四个维度---- 时间。

Time is the enemy of immorality and injustice. It is the friend of justice and morality. Failure to recognize this fact has been responsible for the crime wave among the youths of the world.

时间是不道德和不公正的敌人。它是正义和道德的朋友。未能认识到这一事实是造成世界青少年犯罪浪潮的原因。

The youthful, inexperienced mind is apt to mistake temporary success for permanency. The youth often makes the mistake of coveting the temporary gains of immoral, unjust plans, but neglects to look ahead and observe the penalties which follow as definitely as night follows day.

年轻，没有经验的头脑容易把暂时的成功误认为是永久的。年轻人经常犯下这样的错误: 贪图不道德、不公正计划的暂时收益，却忽视了向前看和遵守随之而来的惩罚。





Chapter Nine

EDUCATION AND RELIGION

第九章教育与宗教

Q THIS IS PRETTY DEEP STUFF, Your Majesty. Let us get back to the discussion of lighter and more concrete subjects that are likely to interest the majority of people. I am interested in discussing the things that make people happy and miserable, rich and poor, sick and healthy. In brief, I am interested in everything that can be used by human beings to make life pay satisfactory dividends in return for the effort that one puts into the business of living.

问: 这是很深奥的东西，陛下。让我们回到可能引起大多数人兴趣的较轻松和较具体的议题上来。我感兴趣的是讨论那些使人们快乐和悲惨，富有和贫穷，疾病和健康的事情。简而言之，我对人类可以利用的一切事物感兴趣，这些事物可以使生活付出令人满意的回报，以换取人们为生活所付出的努力。

A Very well, let us be definite.

A 好吧，让我们明确一点。

Q You have my idea. Your Majesty has a tendency to stray off into abstract details which most people can neither understand nor use in the solution of their problems. Could that, by any chance, be a definite plan of yours to answer my questions with indefinite answers? If that is your plan, it is a slick trick but it will not work. Go ahead now and tell me something more of the miseries and failures of human beings growing directly out of indefiniteness.

问: 你知道我的想法。陛下有一种偏离主题的倾向，总是谈到一些大多数人既不能理解也不能用来解决问题的抽象的细节。这是否可能是你用不确定的答案回答我的问题的明确计划？如果这就是你的计划，这是一个狡猾的伎俩，但不会奏效。现在继续，告诉我更多的痛苦和失败的人类直接成长的不确定性。

A Why not permit me to tell you more of the pleasures and successes of people who understand and apply the principle of definiteness?

A 为什么不允许我告诉你更多那些理解并应用明确性原则的人的快乐和成功呢？

Q I observe that sometimes people with definiteness of plan and purpose get what they ask from life only to find after they get it that they do not want it. What then?

问: 我观察到，有时候有明确计划和目标的人从生活中得到他们想要的东西，但是当他们得到之后却发现他们不想要了。然后呢？

A Generally one can get rid of whatever is not wanted by application of the same principle of definiteness with which the thing was acquired. A life that is lived with fullness of peace of mind, contentment, and happiness always divests itself of everything it does not want. Anyone who submits to annoyance by things he does not want is not definite. He is a drifter.

一般来说，一个人可以通过运用确定性原则来摆脱任何不想要的东西，这个原则就是用来获得某件东西的。一个充满了平静、满足和幸福的生活总是会把它不需要的一切都抛在脑后。任何人因为不想要的东西而屈服于烦恼是不确定的。他是个流浪汉。

“A life that is lived with fullness of peace of mind, contentment, and happiness always divests itself of everything it does not want.”

“一个充满安宁、满足和幸福的生活总是会把它不需要的一切都抛诸脑后。”

How many of us are truly content? In a world where so many people are trying to “keep up with the Joneses,” could we not all learn something here? Is there something in your life that you need to divest yourself of? Make a commitment to catch yourself when you are feeling annoyed . . . and remember the Devil’s words, “Anyone who submits to annoyance by things he does not want is not definite. He is a drifter.”

我们中有多少人是真正满足的？在一个有那么多人试图“攀比”的世界里，难道我们不能在这里学到一些东西吗？你的生活中是否有什么东西需要你舍弃？当你感到烦恼的时候，承诺抓住你自己... 并且记住魔鬼的话: “任何人因为他不想要的东西而屈服于烦恼是不确定的。他是个流浪汉。”

Q What about married people who cease to want each other? Should they separate, or is it true that all marriages are made in heaven and the contracting parties are, therefore, forever bound by their bargain, even though it may prove to be a poor one for both.

问: 已婚的人不再想要对方了，这又怎么样呢？他们是否应该分开，或者所有的婚姻都是天作之合，因此，缔约双方永远受制于他们之间的协议，即使这对双方来说都可能是一个糟糕的协议。

A First, let me correct that old saying that all marriages are made in heaven. I know of some which were made on my side of the fence. Minds which do not harmonize should never be forced to remain together in marriage or any other relationship. Friction and all forms of discord between minds lead inevitably to the habit of drifting, and of course to indefiniteness.

首先，让我纠正一下那句老话，所有的婚姻都是天作之合。我知道有些是在我这边的篱笆上做的。不和谐的心灵永远不应该被迫在婚姻或任何其他关系中继续在一起。思想之间的摩擦和各种形式的不和谐不可避免地导致漂泊的习惯，当然也导致不确定性。

Q Aren’t people sometimes bound to others by a relationship of duty which renders it impractical for them to take from life what they want most?

难道人们不是因为一种责任关系而与他人结合在一起，从生活中拿走他们最想要的东西是不切实际的吗？

A “Duty” is one of the most abused and misunderstood words in existence. The first duty of every human being is to himself. Every person owes himself the duty of finding how to live a full and happy life. Beyond this, if one has time and energy not needed in the fulfillment of his own desires, one may assume responsibility for helping others.

“责任”是现存最常被滥用和误解的词汇之一。每个人的首要职责是对自己负责。每个人都有责任去寻找如何过上充实而幸福的生活。除此之外，如果一个人有时间和精力去满足他自己的欲望，他可能会承担起帮助他人的责任。

“The first duty of every human being is to himself. Every person owes himself the duty of finding how to live a full and happy life.”

“每个人的首要职责是对自己负责。每个人都有责任寻找如何过上充实而幸福的生活。”

Of course, though compelled to answer accurately, the Devil still responds from the perspective of the Devil. Is it possible that Mother Teresa or Gandhi had a very different opinion on this issue? They lived their lives in service of others. How do you feel? Do you put finding a full and happy life first in your life? Do you agree with those who would argue that to truly be of service to others you need to take care of yourself first? Is it then possible that Mother Teresa and Gandhi found their full and happy lives—through service to others?

当然，虽然被迫准确地回答，魔鬼仍然从魔鬼的角度作出回应。有没有可能特蕾莎修女和甘地在这个问题上有着截然不同的观点？他们一生都在为他人服务。你感觉怎么样？你是否把寻找一个充实而幸福的生活放在生活的第一位？你是否同意那些认为要真正为他人服务，你首先需要照顾好自己的人的观点？那么特蕾莎修女和甘地是否有可能通过服务他人而找到他们充实而幸福的生活呢？

Q Isn’t that a selfish attitude, and isn’t selfishness one of the causes of failure to find happiness?

这难道不是一种自私的态度吗? 难道自私不是找不到幸福的原因之一吗？

A I stand by my statement that there is no higher duty than that which one owes himself.

A 我坚持我的声明，没有比一个人对自己的责任更高的义务了。

Q Doesn’t a child owe something in the way of duty to its parents who gave it life and sustenance during its periods of helplessness?

在孩子无助的时候，父母给了他们生命和食物，难道孩子不应该对父母负责吗？

A Not at all. It is just the other way around. Parents owe their children everything they can give them in the way of knowledge. Beyond that, parents often spoil instead of helping their offspring by a false sense of duty which prompts them to indulge their children instead of forcing them to seek and gain knowledge at first hand.

A 一点也不。恰恰相反。父母应该用知识的方式给予孩子一切。除此之外，父母经常惯坏孩子而不是帮助他们的错误责任感，促使他们纵容他们的孩子，而不是迫使他们寻求和获得第一手的知识。

Q I see what you mean. Your theory is that too much help thrust upon the youth encourages him to drift and become indefinite in all things. You believe that necessity is a teacher of great sagacity, that defeat carries with it an equivalent virtue, that unearned gifts of every nature may become a curse instead of a blessing. Is that correct?

我明白你的意思了。你的理论是，太多的帮助强加在年轻人身上，会使他们在一切事情上游离不定。你相信需求是伟大睿智的导师，失败带来了同等的美德，不劳而获的天赋可能成为诅咒而不是祝福。是这样吗？

Hill notes, “Unearned gifts of every nature may become a curse instead of a blessing.” In our effort to give to our children, are we really cursing them? A very sobering thought, but also great advice, for parents.

希尔指出，“不劳而获的礼物可能成为诅咒而不是祝福。”在我们努力给予孩子的过程中，我们真的在诅咒他们吗？对父母来说，这是一个发人深省的想法，同时也是一个很好的建议。

A You have stated my philosophy perfectly. My belief is not theory. It is fact.

A 你完美地阐述了我的哲学。我的信仰不是理论，而是事实。

Q Then you do not advocate prayer as a means of gaining desirable ends?

那么你不主张祈祷是达到理想目的的一种手段吗？

A On the contrary I do advocate prayer, but not the sort of prayer that consists of empty, begging, meaningless words. The sort of prayer against which I am helpless is the prayer of definiteness of purpose.

相反，我确实提倡祈祷，但不是那种由空洞的、乞求的、毫无意义的话语组成的祈祷。我无能为力的那种祈祷，就是明确目标的祈祷。

Q I never thought of definiteness of purpose as being a prayer. How can it be?

我从来没有想过明确目标是一种祈祷，怎么可能呢？

A Definiteness is in effect the only sort of prayer upon which one can rely. It places one in the way of using hypnotic rhythm to attain definite ends . . . by the mere act of appropriating it from the great universal storehouse of Infinite Intelligence. The appropriation, in case you are interested, takes place through definiteness of purpose, persistently pursued!

明确的祷告实际上是人们唯一可以依靠的祷告。它将人置于催眠的节奏中，以达到确定的目的... ... 仅仅通过从无限智慧的巨大宇宙宝库中占有它的行为。如果你感兴趣的话，这种挪用是通过明确目标和坚持不懈的追求而发生的！

Q Why do the majority of prayers fail?

问: 为什么大多数的祷告都失败了？

A They don’t. All prayers bring that for which one prays.

A 他们没有. 所有的祈祷者都带来了他们祈祷的东西。

Q But you just said that definiteness of purpose is the only sort of prayer upon which one can rely. Now you say that all prayers bring results. What do you mean?

但是你刚才说明确的目标是唯一可以信赖的祈祷。现在你说所有的祈祷都会带来结果。什么意思？

A There is nothing inconsistent about it. The majority of people who pray go to prayer only after everything else fails them. Naturally they go with their minds filled with fear that the prayers will not be answered. Well, their fears are realized.

A 这没有什么不一致的地方。大多数祈祷的人只有在其他事情都让他们失望之后才会去祈祷。很自然地，他们心里充满了恐惧，担心祷告得不到回应。他们的恐惧终于实现了。

The person who goes to prayer with definiteness of purpose and faith in the attainment of that purpose puts into motion the laws of nature which transmute one’s dominating desires into their physical equivalent. That is all there is to prayer.

一个人带着明确的目的和达到这个目的的信念去祈祷，就会把把一个人支配的欲望转化为他们的物理等价物的自然法则付诸行动。这就是祈祷的全部内容。

One form of prayer is negative and brings only negative results. One form is positive and brings definite, positive results. Could anything be more simple?

有一种祈祷方式是消极的，只会带来消极的结果。一种形式是积极的，并带来明确的，积极的结果。还有比这更简单的吗？

People who whine and beg God to assume responsibility for all their troubles and provide them with all the necessities and luxuries of life are too lazy to create what they want and translate it into existence through the power of their own minds.

那些抱怨并乞求上帝为他们所有的困难承担责任，为他们提供生活必需品和奢侈品的人太懒了，他们不愿意创造他们想要的东西，也不愿意通过他们自己的思想力量将其转化为存在。

When you hear a person praying for something that he should procure through his own efforts, you may be sure you are listening to a drifter. Infinite Intelligence favors only those who understand and adapt themselves to her laws. She makes no discrimination because of fine character or pleasing personality. These things help people negotiate their way through life more harmoniously with one another, but the source from which prayer is answered is not impressed by fine feathers. Nature’s law is, “Know what you want, adapt yourself to my laws, and you shall have it.”

当你听到一个人在为他应该通过自己的努力得到的东西祈祷时，你可能会确信你正在听一个流浪汉的祈祷。无限智慧只青睐那些理解并适应她的法则的人。她没有因为良好的品格或讨人喜欢的性格而受到歧视。这些事情帮助人们在生活中更和谐地相处，但是祈祷得到回应的源泉并不是美丽的羽毛。大自然的法则是，“知道你想要什么，让你自己适应我的法则，你就会得到它。”

The preceding question and answer push the boundaries of Hill’s critique of organized religion versus personal spirituality and responsibility.

前面的问题和答案推动了希尔对有组织的宗教与个人精神和责任的批判的界限。

Q Does that harmonize with the teachings of Christ?

问: 这是否与基督的教导相一致？

A Perfectly. Also it harmonizes with the teachings of all truly great philosophers.

一个完美的。而且它与所有真正伟大的哲学家的教义相协调。

Q Is your theory of definiteness in harmony with the philosophy of men of science?

问: 你的确定性理论是否与科学哲学相一致？

A Definiteness is the major difference between a scientist and a drifter. Through the principle of definiteness of purpose and plan, the scientist forces nature to hand over her most profound secrets. It was through this principle that Edison uncovered the secret of the talking machine, the incandescent electric light, and scores of other benefits for mankind.

明确性是科学家和漂泊者的主要区别。通过明确目标和计划的原则，科学家迫使自然交出她最深奥的秘密。正是通过这个原理，爱迪生发现了会说话的机器的秘密，白炽电灯，以及其他许多对人类有益的东西。

Q Then I understand that definiteness is the first requisite for success in all earthly undertakings? Is that right?

问: 那么我明白了，明确是人世间所有事业成功的首要条件，对吗？

A Exactly! Anything which teaches people to examine facts and coordinate them into definite plans through accurate thinking is hard on my profession. If this thirst for definite knowledge now spreading over the world keeps up, my business will be shot to pieces within the next few centuries. I thrive on ignorance, superstition, intolerance, and fear, but I cannot stand up under definite knowledge properly organized into definite plans in the minds of people who think for themselves.

A 完全正确！任何教导人们通过准确的思考来审视事实并协调它们成为明确的计划的事情，对我的职业来说都是困难的。如果现在世界各地对确切知识的渴望继续下去，我的事业在未来几个世纪内就会支离破碎。我以无知、迷信、偏狭和恐惧为乐，但是我无法站起来，在那些独立思考的人的头脑中，把明确的知识恰当地组织成明确的计划。

Q Why don’t you take over Omnipotence and manage the whole works in your own way?

问: 你为什么不接管全能，用你自己的方式管理整个工作？

A You might as well ask why the negative portion of the electron doesn’t take over the positive portion and run the entire works. The answer is that both the positive and the negative charges of energy are necessary to the existence of the electron. One is balanced equally against the other, stalemated, as it were.

你可能会问，为什么电子的负部分不接管正部分，而是运行整个过程。答案是，能量的正电荷和负电荷对于电子的存在都是必要的。一方与另一方之间的平衡陷入了僵局。

So it is with what you call Omnipotence and I. We represent the positive and the negative forces of the entire system of universes, and we are equally balanced one against the other.

你们所谓的全能和我也是如此。我们代表着整个宇宙系统的积极力量和消极力量，我们平等地平衡着这两种力量。

If this power of balance were shifted the slightest degree, the whole system of universes would become quickly reduced to a mass of inert matter. Now you know why I cannot take over the whole show and run it my way.

如果这种平衡的力量稍有改变，整个宇宙系统就会迅速减少为一团惰性物质。现在你知道为什么我不能接管整个演出并按照我的方式进行了。

Q If what you say is true, you have exactly the same power as Omnipotence. Is that true?

问: 如果你说的是真的，你就拥有和全能者一样的力量，是这样吗？

A That is correct. My opposition—you call it Omnipotence— expresses itself through the forces which you call good, the positive forces of nature. I express myself through the forces you call bad, the negative forces. Both good and bad are coincidental with existence. One is as important as the other.

A 是的。我的反对者——你们称之为全能者——通过你们称之为善的力量——自然界的积极力量来表达自己。我通过你们所谓的坏的力量，消极的力量来表达我自己。好与坏都是与存在相一致的。一个和另一个一样重要。

Q Then the doctrine of predestination is sound. People are born to success or failure, misery or happiness, to be good or bad, and they have nothing to do with this nor can they modify their natures. Is that your claim?

那么宿命论是合理的。人生来就有成功或失败，痛苦或幸福，好或坏，他们与此无关，也无法改变他们的本性。这是你的要求吗？

A Emphatically not! Every human being has a wide range of choice in both his thoughts and his deeds. Every human being can use his brain for the reception and the expression of positive thoughts or he can use it for the expression of negative thoughts. His choice in this important matter shapes his entire life.

A 绝对不行！每个人的思想和行为都有广泛的选择。每个人都可以用大脑来接受和表达积极的思想，或者用大脑来表达消极的思想。他在这个重要问题上的选择塑造了他的一生。

Q From what you have said I gather the idea that human beings have more freedom of expression than either you or your opposition. Is that correct?

问: 从你所说的话中，我可以推断出人类比你或你的反对者有更多的言论自由。是这样吗？

A That is true. Omnipotence and I are bound by immutable laws of nature. We cannot express ourselves in any manner not conforming to these laws.

A 那是真的。全能和我都受到不可改变的自然法则的约束。我们不能以任何不符合这些法律的方式表达自己。

Q Then it is true that man has rights and privileges not available to either Omnipotence or the Devil. Is that the truth?

那么人类确实拥有全能者和魔鬼所没有的权利和特权。这是真的吗？

A Yes, that is true, but you might well have added that man has not yet fully awakened to the realization of this potential power. Man still regards himself as something resembling the worms in the dust, when in reality he has more power than all other living things combined.

答: 是的，这是事实，但是你可以补充说，人类还没有完全意识到这种潜在力量的实现。人类仍然把自己看作是尘埃中的蠕虫，而实际上他拥有的力量比所有其他生物加起来还要大。

Q Definiteness of purpose seems to be a panacea for all evils of man.

明确目标似乎是治疗人类所有罪恶的灵丹妙药。

A Not that perhaps, but you may be sure no one ever will become self-determining without it.

A 也许不是这样，但是你可以肯定，没有它，没有人会变得自主。

Q Why aren’t children taught definiteness of purpose in the public schools?

问: 为什么公立学校没有教孩子明确目标？

A For the reason that there is no definite plan or purpose behind any of the school curricula! Children are sent to school to make credits and to learn how to memorize, not to learn what they want of life.

因为学校课程背后没有明确的计划或目的！孩子们被送到学校是为了获得学分和学习如何记忆，而不是学习他们想要的生活。

Says the Devil: “Children are sent to school to make credits and to learn how to memorize, not to learn what they want of life.”

魔鬼说: “孩子们被送到学校是为了获得学分和学习如何记忆，而不是学习他们想要的生活。”

Again, I find this chilling. Hill sounded this alarm in 1938 and yet the manuscript went unpublished and today we are still “teaching to the test” in our schools. I am on a mission to promote financial education to teach young people about money, a true life skill, and yet many schools still reject it because it does not satisfy the “test requirements” upon which they are graded and receive funding. Is it not time to sound the alarms again?

再一次，我发现这令人不寒而栗。希尔在1938年敲响了这个警钟，然而手稿还没有出版，直到今天我们仍然在学校里“应试教育”。我的使命是促进金融教育，向年轻人传授金钱这一真正的生活技能。然而，许多学校仍然拒绝接受金钱教育，因为它不能满足他们评分和获得资金的“考试要求”。现在不是再次拉响警报的时候吗？

Q What good is a school credit if one cannot convert it into the material and spiritual needs of life?

如果学分不能转化为生活的物质和精神需要，那它还有什么用呢？

A I am only a Devil, not an un-winder of riddles!

A 我只是一个魔鬼，不是一个谜团的解开者！

Q I deduce from all you say that neither the schools nor the churches prepare the youths of the world with a practical working knowledge of their own minds. Is anything of more importance to a human being than an understanding of the forces and circumstances which influence his own mind?

问: 我从你们所说的一切推断，学校和教会都没有使世界上的青年人具备他们自己心灵的实际工作知识。对于一个人来说，还有什么比了解影响他自己心智的力量和环境更重要的吗？

A The only thing of enduring value to any human being is a working knowledge of his own mind. The churches do not permit a person to inquire into the possibilities of his own mind, and the schools do not recognize that such a thing as a mind exists.

对于任何人来说，唯一具有持久价值的东西就是他自己头脑中的工作知识。教会不允许一个人探究自己思想的可能性，学校也不承认有思想这样的东西存在。

Why is Napoleon Hill so down on churches and the prevailing organized religions of his day? I believe his criticism stems from an abiding love for the true spirit and meaning of faith and the underlying validity of all religious traditions— despite what human beings do to weaken or corrupt them. What is the balance between accepting that which is revealed to your mind and heart—your soul—and the reality of life in a world so often infected with evil, as personified by Hill’s Devil?

为什么拿破仑 · 希尔对他那个时代的教堂和盛行的有组织的宗教如此失望？我相信他的批评源于对信仰的真正精神和意义的持久热爱，以及所有宗教传统的潜在有效性ーー尽管人类做了削弱或腐化他们的事情。在接受你的头脑和心灵ーー你的灵魂ーー所显示的东西和生活在一个经常充满邪恶的世界中的现实之间的平衡是什么，就像希尔的魔鬼拟人化的那样？

Q Aren’t you a little hard on the schools and the churches?

问: 你是不是对学校和教堂太苛刻了？

A No, I am merely describing them as they are, without bias or prejudice.

答: 不，我只是把它们描述成它们的本来面目，没有偏见或偏见。

Q Aren’t the schools and the churches your bitter enemies?

难道学校和教堂不是你们的死敌吗？

A Their leaders may think they are, but I am impressed only by facts. The truth is this, if you must know it: the churches are my most helpful allies and the schools run the churches a close second.

A 他们的领导人可能认为他们是，但我只对事实印象深刻。事实是这样的，如果你一定要知道的话: 教会是我最有帮助的盟友，学校紧随其后经营教会。

Q On what specific or general grounds do you make this claim?

问: 基于什么具体或一般的理由，你提出这一要求？

A On the grounds that both the churches and the schools help me to convert people to the habit of drifting.

A 理由是教堂和学校都帮助我使人们改变漂泊的习惯。

Q Do you realize that your charge is substantially a sweeping indictment of the two institutions of major importance which have been responsible for civilization, in its present form?

问: 你是否意识到你的指控实质上是对两个重要机构的全面控诉，这两个机构以目前的形式对文明负有责任？

A Do I realize it? Man alive, I gloat over it. If the schools and churches had taught people how to think for themselves, where would I be, now?

A 我意识到了吗？我幸灾乐祸地看着它。如果学校和教堂教会人们如何独立思考，我现在会在哪里？

Q This confession of yours will disillusion millions of people whose only hope for salvation is in their churches. Isn’t that a cruel thing to do to them? Wouldn’t most people be better off living in the bliss of ignorance than to know the truth about you?

问: 你的这个忏悔会使数以百万计的人破灭幻想，他们唯一的救赎希望就是在他们的教会里。这样对他们不是很残忍吗？难道大多数人生活在无知的幸福中不比了解你的真相更好吗？

A What do you mean by the term “salvation”? From what are people being saved? The only form of enduring salvation that is worth a green fig to any human being is that which comes from recognition of the power of his own mind. Ignorance and fear are the only enemies from which men need salvation.

A 你所说的“救赎”是什么意思？人们从什么中被拯救？对于任何人来说，唯一值得持久拯救的形式就是承认自己心灵的力量。无知和恐惧是人类唯一需要拯救的敌人。

Q You seem to hold nothing sacred.

问: 你似乎没有什么是神圣的。

A You are wrong. I hold sacred the one thing which is my master—the one thing I fear.

A 你错了。我认为我的主人——我唯一害怕的东西——是神圣的。

Q What is that?

问: 那是什么？

A The power of independent thought backed by definiteness of purpose.

有明确目标支持的独立思考的力量。

Q Then you do not have many people to fear?

问: 那么你不怕很多人吗？

A Only two out of every 100 to be exact. I control all others.

确切地说，每100个人中只有2个人是这样，其他人都是我控制的。

Q Let’s give the churches a rest and get back to the public schools. Your confession has shown clearly that you thrive and perpetuate yourself from one generation to another by the clever trick of taking over the minds of children before they have the chance to learn how to use their minds.

让我们让教会休息一下，然后回到公立学校。你的坦白清楚地表明，在孩子们有机会学会如何使用他们的思想之前，你就已经通过一种巧妙的方法控制了他们的思想，从而使自己一代又一代地茁壮成长。

I wish to know what is wrong with a public school system that permits the Devil to control so many people. I wish to know, also, what can be done to the established system of teaching that will insure all children the opportunity to learn, first, that they have minds, and second, how to use those minds to bring spiritual and economic freedom.

我想知道一个允许魔鬼控制这么多人的公立学校系统出了什么问题。我还想知道，对于确保所有儿童都有机会学习的既定教学体系，我们能够做些什么，首先，他们有头脑，其次，如何利用这些头脑带来精神和经济自由。

I am putting the question to you definitely enough, and since you have stressed the importance of definiteness of purpose I am here and now putting you on notice that your answer to my question must be definite.

既然你已经强调了明确目标的重要性，我现在就在这里提醒你，你对我的问题的答案必须是明确的。

A Wait a moment while I catch my breath. You have given me quite an order! It seems strange that you would come to the Devil to learn how to live. I should think you would go to my opposition. Why don’t you?

A 等一下，让我喘口气。你给了我一个很大的命令！你来魔鬼那里学习如何生活，这似乎很奇怪。我想你会站在我这边的。为什么不呢？

Q Your Majesty, it is you who are on trial here, not I. I want the truth and I am not particular as to the source from which I get it. There is something radically wrong with the system of education that has given us a balance sheet with life that shows us hopelessly in the red and groping for the road to self-determination as if we were so many animals lost in the jungle.

问: 陛下，在这里接受审判的是您，而不是我。我想知道真相，而且我并不特别关心我从哪里得到的真相。教育系统的某些根本性的错误给了我们一张生活的资产负债表，让我们绝望地赤身裸体，摸索着通往自决的道路，仿佛我们是丛林中迷失的许多动物。

I want to know two things about this system. First, what is the major weakness of the system? Second, how can this weakness be eliminated? The floor is yours again! Please stick to the question and stop trying to decoy me into the discussion of deep, abstract subjects. That’s definite, is it not?

我想知道关于这个系统的两件事。首先，这个体系的主要弱点是什么？第二，如何消除这一弱点？地板又是你的了！请专注于这个问题，不要试图把我引诱到深奥的、抽象的主题讨论中去。这是肯定的，不是吗？

A You leave me no choice but that of direct answer. To begin with, the public school system approaches the subject of education from the wrong angle. The school system endeavors to teach children to memorize facts, instead of teaching them how to use their own minds.

A 你让我别无选择，只能直接回答。首先，公立学校制度对教育主体的认识是错误的。学校系统努力教孩子们记忆事实，而不是教他们如何使用自己的头脑。

Q Is that all that is wrong with the system?

问: 这就是整个系统的问题所在吗？

A No, that is only the beginning. Another major weakness of the school system is that it does not establish in the minds of children either the importance of definiteness of purpose or make any attempt to teach youths how to be definite about anything.

A 不，那只是个开始。学校系统的另一个主要弱点是，它既没有在孩子们的头脑中树立明确目标的重要性，也没有试图教导年轻人如何对任何事情做到明确。

The major object of all schooling is to force the students to cram their memories with facts instead of teaching them how to organize and make practical use of facts.

所有学校教育的主要目的是迫使学生用事实填充记忆，而不是教他们如何组织和实际应用事实。

This cramming system centers the attention of students on the accumulation of “credits” but overlooks the important question of how to use knowledge in the practical affairs of life. This system turns out graduates whose names are inscribed upon parchment certificates, but whose minds are empty of self-determination. The school system got off to a bad start at the beginning. The schools began as institutions of “higher learning,” operated entirely for the select few whose wealth and family entitled them to education.

这种填鸭式的教学模式把学生的注意力集中在“学分”的积累上，而忽视了在实际生活中如何运用知识这一重要问题。这个系统的结果是，毕业生的名字被写在羊皮纸证书上，但他们的脑子里却没有自决。学校系统一开始就不顺利。这些学校最初是作为“高等教育”的机构，完全为少数几个有财富和家庭资格接受教育的人运作。

Thus the entire school system was evolved by beginning at the top and working back down to the bottom. It is no wonder the system neglects to teach children the importance of definiteness of purpose when the system, itself, has literally evolved through indefiniteness.

因此，整个学校系统是从上到下逐步发展起来的。难怪这个系统忽视教育孩子明确目标的重要性，而这个系统本身就是通过不确定性逐步发展起来的。

Q What would correct this weakness of the public school system? Let’s not complain of the weakness of the system unless we are prepared to offer a practical remedy with which it can be corrected. In other words, while we are discussing the importance of definiteness of plan and purpose, let us take our own medicine and be definite.

问: 怎样才能纠正公立学校系统的这一弱点？我们不要抱怨这个制度的弱点，除非我们准备提供一个可以纠正它的实际补救办法。换句话说，当我们在讨论明确计划和目标的重要性时，让我们以我们自己的方式来明确。

A Why don’t you lay off the schools and churches and save yourself plenty of trouble? Don’t you know that you are poking your nose into the affairs of the two forces that control the world? Suppose you do show up the schools and the churches as being weak and inadequate for the needs of human beings? What then? With what are you going to replace these two institutions?

A 你为什么不放弃学校和教堂，省得自己麻烦缠身呢？难道你不知道你正在插手控制世界的两股势力的事务吗？假如你确实表现出学校和教会软弱无能，不能满足人类的需要呢？然后呢？你打算用什么来取代这两个机构？

Q Stop trying to evade my questions by the old trick of asking a counter-question! I do not propose to replace the schools and churches. But I do propose to find out, if I can, how these organized forces can be modified so they will serve people instead of keeping them in ignorance. Go ahead, now, and give me a detailed catalogue of all the changes in the public school system which would improve it.

不要再试图用反问的老把戏来回避我的问题了！我并不打算取代学校和教堂。但是，如果可以的话，我确实建议找出，如何改变这些有组织的力量，使它们为人民服务，而不是让它们一无所知。来吧，现在，给我一份详细的目录，列出公立学校系统中能够改进它的所有变化。

A So you want the entire catalogue, do you? Do you want the suggested changes in the order of their importance?

A 所以你想要整个目录，是吗？您是否希望按照建议的重要性顺序进行更改？

This is another point at which the questioner forces the Devil out of his comfort zone. It is amusing and instructive to witness this exchange, which provides a roadmap for improvement of our public schools.

这是另一个提问者迫使魔鬼离开他的安乐窝的地方。见证这次交流很有趣，也很有教育意义，它为我们公立学校的改进提供了一个路线图。

Q Describe the changes needed just as they come to you.

描述需要的改变，正如他们来到你身边。

A You are forcing me to commit an act of treason against myself, but here it is:

A 你是在强迫我犯下背叛自己的罪行，但事实如此:

Reverse the present system by giving children the privilege of leading in their school work instead of following orthodox rules designed only to impart abstract knowledge. Let instructors serve as students and let the students serve as instructors.

改变目前的制度，给予儿童在学校工作中领导的特权，而不是遵循只是为了传授抽象知识而设计的正统规则。让教师充当学生，让学生充当教师。

As far as possible, organize all school work into definite methods through which the student can learn by doing, and direct the class work so that every student engages in some form of practical labor connected with the daily problems of life.

尽可能将所有的学校工作组织成一个明确的方法，通过这个方法学生可以通过实践来学习，并且指导班级工作，使每个学生从事与日常生活问题有关的某种形式的实际劳动。

Ideas are the beginning of all human achievement. Teach all students how to recognize practical ideas that may be of benefit in helping them acquire whatever they demand of life.

思想是人类所有成就的开始。教导所有的学生如何认识到实际的想法，这些想法可能有助于帮助他们获得生活中他们所需要的任何东西。

Teach the students how to budget and use time, and above all teach the truth that time is the greatest asset available to human beings and the cheapest.

教导学生如何预算和使用时间，最重要的是告诉他们时间是人类最宝贵的财富，也是最便宜的。

Teach the student the basic motives by which all people are influenced and show how to use these motives in acquiring the necessities and the luxuries of life.

教导学生影响所有人的基本动机，并指出如何使用这些动机来获得生活的必需品和奢侈品。

Teach children what to eat, how much to eat, and what is the relationship between proper eating and sound health.

教孩子吃什么，吃多少，合理的饮食和健康的关系是什么。

Teach children the true nature and function of the emotion of sex, and above all, teach them that it can be transmuted into a driving force capable of lifting one to great heights of achievement.

教导孩子性爱的真正本质和功能，最重要的是，教导他们性爱可以转化为一种驱动力，能够将一个人提升到很高的成就。

Teach children to be definite in all things, beginning with the choice of a definite major purpose in life!

教导孩子在任何事情上都要有明确的目标，从选择一个明确的人生主要目标开始！

Teach children the nature of and possibilities for good and evil in the principle of habit, using as illustrations with which to dramatize the subject the everyday experiences of children and adults.

根据习惯原则教导儿童善与恶的本质和可能性，并以此作为插图，将儿童和成人的日常经历生动地表现出来。

Teach children how habits become fixed through the law of hypnotic rhythm, and influence them to adopt, while in the lower grades, habits that will lead to independent thought!

教导孩子习惯如何通过催眠节奏的规律变得固定，并影响他们采用，而在低年级，习惯会导致独立思考！

Teach children the difference between temporary defeat and failure, and show them how to search for the seed of an equivalent advantage which comes with every defeat.

告诉孩子们暂时失败和失败的区别，告诉他们如何寻找每次失败都会带来的同等优势的种子。

Teach children to express their own thoughts fearlessly and to accept or reject, at will, all ideas of others, reserving to themselves, always, the privilege of relying upon their own judgment.

教导孩子无畏地表达自己的想法，随意地接受或拒绝别人的所有想法，永远保留自己依靠自己判断的特权。

Teach children to reach decisions promptly and to change them, if at all, slowly and with reluctance, and never without a definite reason.

教导孩子们迅速做出决定并改变它们，如果有的话，要慢慢地、勉强地做出决定，而且永远不要没有明确的原因。

Teach children that the human brain is the instrument with which one receives, from the great storehouse of nature, the energy which is specialized into definite thoughts; that the brain does not think, but serves as an instrument for the interpretation of stimuli which cause thought.

告诉孩子们，人类的大脑是一种工具，通过这种工具，人们从自然的巨大宝库中接收到专门化为明确思想的能量; 大脑不是思考，而是作为一种工具，用来解释引起思考的刺激。

Teach children the value of harmony in their own minds and that this is attainable only through self-control.

教导孩子在他们自己的头脑中和谐的价值，这只有通过自我控制才能实现。

Teach children the nature and the value of self-control.

教导孩子自我控制的本质和价值。

Teach children that there is a law of increasing returns which can be and should be put into operation, as a matter of habit, by rendering always more service and better service than is expected of them.

告诉孩子们有一条回报递增的法则，作为一种习惯，通过总是提供比预期更多的服务和更好的服务，这条法则可以而且应该付诸实施。

Teach children the true nature of the Golden Rule, and above all show them that through the operation of this principle, everything they do to and for another they do also to and for themselves.

教导孩子们黄金法则的真正本质，最重要的是告诉他们，通过这一原则的运作，他们对他人所做的每一件事都是为了自己，也是为了自己。

Teach children not to have opinions unless they are formed from facts or beliefs which may reasonably be accepted as facts. Teach children that cigarettes, liquor, narcotics, and overindulgence in sex destroy the power of will and lead to the habit of drifting. Do not forbid these evils—just explain them.

教育孩子不要有观点，除非这些观点是根据可以合理地被接受为事实的事实或信念形成的。告诉孩子们，香烟、酒精、麻醉剂和过度沉溺于性会摧毁意志的力量，并导致漂泊的习惯。不要禁止这些罪恶ーー只要解释它们就行了。

Teach children the danger of believing anything merely because their parents, religious instructors, or someone else says it is so.

告诉孩子们，仅仅因为他们的父母、宗教导师或其他人的说法，就相信任何事情是危险的。

Teach children to face facts, whether they are pleasant or unpleasant, without resorting to subterfuge or offering alibis.

教导孩子面对事实，不管它们是令人愉快的还是令人不快的，不要使用托词或提供不在场证明。

Teach children to encourage the use of their sixth sense through which ideas present themselves in their minds from unknown sources, and to examine all such ideas carefully.

教导孩子们鼓励使用他们的第六感，通过这种第六感，来自未知来源的想法在他们的头脑中呈现出来，并仔细检查所有这些想法。

Teach children the full import of the law of compensation as it was interpreted by Ralph Waldo Emerson, and show them how the law works in the small, everyday affairs of life.

告诉孩子们补偿法的全部含义，正如拉尔夫·沃尔多·爱默生所解释的那样，并向他们展示法律是如何在日常生活的琐碎事务中发挥作用的。

Teach children that definiteness of purpose, backed by definite plans persistently and continuously applied, is the most efficacious form of prayer available to human beings.

教导孩子明确目标，坚持不懈地执行明确的计划，是人类最有效的祈祷方式。

Teach children that the space they occupy in the world is measured definitely by the quality and quantity of useful service they render the world.

告诉孩子们，他们在世界上所占有的空间是由他们为世界提供的有用服务的质量和数量来衡量的。

Teach children there is no problem which does not have an appropriate solution and that the solution often may be found in the circumstance creating the problem.

教育孩子没有问题是没有适当的解决办法的，解决办法往往可以在制造问题的情况下找到。

Teach children that their only real limitations are those which they set up or permit others to establish in their own minds.

告诉孩子们，他们唯一真正的局限是那些他们自己建立或允许他人在他们自己的头脑中建立的。

Teach them that man can achieve whatever man can conceive and believe!

告诉他们人类可以实现任何人类能够构想和相信的东西！

Teach children that all schoolhouses and all textbooks are elementary implements which may be helpful in the development of their minds, but that the only school of real value is the great University of Life wherein one has the privilege of learning from experience.

告诉孩子们，所有的学校和教科书都是基本的工具，可能有助于他们头脑的发展，但唯一真正有价值的学校是伟大的生活大学，其中一个人有从经验中学习的特权。

Teach children to be true to themselves at all times and, since they cannot please everybody, therefore to do a good job of pleasing themselves.

教育孩子时刻忠于自己，因为他们不能取悦所有人，所以要做好取悦自己的工作。

Q That is an imposing list, but it seems conspicuous by the fact it ignores practically every subject now taught in the public schools. Was that intended?

这是一个令人印象深刻的清单，但它似乎显而易见的事实是，它几乎忽略了现在在公立学校教授的每一门课程。这是有意的吗？

A Yes. You asked for a list of suggested changes in public school curricula which would benefit children—well, that is what you got.

A 是的。你要求提供一份建议对公立学校课程进行改革的清单，这些改革将有利于儿童ーー嗯，这就是你得到的结果。

Q Some of the changes you suggest are so unorthodox they would shock most of the educators of today, wouldn’t they?

问: 你提出的一些改革是如此非正统，它们会震惊今天的大多数教育工作者，不是吗？

A Most of the educators of today need to be shocked. A good sound shock often helps the brain that has been atrophied by habit.

今天的大多数教育工作者需要感到震惊。一个良好的声音冲击通常有助于大脑已经萎缩的习惯。

Q Would the changes you suggest for the public schools give children immunity against the habit of drifting?

问: 你对公立学校提出的改革建议是否会让孩子们免受漂泊习惯的影响？

A Yes, that is one of the results the changes would bring, but there are others too.

A 是的，这是改革将带来的结果之一，但也有其他的结果。

I can’t say that I agree with each thing on the Devil’s list. However, when I stopped to analyze his list of recommendations, this question came to my mind: Isn’t that what our schools should be teaching our children? The Devil knew this and we didn’t?!?

我不能说我同意魔鬼清单上的每一件事。然而，当我停下来分析他的建议时，我突然想到一个问题: 这不是我们的学校应该教给我们的孩子的东西吗？魔鬼知道而我们不知道? ! ？

I wish Hill had thought to ask why our schools are what they are—and where they are—or what and where they aren’t. The great scholars who designed our system of schooling must have realized the importance of at least some of what the Devil professed our schools should be teaching. Why aren’t these things part of the system? How could the original architects of what is today our compulsory education system have been so far off target? The Devil did make the claim that the school system is one of his primary vehicles for creating and sustaining his large army of drifters. Could it be?

我希望希尔能想到问一问，为什么我们的学校是现在这个样子ーー它们在哪里ーー或者它们是什么，又或者它们不在哪里。那些设计我们学校教育体系的伟大学者一定已经意识到，至少魔鬼宣称的我们学校应该教授一些东西的重要性。为什么这些东西不是系统的一部分？为什么今天我们的义务教育系统的原始设计师会离目标如此遥远？魔鬼确实声称学校系统是他创造和维持他的大批流浪者的主要工具之一。可能吗？

Q How could the suggested changes be forced into the public school system? You know, of course, it is as difficult to get a new idea into an educator’s brain as it is to interest a religious leader in modifying religion so it will help people to get more from life.

问: 建议的改革如何被强制纳入公立学校系统？当然，你知道，要把一个新的想法灌输到一个教育家的大脑里，就像要让一个宗教领袖对改变宗教感兴趣一样困难，因为改变宗教会帮助人们从生活中获得更多。

Any of you who have tried to work to make changes in the public school system are probably nodding right now.

你们中任何一个曾经试图改变公立学校系统的人现在可能正在点头。

A The quickest and surest way to force practical ideas into the public schools is to first introduce the ideas through private schools and establish such a demand for their use that public school officials will be compelled to employ them.

A 将实用思想强加于公立学校的最快和最可靠的方法是首先通过私立学校介绍这些思想，并确立使用这些思想的要求，以迫使公立学校的官员雇用这些思想。

Q Should any other changes be made in the public school system?

问: 公立学校系统是否需要作出其他改变？

A Yes, many. Among other changes needed in all public school programs is the addition of a complete course of training in the psychology of harmonious negotiation between people. All children should be taught how to sell their way through life with the minimum amount of friction.

A 是的，很多。在所有公立学校项目中需要进行的其他变革之一是增加了关于人与人之间和谐谈判心理学的完整培训课程。所有的孩子都应该被教导如何以最小的摩擦来销售他们的生活方式。

Every public school should teach the principles of individual achievement through which one may attain a position of financial independence.

每一所公立学校都应该教授个人成就原则，通过这些原则，人们可以获得经济独立的地位。

Classes should be abolished altogether. They should be replaced by the round table or conference system such as businessmen employ. All students should receive individual instruction and guidance in connection with subjects which cannot be properly taught in groups.

阶级应该完全废除。他们应该被圆桌会议或会议制度所取代，比如商人雇佣制度。所有学生都应该接受个别的指导和指导，这些指导和指导与那些在小组中不能正确教授的科目有关。

Every school should have an auxiliary group of instructors consisting of business and professional people, scientists, artists, engineers, and newspapermen, each of whom would impart to all the students a practical working knowledge of his own profession, business, or occupation. This instruction should be conducted through the conference system, to save the time of the instructors.

每个学校都应该有一个辅助团体，由商业人士和专业人士、科学家、艺术家、工程师和新闻记者组成，每个辅助团体都应该向所有学生传授他们自己的专业、业务或职业的实际工作知识。这个指导应该通过会议系统进行，以节省教员的时间。

Q What you have suggested is, in effect, an auxiliary system of instruction that would give all school children a working knowledge of the practical affairs of life, direct from the original source. Is that the idea?

问: 你所建议的实际上是一个辅助教学系统，它将直接从最初的来源向所有学生提供有关生活实际事务的实用知识。这就是你的想法吗？

A You’ve stated it correctly.

A 你说得对。

This is another subject that strikes close to home. My husband recalls that during the early 1970s in New Jersey, one of the organizations that he was involved with assembled a group of scientists and businessmen to teach basic courses— for example, mathematics and physics—in their fields as volunteers in the public schools, only to be told that since the scientists and businessmen were not professional teachers, they were not welcome.
