More recently, the mission of bringing practical teaching into the schools has been popularized by several groups (Teach for America, America Saves, Junior Achievement), but it is still often viewed as enhancement material and not part of the core curriculum.

这是另一个触目惊心的话题。我丈夫回忆说，上世纪70年代初，在新泽西州，他参与的一个组织召集了一群科学家和商人，在他们的领域里担任公立学校的志愿者，教授数学和物理等基础课程，结果却被告知，由于科学家和商人不是专业教师，他们不受欢迎。最近，将实践教学带入学校的使命已经被一些团体(为美国而教，美国拯救，青年成就)普及，但是它仍然经常被视为提高教学质量的材料，而不是核心课程的一部分。

This and many other shifts in how content, context, principles, and skills are delivered to our children in our compulsory system of education need to be included as part of an interactive, experiential process that will determine how our children live their lives—and what impact they will have on this complex world in which we live. The challenge is this: How do we package it all into a deliverable program that can be systematically and systemically implemented so it is success-oriented, rewarding, and fulfilling for all participants, children and adults alike? I am pleased and proud to say that I work with groups that have designed such programs—and they’re taking these programs forward with definiteness of purpose.

在我们的义务教育体系中，教育内容、背景、原则和技能如何传授给我们的孩子，这种转变以及其他许多转变需要纳入一个互动的、经验性的过程，这个过程将决定我们的孩子如何生活，以及他们将对我们生活的这个复杂的世界产生何种影响。挑战在于: 我们如何将它们整合成一个可交付的项目，这个项目能够系统地、有系统地执行，从而使它对所有参与者，无论是儿童还是成年人，都是以成功为导向、有益且令人满意的？我很高兴也很自豪地说，我与设计了这些项目的团队一起工作，他们正在明确目标地推进这些项目。

Their vision of the future—like ours—is to have an educational system that evolves into a powerful force, capable of producing self-motivated, independent-thinking, self-reliant, contributing members of society. And capable also of producing something more important—future generations ready and able to work in a complex world, to live successfully, to take pleasure in empowering themselves and others, and to make a real and lasting difference in the world as informed, responsible, involved global citizens, each with definiteness of purpose!

他们和我们一样，对未来的愿景是建立一个能够发展成为一股强大力量的教育体系，能够培养出自我激励、独立思考、自力更生、对社会有贡献的成员。而且还能够产生更重要的东西ーー未来的子孙后代已经准备好并能够在一个复杂的世界中工作，能够成功地生活，能够从赋予自己和他人权力中获得乐趣，能够作为知情的、负责任的、参与其中的全球公民，为世界带来真正和持久的变化，每个人都有明确的目标！

Q Let us dismiss the public school system and go back to the churches for a moment. All my life I have heard clergymen preaching against sin and warning sinners to beware and repent so they could be saved. But I have never heard any of them tell me what sin is. Will you give me some light on this subject?

问: 让我们放弃公立学校的制度，回到教堂一会儿。在我的一生中，我一直听到牧师布道反对罪恶，警告罪人当心和忏悔，以便他们可以得救。但是我从来没有听到他们告诉我什么是罪。你能给我讲讲这个问题吗？

A Sin is anything one does or thinks which causes one to be unhappy! Human beings who are in sound physical and spiritual health should be at peace with themselves and always happy. Any form of mental or physical misery indicates the presence of sin.

罪就是一个人做的或想的任何事情导致他不快乐！身体和精神健康的人应该与自己和平相处并且永远快乐。任何形式的精神或身体上的痛苦都表明罪的存在。

Q Name some of the common forms of sin.

问: 列举一些常见的罪恶形式。

A It is a sin to overeat because that leads to ill health and misery.

A 吃得过多是一种罪恶，因为这会导致健康不良和痛苦。

It is a sin to over-indulge in sex because that breaks down one’s will power and leads to the habit of drifting.

过度沉迷于性是一种罪恶，因为那会破坏一个人的意志力，导致漂泊的习惯。

It is a sin to permit one’s mind to be dominated by negative thoughts of envy, greed, fear, hatred, intolerance, vanity, self-pity, or discouragement, because these states of mind lead to the habit of drifting.

允许一个人的心灵被嫉妒、贪婪、恐惧、仇恨、不宽容、虚荣、自怜或气馁等负面思想所支配，是一种罪恶，因为这些思想状态会导致漂泊的习惯。

It is a sin to cheat, lie, and steal, because these habits destroy self-respect, subdue one’s conscience, and lead to unhappiness.

欺骗、撒谎和偷窃是一种罪恶，因为这些习惯破坏了自尊，征服了一个人的良心，并导致不幸。

It is a sin to remain in ignorance because that leads to poverty and loss of self-reliance.

保持无知是一种罪恶，因为这会导致贫穷和失去自力更生。

It is a sin to accept from life anything one does not want because that indicates an unpardonable neglect to use the mind.

从生活中接受任何自己不想要的东西是一种罪恶，因为这意味着不可原谅的忽视了思想的使用。

Q Is it a sin for one to drift through life, without definite aim, plan, or purpose?

一个人在生活中漂泊，没有明确的目标、计划或目的，这是一种罪过吗？

A Yes, because this habit leads to poverty and destroys the privilege of self-determination. It also deprives one of the privilege of using his own mind as a medium of contact with Infinite Intelligence.

答: 是的，因为这种习惯会导致贫穷，破坏自决的特权。它也剥夺了一个人使用自己的思想作为与无限智慧接触的媒介的特权。

Q Are you the chief inspirer of sin?

问: 你是罪恶的主要诱因吗？

A Yes! It is my business to gain control of the minds of people in every way possible.

A 是的! 我的工作就是以各种可能的方式控制人们的思想。

Q Can you control the mind of a person who commits no sin?

问: 你能控制一个没有犯罪的人的思想吗？

A I cannot, because that person never permits his mind to be dominated by any form of negative thought. I cannot enter the mind of one who never sins, let alone control it.

答: 我不能，因为那个人从不允许他的思想被任何形式的消极思想所支配。我无法进入一个从不犯罪，更不用说控制它的人的心灵。

Q What is the commonest and most destructive of all sins?

什么是所有罪恶中最常见和最具破坏性的？

A Fear and ignorance.

恐惧和无知。

Q Have you nothing else to add to the list?

问: 你还有什么要补充的吗？

A There is nothing else to be added.

A 没有其他可以补充的了。

Q What is faith?

什么是信仰？

A It is a state of mind wherein one recognizes and uses the power of positive thought as a medium by which one contacts and draws upon the universal store of Infinite Intelligence at will.

这是一种精神状态，在这种状态中，一个人认识到并使用积极思想的力量，作为一种媒介，通过这种媒介，一个人可以随心所欲地接触和利用无限智慧的普遍存储。

Q In other words, faith is the absence of all forms of negative thought. Is that the idea?

换句话说，信仰就是所有形式的消极思想的消失，是这个意思吗？

A Yes, that is another way of describing it.

A 是的，这是另一种描述它的方式。

Q Has a drifter the capacity to use faith?

是否有一个漂泊者运用信仰的能力？

A He may have the capacity but he does not use it. Everyone has the potential power to clear his mind of all negative thoughts and thereby avail himself of the power of faith.

A 他可能有这个能力，但他没有使用它。每个人都有潜在的力量，可以清除所有的负面思想，从而利用信仰的力量。

Q Stating the matter in another way, faith is definiteness of purpose backed by belief in the attainment of the object of that purpose. Is that correct?

用另一种方式来说明这个问题，信仰是明确的目的，并且相信目的的实现。是这样吗？

A That’s the idea, exactly.

A 就是这个意思，没错。

Faith is “a state of mind wherein one recognizes and uses the power of positive thought as a medium by which one contacts and draws upon the universal store of Infinite Intelligence at will.”

信仰是“一种精神状态，在这种精神状态中，人们认识到并利用积极思想的力量作为一种媒介，通过这种媒介，人们可以随心所欲地接触和利用无限智慧的普遍存储。”

Hill succinctly sums up the definition: “Faith is definiteness of purpose backed by belief in the attainment of the object of that purpose.”

希尔简洁地总结了这个定义: “信仰是明确的目的，并以信仰为基础，以实现目的为目的。”





Chapter Ten

SELF-DISCIPLINE

第十章自律

Q WHAT PREPARATION MUST ONE UNDERGO before being able to move with definiteness of purpose at all times?

问: 一个人必须经历什么样的准备才能始终有明确的目标？

A One must gain mastery over self. This is the second of the seven principles. The person who is not master of himself can never be master of others. Lack of self-mastery is, of itself, the most destructive form of indefiniteness.

一个人必须掌握自我。这是七条原则中的第二条。不能主宰自己的人永远不能主宰别人。缺乏自我掌控本身就是不确定性最具破坏性的形式。

“The person who is not master of himself can never be master of others.”

“不能主宰自己的人永远不能主宰别人。”

How true this is! Think of our political leaders who have fallen from grace because they could not control their own behavior. How can we trust them to control ours?

这是多么真实啊！想想那些因为无法控制自己的行为而失宠的政治领导人。我们怎么能相信他们能控制我们？

Q Where should one begin when making a start at control over self?

当一个人开始控制自己的时候，应该从哪里开始呢？

A By mastering the three appetites responsible for most of one’s lack of self-discipline. The three appetites are (1) the desire for food, (2) the desire for expression of sex, (3) the desire to express loosely organized opinions.

通过掌握一个人缺乏自律的三个原因。这三种欲望是: (1)对食物的渴望，(2)对性表达的渴望，(3)对表达松散组织的观点的渴望。

Q Does man have other appetites which need control?

问: 人类是否有其他需要控制的欲望？

A Yes, many of them, but these three are the ones which should be conquered first. When a man becomes master of these three appetites, he has developed enough self-discipline to conquer easily those of lesser importance.

A 是的，有很多，但是这三个是首先应该征服的。当一个人成为这三种欲望的主人时，他已经发展出足够的自律，可以轻而易举地征服那些不那么重要的欲望。

Q But these are natural appetites. They must be indulged if one is to be healthy and happy.

问: 但这些都是自然的欲望，如果一个人想要健康快乐，就必须纵容这些欲望。

A To be sure they are natural appetites, but they are also dangerous because people who have not mastered themselves overfeed the appetites. Self-mastery contemplates sufficient control over the appetites to enable one to feed them what they need and withhold food not needed.

答: 可以肯定的是，它们是自然的欲望，但它们也是危险的，因为那些没有掌握自己的人会过度满足欲望。自我控制设想对欲望的充分控制，使一个人能够满足他们的需要，并扣留不需要的食物。

Q Your viewpoint is both interesting and educational. Describe the details through which I may understand how and under what circumstances people over-feed the appetites.

你的观点既有趣又有教育意义。描述一些细节，通过这些细节我可以理解人们是如何以及在什么情况下过度满足食欲的。

A Take the desire for physical food, for example. The majority of people are so weak in self-discipline they fill their stomachs with combinations of rich food which please the taste but overwork the organs of digestion and elimination.

以对物质食物的渴望为例。大多数人在自律方面是如此的脆弱，他们用丰富的食物组合填满他们的胃，这些食物的味道令人愉悦，但却过度消化和排泄的器官。

They pour into their stomachs both quantity and combinations of food which the body chemist can dispose of only by converting the food into deadly toxic poisons.

他们把食物的数量和组合倾倒进他们的胃里，而身体化学家只能通过将食物转化为致命的有毒物质来处理这些食物。

These poisons clog and stagnate the body sewer system until it slows down in its work of elimination of waste matter. After a while the sewer system stops working altogether, and the victim has what he calls “constipation.”

这些有毒物质阻塞并使人体下水道系统停滞，直到其排泄废物的速度减慢。过了一会儿，下水道系统完全停止工作，患者患上了他所说的“便秘”

By that time he is ready for the hospital. Auto-intoxication, or body sewer poisoning, takes the machinery of the brain and rolls it into something resembling a wad of putty.

到那时他已经准备好去医院了。自体中毒，或者说下水道中毒，利用大脑的机能，把它卷成一团油灰。

The victim then becomes sluggish in his physical movements and mentally irritable and fussy. If he could only take one good look at, and one bad smell of, his sewer system, he would be ashamed to look himself in the face.

然后受害者在他的身体运动变得迟缓，精神上易怒和挑剔。如果他只能好好看一眼他的下水道系统，再闻一闻，他会羞于直视自己的脸。

City sewers are not the pleasantest of places when they become over-loaded or clogged, but they are clean and sweet compared with the intestinal sewer when it has been overloaded or clogged. This is not a pretty story to be associated with the pleasant and necessary act of eating, but that is where it belongs because over-eating and wrong food combinations are the evils which cause auto-intoxication.

城市下水道负荷过重或堵塞时，并不是最令人愉快的地方，但与超负荷或堵塞时的肠道下水道相比，它们干净、舒适。这不是一个美好的故事，与愉快的和必要的行为吃，但这是它属于，因为过度饮食和错误的食物组合是邪恶的，导致自我陶醉。

People who eat wisely and keep their body sewers clean handicap me because a clean body sewer generally means a sound body and a brain that functions properly.

那些饮食明智并保持下水道清洁的人阻碍了我，因为一个干净的下水道通常意味着一个健康的身体和一个正常工作的大脑。

Imagine—if your imagination can be stretched that far— how any human being could move with definiteness of purpose with his body sewer filled with enough poison to kill a hundred people if it were injected into their bloodstream directly.

想象一下ーー如果你的想象力可以延伸到那么远的地方ーー任何一个人如果被直接注射到血液中，他的身体下水道里充满了足以杀死100人的毒药，他是如何能够明确目标地移动的。

Here again, Napoleon Hill is far ahead of his time. Science eventually caught up with Hill—and even surpassed his intuition about physical processes and how they link to mental and emotional health.

在这一点上，拿破仑 · 希尔又一次遥遥领先于他的时代。科学最终赶上了希尔，甚至超越了他对物理过程及其与心理和情感健康之间联系的直觉。

Q And all this trouble is the result of lack of control over the physical appetite for food?

问: 所有这些麻烦都是由于对食物的身体需求缺乏控制？

A Well, if you wish to be absolutely correct you should say that improper eating is responsible for the majority of the ills of the body, and practically all headaches.

A 哦，如果你希望绝对正确，你应该说不适当的饮食是造成身体大部分疾病和几乎所有头痛的原因。

If you want proof of this, select 100 people suffering with headaches and give each of them a thorough washing out of their body sewer systems with a high enema, and observe that no fewer than ninety-five of the headaches will disappear within a few minutes after their sewers have been cleaned.

如果你想要证明这一点，选择100个头痛的人，用高效灌肠法彻底清洗他们的下水道系统，并观察到不少于95个头痛会在他们的下水道被清理后几分钟内消失。

Q From all you say about the intestinal tract, I gather the impression that mastery over the physical appetite for food means also mastery over the habit of neglecting to keep the intestines clean?

问: 从你所有关于肠道的说法中，我得到的印象是，掌握对食物的身体需求也意味着掌握了忽略保持肠道清洁的习惯？

A Yes, that is true. It is just as important to eliminate the waste matter of the body and the unused portions of food as it is to take the right amount and the correct combinations of food.

A 是的，这是真的。同样重要的是要消除身体的废物和未使用的部分食物，因为它是采取正确的数量和正确的食物组合。

Q I never thought of auto-intoxication as being one of your devices of control over people, and I am utterly shocked to know how many people are victims of this subtle enemy. Let’s hear what you have to say of the other two appetites.

问: 我从来没有想过自我陶醉是你控制别人的手段之一，当我知道有多少人是这个微妙敌人的受害者时，我感到非常震惊。让我们听听你对另外两种食欲有什么看法。

A Well, take the desire for sex expression. Now there is a force with which I master the weak and the strong, the old and the young, the ignorant and the wise. In fact, I master all who neglect to master sex!

好吧，以性表达的欲望为例。现在有一种力量，我可以用它来控制弱者和强者，老者和年轻人，无知者和智者。事实上，我掌握了所有忽略掌握性的人！

Q How can one master the emotion of sex?

问: 怎样才能掌握性的情感？

A By the simple process of transmuting that emotion into some form of activity other than copulation. Sex is one of the greatest of all forces which motivate human beings. Because of this fact it is also one of the most dangerous forces. If humans would control their sex desires and transmute them into a driving force with which to carry on their occupation—that is, if they spent on their work one half the time they dissipate in pursuit of sex, they would never know poverty.

通过简单的过程将这种情绪转化为某种形式的活动，而不是交配。性是激励人类的最强大的力量之一。因为这个事实，它也是最危险的力量之一。如果人类能够控制自己的性欲望，并将其转化为继续从事自己职业的动力---- 也就是说，如果他们把一半的时间花在工作上去追求性，他们就永远不会知道贫穷。

Q Do I understand you to imply there is a relationship between sex and poverty?

问: 我是否理解你暗示性和贫穷之间存在关系？

A Yes, where sex is not under definite control. If allowed to run its natural course, sex will quickly lead one into the habit of drifting.

A 是的，性别不受明确控制。如果任其自然发展，性会很快使人养成随波逐流的习惯。

Q Is there any relationship between sex and leadership?

问: 性和领导力之间有什么关系吗？

A Yes, all great leaders in every walk of life are highly sexed, but they follow the habit of controlling their sex desires, switching them into a driving force behind their occupation.

答: 是的，所有各行各业的伟大领导者都是高度性感的，但他们遵循控制自己性欲的习惯，把性欲转化为职业背后的驱动力。

Q Is the habit of over-indulgence in sex as dangerous as the habit of taking narcotics or liquor?

过度放纵性生活的习惯和吸食麻醉剂或酒精的习惯一样危险吗？

A There is no difference between these habits. Both lead to hypnotic control, through the habit of drifting!

A 这两种习惯没有区别。都通过漂泊的习惯导致催眠控制！

Q Why does the world look upon sex as something vulgar?

问: 为什么这个世界把性看作庸俗的东西？

A Because of the vulgar abuse people have made of this emotion. It is not sex that is vulgar. It is the individual who neglects or refuses to control and guide it.

A 因为人们对这种情感的粗俗滥用。粗俗的不是性。是个人忽视或拒绝控制和引导它。

Q Do you mean, by your statement, that one should not indulge the desire for sex?

问: 你的意思是说，一个人不应该沉溺于对性的渴望？

A No, I mean that sex, like all other forces available to man, should be understood, mastered, and made to serve man. The desire for sex expression is as natural as the desire for food. The desire can no more be killed than one can entirely stop a river from flowing. If the emotion of sex is shut off from the natural mode of expression, it will break out in some other less desirable form, just as a river will, if dammed, break through and flow around the dam. The person who has self-discipline understands the emotion of sex, respects it, and learns to control and transmute it into constructive activities.

答: 不，我的意思是性，就像所有其他可用于人类的力量一样，应该被理解，被掌控，并被用来为人类服务。对性表达的渴望就像对食物的渴望一样自然。欲望不能被扼杀，正如一条河流不能被完全阻断一样。如果性的情感与自然的表达方式隔绝，它就会以其他不那么令人满意的形式爆发出来，就像河流一样，如果筑坝，就会冲破堤坝，绕过堤坝。自律的人理解性的情感，尊重它，并学会控制它，把它转化为建设性的活动。

Q Just what damage is there in over-indulgence of sex?

问: 过度放纵的性生活有什么危害？

A The greatest damage is that it depletes the source of man’s greatest driving force, and wastes, without adequate compensation, man’s creative energy.

A 最大的损害是，它耗尽了人类最大的动力之源，浪费了人类的创造力，而且没有给予足够的补偿。

It dissipates energy needed by nature to maintain physical health. Sex is nature’s most useful therapeutic force.

性是自然界最有用的治疗力量，它可以消耗自然界维持身体健康所需要的能量。

It depletes the magnetic energy which is the source of an attractive, pleasing personality.

它消耗了磁性能量，而磁性能量是一个有吸引力的，令人愉快的人格的来源。

It removes the sparkle from one’s eyes and sets up discord in the tone of one’s voice.

它使一个人的眼睛失去光彩，使一个人的声调变得不和谐。

It destroys enthusiasm, subdues ambition, and leads inevitably to the habit of drifting on all subjects.

它摧毁了热情，压制了野心，并不可避免地导致在所有问题上游移不定的习惯。

Q I would like for you to answer my question in another way by telling me what beneficial ends the emotion of sex may be made to attain, if mastered and transmuted.

问: 我想让你用另一种方式回答我的问题，告诉我，如果能够掌握和改变，性爱的情感可以达到什么样的有益结果。

A Controlled sex supplies the magnetic force that attracts people to one another. It is the most important factor of a pleasing personality.

受控制的性行为提供了吸引人们彼此的磁力。这是一个令人愉快的人格最重要的因素。

It gives quality to the tone of voice and enables one to convey through the voice any feeling desired.

它赋予声音的质量，并使人能够通过声音传达任何想要的感觉。

It serves, as nothing else can serve, to give motive-power to one’s desires.

任何其他事物都不能做到的是，它使人的欲望具有动力。

It keeps the nervous system charged with the energy needed to carry on the work of maintaining the body.

它使神经系统充满能量，以进行维持身体的工作。

It sharpens the imagination and enables one to create useful ideas.

它可以激发想象力，使人产生有用的想法。

It gives quickness and definiteness to one’s physical and mental movements.

它使一个人的身体和心理运动变得敏捷和明确。

It gives one persistence and perseverance in the pursuit of one’s major purpose in life.

它使人在追求人生的主要目标时具有坚持和毅力。

It is a great antidote for all fear.

这是治疗所有恐惧的良药。

It gives one immunity against discouragement.

它给予一个抵抗挫折的豁免权。

It helps to master laziness and procrastination.

它有助于克服懒惰和拖延症。

It gives one physical and mental endurance while undergoing any form of opposition or defeat.

在经历任何形式的对抗或失败时，它给予一个人身体和精神上的忍耐力。

It gives one the fighting qualities necessary under all circumstances for self-defense.

它赋予一个人在任何情况下自卫所必需的战斗品质。

In brief, it makes winners and not quitters!

简而言之，它是成功者，而不是放弃者！

Q Are those all the advantages you claim for controlled sex energy?

问: 这些都是你声称的控制性能量的好处吗？

A No, they are only some of the more important benefits it provides. Perhaps some will believe the greatest of all the virtues of sex is that it is nature’s method of perpetuation of all living things. This alone should remove all thought that sex is vulgar.

答: 不，它们只是它提供的更重要的好处中的一部分。也许有些人会相信，性爱最大的优点就是它是所有生物延续生命的自然方法。仅此一点就足以消除所有认为性是粗俗的想法。

Q I gather, from what you say, that the emotion of sex is a virtue, not a fault.

问: 我从你的话中推断，性的情感是一种美德，而不是缺点。

A It is a virtue when controlled and directed to the attainment of desirable ends. It is a fault when neglected and permitted to lead to acts of lust.

当被控制和引导以达到理想的目的时，它就是一种美德。这是一个错误，如果忽视和允许导致的行为淫欲。

Q Why aren’t these truths taught to children by their parents and the public schools?

问: 为什么家长和公立学校不教给孩子这些真理？

A The neglect is due to ignorance of the real nature of sex. It is just as necessary in maintaining health for one to understand and properly use the emotion of sex as it is to keep the body sewer system clean. Both subjects should be taught in all public schools and all homes where there are children.

这种忽视是由于对性的真实本质的无知。正如保持身体下水道系统的清洁一样，对于一个人来说，理解和正确使用性的情感对于保持健康也是必要的。所有公立学校和有儿童的家庭都应教授这两门课程。

Q Wouldn’t the majority of parents need instruction on the proper function and use of sex before they could intelligently teach their children?

问: 难道大多数父母在智慧地教育他们的孩子之前，不需要关于性的正确功能和使用的指导吗？

A Yes, and so would the public schoolteachers.

A 是的，公立学校的老师也是。

Q What relative position of importance would you give to the need for accurate knowledge on the subject of sex?

问: 你认为在性方面需要准确的知识有多重要？

A It is next to the top of the list. There is but one thing of greater importance to human beings. That is accurate thought.

A 它紧挨着名单的顶部。对人类来说，只有一件事比这更重要。这是正确的想法。

“There is but one thing of greater importance to human beings. That is accurate thought.”

“对人类来说，只有一件事更重要，那就是准确的思想。”

Q Do I understand you to say that knowledge of the true functions of sex and ability to think accurately are the two things of greatest importance to mankind?

问: 你是否认为性的真正功能和精确思考的能力是人类最重要的两件事？

A That is what I intended you to understand. Accurate thinking comes first because it is the solution to all man’s problems, the answer to all his prayers, the source of opulence and all material possessions. Accurate thinking is aided by properly controlled and directed sex emotion because sex emotion is the same energy as that with which one thinks. It begins with those who desire self-determination sufficiently to be willing to pay its price. No one can be entirely free—spiritually, mentally, physically, and economically—without learning the art of accurate thinking. No one can learn to think accurately without including, as a part of the needed knowledge, information on the control of sex emotion through transmutation.

A 这就是我想让你明白的。精确的思考是第一位的，因为它是解决所有人类问题的方法，是对他们所有祈祷的回应，是财富和物质财富的来源。正确的思考得益于适当的控制和导向的性情绪，因为性情绪与人们思考的能量是一样的。它始于那些充分渴望自决，愿意付出代价的人。没有人可以在精神上、心理上、身体上和经济上完全自由，除非学会准确思考的艺术。没有人可以学会准确地思考，除非包括，作为所需知识的一部分，关于通过转化控制性情绪的信息。

Q It will be a great surprise to many people to learn there is so close a relationship between thinking and sex emotion. Tell us, now, about the third appetite, and let’s see what it has to do with self-discipline.

很多人都会感到惊讶，因为他们知道思维和性情感之间有着如此密切的关系。现在，告诉我们第三个胃口，让我们看看它和自律有什么关系。

A The habit of expressing loosely organized opinions is one of the most destructive of habits. Its destructiveness consists in its tendency to influence people to guess instead of searching for the facts when they form opinions, create ideas, or organize plans.

表达松散观点的习惯是最具破坏性的习惯之一。它的破坏性在于，当人们形成意见、产生想法或组织计划时，它倾向于影响人们去猜测，而不是去寻找事实。

The habit develops a grasshopper mind—one that jumps from one thing to another but never completes anything.

这种习惯会培养出一种蚱蜢般的头脑——从一件事跳到另一件事，但从未完成任何事情。

And of course, carelessness in the expression of opinions leads to the habit of drifting. From there it is only a step or two until one is bound by the law of hypnotic rhythm which automatically prohibits accurate thinking.

当然，表达意见时的粗心大意也会导致随波逐流的习惯。从那里它只是一个或两个步骤，直到一个人被催眠节奏的法律自动禁止准确的思考。

“The habit of expressing loosely organized opinions is one of the most destructive of habits.”

“表达松散观点的习惯是最具破坏性的习惯之一。”

Q What other disadvantages are there in free expression of opinions?

问: 自由表达意见还有什么其他缺点？

A The person who talks too much informs the world of his aims and plans and gives to others the opportunity to profit by his ideas.

说得太多的人会让世界知道他的目标和计划，并给别人机会从他的想法中获益。

Wise men keep their plans to themselves and refrain from expressing uninvited opinions. This prevents others from appropriating their ideas and makes it difficult for others to interfere with their plans.

聪明人把自己的计划藏在心里，不发表不请自来的意见。这样可以防止别人盗用他们的想法，并使其他人难以干预他们的计划。

Q Why do so many people indulge in the habit of expressing uninvited opinions?

问: 为什么这么多人习惯于表达不请自来的意见？

A The habit is one way of expressing egotism and vanity. The desire for self-expression is inborn in people. The motive behind the habit is to attract the attention of others and to impress them favorably. Actually it has just the opposite effect. When the self-invited speaker attracts attention, it usually is unfavorable.

A 习惯是表达自负和虚荣心的一种方式。自我表达的欲望是与生俱来的。这个习惯背后的动机是为了吸引别人的注意力并给他们留下良好的印象。事实上，它只有相反的效果。当自我邀请的说话者引起注意时，通常是不利的。

Q Yes, what other disadvantages has the habit?

问: 是的，这个习惯还有什么其他缺点？

A The person who insists on talking seldom has an opportunity to learn by listening to others.

坚持说话的人很少有机会通过倾听别人来学习。

Q But isn’t it true that a magnetic speaker often puts himself in the way of opportunity to benefit himself by attracting the attention of others through his powers of oratory?

但是，一个有吸引力的演讲者通常会通过他的演讲能力来吸引别人的注意，从而使自己有机会从中受益，这是真的吗？

A Yes, a magnetic orator does have an asset of tremendous value in his ability to impress people by his speech, but he cannot make the best use of this asset if he forces his speech on others without their invitation.

答: 是的，一个富有磁性的演说家的确有一项巨大的资产，那就是他的演说能够给人们留下深刻印象，但是如果他在没有别人邀请的情况下强迫别人听他的演说，他就不能充分利用这项资产。

No single quality adds more to one’s personality than the ability to speak with emotional feeling, force, and conviction, but the speaker must not impose his speech upon others without being invited to do so. There is an old saying that nothing is worth more than its actual cost. This applies as well to the free uninvited expression of opinions as to material things.

没有任何一种品质能比带着感情、力量和信念说话的能力更能增加一个人的个性，但是演讲者在没有被邀请的情况下不能把他的演讲强加给别人。有句老话说，没有什么比它的实际成本更值钱。这也适用于对物质事物不请自来的意见表达。

Q What about people who volunteer their opinions by expressing them in writing? Do they also suffer by lack of self-discipline?

问: 那些通过书面形式表达自己观点的人呢？他们是否也因缺乏自律而受苦？

A One of the worst pests on earth is the person who writes uninvited letters to people of prominence. Men in public office, moving picture stars, men who have succeeded in business or written a best-selling book, and people whose names appear often in the newspapers are continuously besieged by people who write letters expressing their opinion on all subjects.

地球上最可怕的害虫之一是给名人写不请自来的信的人。担任公职的人、电影明星、在商业上取得成功或写出畅销书的人，以及那些经常出现在报纸上的人，不断被那些就所有问题写信表达意见的人所包围。

Q But the writing of uninvited letters is a harmless way of finding pleasure through self-expression, is it not? What damage does one do by the habit?

但是写不请自来的信是一种通过自我表达来寻找快乐的无害方式，不是吗？一个人的习惯会造成什么样的伤害？

Take a moment to remember that letter-writing was about the only way to communicate in the written form when Napoleon Hill wrote this manuscript. As you read, think about how his thoughts would apply to today’s world of blogging and social networking.

花一点时间想想，当拿破仑 · 希尔写下这份手稿时，写信是以书面形式交流的唯一方式。当你阅读时，想想他的想法将如何应用到当今的博客和社交网络世界。

A Habits are contagious. Every habit attracts a flock of its relatives. The habit of doing anything that is useless leads to the formation of other habits that are useless, especially the habit of drifting.

习惯是会传染的。每一种习惯都会吸引一群亲戚。做任何无用的事情的习惯会导致其他无用的习惯的形成，尤其是随波逐流的习惯。

But that is not all the dangers associated with the habit of indulging in uninvited expression of opinions. The habit creates enemies and places in their hands dangerous weapons by which they may do great injury to the one who indulges in it. Thieves and confidence men and racketeers pay big prices for the names and addresses of the writers of uninvited letters, knowing as they do the writers of these letters become easy victims of all manner of schemes that result in the loss of their money. They refer to the writers of such letters as “nuts.” If you wish to know how foolish people are who write uninvited letters, read the “nut column” of any newspaper—the column in which the paper publishes the voluntary opinions of its readers—and you will see for yourself how the writers of such letters antagonize people and invite opposition from others.

但这并不是沉溺于不请自来地表达意见的习惯所带来的全部危险。习惯在他们手中制造了敌人和危险的武器，他们可能会用这些武器伤害那些沉迷于此的人。小偷、骗子和敲诈者为了不速之客的名字和地址付出了高昂的代价，因为他们知道这些信件的作者很容易成为各种骗局的受害者，最终导致他们的金钱损失。他们把这类信件的作者称为“疯子”如果你想知道写不请自来信的人有多愚蠢，那就读读任何报纸的“疯狂专栏”——该报发表读者自愿意见的专栏——你就会亲眼看到，这类信件的作者是如何与人作对，并招致他人反对的。

Q I had no idea, Your Majesty, that people get into so much difficulty through uninvited expression of their opinions, but now that you have brought up the subject I do remember writing the editor of a prominent magazine an uninvited letter of criticism which cost me a fine position on his staff, at a fat salary.

问: 我不知道，陛下，人们会因为不请自来地表达自己的意见而陷入如此困难的境地，但既然你提到了这个话题，我确实记得给一家知名杂志的编辑写了一封不请自来的批评信，这让我在他的职员中失去了一个很好的职位，薪水很高。

A That is a perfect example. The proper place to begin self-discipline is right where you stand. The way to begin is by recognizing the truth—that there is nothing for good or evil throughout the myriads of universes except the power of natural law. There is no individual personality anywhere throughout the myriad of universes with the slightest power to influence a human being save nature and human beings themselves.

A 这是一个完美的例子。开始自律的适当地方就是你站的地方。开始的方法是认识到这样一个事实ーー在无数的宇宙中，除了自然法则的力量之外，没有善与恶之分。在无数的宇宙中，任何地方都没有一个个人具有影响人类拯救自然和人类自身的最轻微的力量。

There is no human being now living, no human being has ever lived, and no human being ever will live with the right or the power to deprive another human being of the inborn privilege of free and independent thought. That privilege is the only one over which any human being can have absolute control. No adult human being ever loses the right to freedom of thought, but most humans lose the benefits of this privilege either by neglect or because it has been taken away from them by their parents or religious instructors before the age of understanding. These are self-evident truths, no less important because they are being called to your attention by the Devil than they would be if brought to your attention by my opposition.

现在没有人活着，从来没有人活着，没有人会有权利或权力剥夺另一个人与生俱来的自由和独立思考的特权。这种特权是任何人都可以绝对控制的唯一特权。没有一个成年人会失去思想自由的权利，但是大多数人失去了这种特权的好处，要么是因为忽视，要么是因为他们的父母或宗教教师在理解他们的年龄之前就剥夺了他们的这种权利。这些是不言而喻的真理，同样重要，因为它们被魔鬼召唤来引起你们的注意，就像它们被我的反对者引起你们的注意一样。

Hill distinguishes our right to have independent thoughts from our uninvited expression of those thoughts. How would you apply this principle in today’s world of blogging and social media?

希尔将我们拥有独立思考的权利与我们不请自来地表达这些思考的权利区分开来。在今天的博客和社交媒体的世界里，你会如何应用这个原则？

Q But what are people going to lean upon in the hour of emergency when they know not where nor to whom to appeal?

问: 但是，当人们不知道在哪里或向谁求助时，在紧急情况下他们会依靠什么呢？

A Let them lean upon the only dependable power available to any human being.

让他们依靠任何人类唯一可靠的力量。

Q And what is that?

问: 那是什么？

A Themselves! The power of their own thoughts. The only power they can control and may rely upon. The only power which cannot be perverted, colored, modified, and falsified by their dishonest fellow human beings.

他们自己！他们自己思想的力量。他们唯一可以控制和依靠的力量。唯一不能被他们那些不诚实的人类同胞所歪曲、歪曲、改造和篡改的力量。

“The only dependable power available to any human being . . . The power of their own thoughts. The only power they can control and may rely upon.”

“人类唯一可以依靠的力量... ... 就是他们自己思想的力量。他们唯一可以控制和依赖的力量。”

You may not be able to control other people . . . but you can control how you react to them and their actions. This is an easy thing to say but much more difficult to do. We tend to want to change other people when we can truly only change ourselves and how we react to others.

你可能无法控制他人... ... 但你可以控制自己对他人及其行为的反应。说起来容易，做起来难得多。当我们只能真正改变自己以及我们对他人的反应时，我们倾向于去改变他人。

Q All you say seems logical, but why must I come to the Devil to discover such profound truths? Let’s get back to the seven principles. You have already disclosed enough information to show clearly that the secret of how to break the power of hypnotic rhythm is wrapped in the seven principles. You have shown, too, that the most important of these principles is self-discipline. Now go ahead and describe the other five principles you have not yet mentioned, and indicate what part they play in giving one self-discipline.

问: 你所说的一切似乎都是合乎逻辑的，但是为什么我必须到魔鬼那里去发现如此深奥的真理呢？让我们回到七个原则。你们已经透露了足够的信息来清楚地表明，如何打破催眠节奏的力量的秘密包含在七个原则中。你也证明了这些原则中最重要的是自律。现在继续描述你还没有提到的其他五个原则，并指出它们在实现自律方面所起的作用。

A First, let me summarize that part of my confession we have already covered.

A 首先，让我总结一下我已经讲过的部分自白。

I have frankly told you that my two most effective devices for mastering human beings are the habit of drifting and the law of hypnotic rhythm. I have shown you that drifting is not a natural law, but a man-made habit which leads to man’s submission to the law of hypnotic rhythm.

我已经坦率地告诉过你们，我掌握人类最有效的两个方法就是随波逐流的习惯和催眠律。我已经向你们表明，漂泊不是一种自然法则，而是一种人为的习惯，它导致人们服从于催眠律。

The seven principles are the media by which man may break the hold of hypnotic rhythm and take possession, again, of his own mind. You see, therefore, the seven principles are the seven steps which lead victims of hypnotic rhythm out of the self-made prisons in which they are bound.

这七项原则是人们打破催眠的节奏，再次占有自己心灵的媒介。因此，你们可以看到，这七个原则是把催眠节奏的受害者从他们被束缚的自制监狱中引出来的七个步骤。

Q The seven principles are the master key that unlocks the door to spiritual, mental, and economic self-determination? Is that true?

7个原则是打开精神、心理和经济自决之门的万能钥匙？是真的吗？

A Yes, that’s another way of stating the truth.

A 是的，这是陈述事实的另一种方式。





Chapter Eleven

LEARNING FROM ADVERSITY

第十一章从逆境中学习

Q IS FAILURE EVER A BENEFIT TO MAN?

失败对人类有益吗？

A Yes. Indeed, learning from adversity is the third of the seven principles. But few people know that every adversity brings with it the seed of an equivalent advantage. Still fewer people know the difference between temporary defeat and failure. If this knowledge were generally known, I would be deprived of one of my strongest weapons of control over human beings.

A 是的。事实上，从逆境中学习是七条原则中的第三条。但很少有人知道，每一次逆境都会带来同等优势的种子。更少的人知道暂时的失败和失败的区别。如果这种知识被普遍知道，我将被剥夺我对人类最强大的控制武器之一。

Q But I understood you to say that failure is one of your greatest allies. I got the impression from your confession that failure causes people to lose ambition and quit trying, and then you take them over without opposition on their part.

问: 但是我理解你说失败是你最大的盟友之一。我从你的坦白中得到的印象是，失败会让人失去雄心，放弃尝试，然后你接管了他们，而他们没有反对。

A That is just the point. I take them over after they quit trying. If they knew the difference between temporary defeat and failure, they would not quit when they meet with opposition from life. If they knew that every form of defeat, and all failures, bring with them the seed of unborn opportunity, they would keep on fighting and win. Success usually is but one short step beyond the point where one quits fighting.

A 这正是问题所在。在他们放弃尝试之后，我接管了他们。如果他们知道暂时的失败和失败的区别，他们就不会在遇到生活的阻力时放弃。如果他们知道每一次失败，每一次失败，都会带来未来机会的种子，他们就会继续战斗，取得胜利。成功通常只是离退出战斗的一小步。

Q Is that all one might learn from adversity, defeat, and failure?

问: 所有人都可以从逆境、失败和失败中学习吗？

A No, that is the least of what one might learn. I hate to tell you this, but failure often serves as a blessing in disguise because it breaks the grip of hypnotic rhythm and frees the mind for a fresh start.

A 不，这是一个人可能学到的最起码的东西。我不想告诉你这个，但失败往往是塞翁失马，焉知非福，因为它打破了催眠的节奏，释放了心灵，重新开始。

Q Now we are getting somewhere. So you have confessed, at long last, that even nature’s law of hypnotic rhythm can be and often is annulled by nature herself. Is that correct?

现在我们有了一些进展。所以你终于承认，即使自然的催眠律也可以而且经常被自然本身废除。是这样吗？

A No, that is not stating the matter accurately. Nature never reverses any of her natural laws. Nature does not take away a human being’s freedom of thought through hypnotic rhythm. The individual gives up his freedom by abuse of this law. If a man jumped from a tree and was killed by the sudden impact of his body with the earth, through the law of gravity, you wouldn’t say nature murdered him, would you? You would say the man neglected to relate himself properly to the law of gravity.

A 不，那不是准确地陈述事情。自然界从不颠倒任何一条自然法则。自然不会通过催眠的节奏夺走人的思想自由。个人滥用这项法律而放弃了自由。如果一个人从树上跳下来，被他的身体与地球的突然碰撞所杀死，通过万有引力定律，你不会说是大自然谋杀了他，对吗？你可能会说这个人忽略了将自己与万有引力定律恰当地联系起来。

Q I am beginning to see. The law of hypnotic rhythm is capable of both negative and positive application. It may drag one down to slavery through loss of the privilege of freedom of thought, or it may help one rise to great heights of achievement through the free use of thought, depending on how the individual relates himself to the law. Is that correct?

我开始明白了。催眠节律具有消极和积极的双重作用。它可能通过丧失思想自由的特权而把一个人变成奴隶，或者它可能通过自由运用思想而帮助一个人达到伟大的成就，这取决于个人如何将自己与法律联系起来。是这样吗？

A Now you have it right.

A 现在你说对了。

Q But what about failure? One does not fail intentionally, with purpose aforethought. No one encourages temporary defeat. These are circumstances over which the individual often has no control whatsoever. How, then, can it be said that nature does not take away one’s freedom of thought when failure destroys ambition, will power, and the self-confidence essential to make a fresh start?

问: 那么失败呢？一个人不会故意失败，也不会有预谋。没有人鼓励暂时的失败。这些情况往往是个人无法控制的。那么，当失败摧毁野心、意志力和重新开始所必需的自信时，怎么能说自然不会夺走一个人的思想自由呢？

A Failure is a man-made circumstance. It is never real until it has been accepted by man as permanent. Stating it another way, failure is a state of mind; therefore, it is something an individual can control until he neglects to exercise this privilege. Nature does not force people to fail. But nature does impose her law of hypnotic rhythm upon all minds and through this law gives permanency to the thoughts which dominate those minds.

失败是人为的环境。只有当它被人类接受为永恒的时候，它才是真实的。换句话说，失败是一种精神状态; 因此，它是一个人可以控制的东西，直到他忽略了行使这种特权。大自然不会强迫人们失败。但是大自然确实将她的催眠律法强加于所有的头脑，并且通过这个律法给予支配那些头脑的想法永久性。

In other words, failure thoughts are taken over by the law of hypnotic rhythm and made permanent if the individual accepts any circumstances as being permanent failure. That same law just as readily takes over and makes permanent thoughts of success.

换句话说，失败的想法被催眠节奏法则所接管，如果个人接受任何情况为永久的失败，那么失败的想法就会永久化。同样的法则也很容易取而代之，使人们永远想着成功。

“Failure is a state of mind; therefore, it is something an individual can control until he neglects to exercise this privilege.”

“失败是一种精神状态，因此，它是一个人可以控制的东西，直到他忽略了行使这种特权。”

Can this be true? Has Hill convinced you that “failure is a man-made circumstance”? I believe he makes a compelling case. If I look closely at my life—my own successes and failures in business, mistakes, and missteps—can I claim that anyone is responsible other than myself? Will a personal inventory of your life yield different results? Hill has helped me place a different value on failure than I did in the past . . .

这是真的吗？希尔是否让你相信“失败是人为的” ？我相信他的观点很有说服力。如果我仔细审视我的生活ーー我自己在商业上的成功和失败、错误和失误ーー我能否断言除了我自己之外，还有其他人对此负有责任？个人的生活清单是否会产生不同的结果？希尔帮助我重新定义了失败的价值观，与过去不同... ..。

Q What part, then, does failure play in helping an individual break the grip of hypnotic rhythm after that law has been fastened upon his mind?

问: 那么，失败在帮助一个人打破催眠节奏方面起到了什么作用呢？

A Failure brings a climax in which one has the privilege of clearing his mind of fear and making a new start in another direction. Failure proves conclusively that something is wrong with one’s aims or the plans by which the object of these aims is sought. Failure is the dead end of the habit-path one has been following, and when it is reached it forces one to leave that path and take up another, thereby creating a new rhythm.

失败带来了一个高潮，在这个高潮中，一个人有特权清除他的恐惧心理，并在另一个方向上开始一个新的开始。失败最终证明，一个人的目标或寻求这些目标的计划出了问题。失败是一个人一直遵循的习惯道路的死胡同，当它到达时，它会迫使一个人离开那条道路，走上另一条道路，从而创造一种新的节奏。

But failure does more than this. It gives an individual an opportunity to test himself wherein he may learn how much will power he possesses. Failure also forces people to learn many truths they would never discover without it. Failure often leads an individual to an understanding of the power of self-discipline without which no one could turn back after having once been the victim of hypnotic rhythm.

但失败不仅仅如此。它给了一个人一个机会来检验自己，在这个机会中他可以了解自己拥有多少意志力。失败也迫使人们学会许多真理，如果没有它们，他们永远不会发现。失败往往会让一个人认识到自律的力量，没有自律，任何人都不可能在一度成为催眠节奏的受害者之后回头。

Study the lives of all people who achieve outstanding success in any calling and observe, with profit, that their success is usually in exact ratio to their experiences of defeat before succeeding.

研究所有在任何领域取得杰出成就的人的生活，带着利益观察他们的成功通常与他们成功之前的失败经历成正比。

“Failure brings a climax in which one has the privilege of clearing his mind of fear and making a new start in another direction.”

“失败带来了一个高潮，在这个高潮中，一个人有特权清除自己的恐惧，朝着另一个方向重新开始。”

Q Is this all you have to say of the advantages of failure?

问: 这就是你所说的失败的好处吗？

A No, I have barely begun. If you want the real significance of adversity, failure, defeat, and all other experiences which break up a human being’s habits and force him to form new habits, watch nature at her work. Nature uses illness to break the physical rhythm of the body when the cells and organs become improperly related. She uses economic depressions to break the rhythm of mass thought when great numbers of people become improperly related—through business, social, and political activities. And she uses failure to break the rhythm of negative thought when an individual becomes improperly related to himself in his own mind.

A 不，我才刚刚开始。如果你想知道逆境、失败、失败以及其他所有打破人类习惯并迫使他形成新习惯的经历的真正意义，那就观察大自然的工作吧。当细胞和器官不适当地联系在一起时，大自然用疾病来打破身体的物理节奏。她利用经济萧条打破了大众思想的节奏，因为很多人通过商业、社会和政治活动变得不适当地联系在一起。当一个人在自己的思想中与自己不恰当地联系起来时，她利用失败来打破消极思想的节奏。

Observe carefully and you will see that everywhere in nature there is always at work a natural law which gives eternal change to all matter, all energy, and to the power of thought. The only permanent thing in the universes is change. Eternal, inexorable change—through which every atom of matter and every unit of energy has the opportunity to properly relate itself to all other units of matter and energy, and every human being has the opportunity and the privilege of properly relating himself to all other human beings no matter how many mistakes he makes, or how many times or in what ways he may be defeated.

仔细观察，你会发现在自然界的任何地方，总是有一条自然法则在起作用，它给所有的物质、所有的能量和思想的力量带来永恒的变化。宇宙中唯一永恒的东西就是变化。永恒的、不可阻挡的变化ーー通过这种变化，每一个物质原子和每一个能量单位都有机会正确地与所有其他物质和能量单位联系起来，每一个人都有机会和特权正确地与所有其他人联系起来，不管他犯了多少错误，犯了多少次错误，也不管他以何种方式被击败。

When mass failure overtakes a nation, such as the 1929 world business depression, the circumstance is in perfect harmony with nature’s plan to break up man’s habits and give out fresh opportunities.

当大规模的失败席卷一个国家，比如1929年的世界商业萧条，环境与大自然打破人类习惯、提供新机会的计划是完美和谐的。

The beauty of publishing this book now, during the current economic turmoil, is that nature is once again breaking up man’s habits and presenting fresh opportunities.

在当前的经济动荡时期，出版这本书的好处在于，大自然再次打破了人类的习惯，提供了新的机遇。

Q What you are saying intrigues me. Am I to understand that hypnotic rhythm has something to do with the way people relate themselves to one another?

你说的话引起了我的兴趣。我是否可以理解，催眠节奏与人们相互联系的方式有关？

A That abstract, elusive thing called character is nothing but a manifestation of the law of hypnotic rhythm; therefore, when speaking of one’s character it would be proper to say his thought-habits have been crystallized into a positive or a negative personality, through hypnotic rhythm. One is good or bad because of the knitting together of his thoughts and deeds through hypnotic rhythm. One is bound by poverty or blessed with abundance because his aims, plans, and desires, or lack of them, have been made permanent and real by hypnotic rhythm.

A 所谓性格的那种抽象、难以捉摸的东西只不过是催眠律的表现; 因此，当谈到一个人的性格时，通过催眠律可以恰当地说，他的思维习惯已经具体化为积极或消极的性格。一个人是好是坏，是因为他的思想和行为通过催眠的节奏编织在一起。一个人因为他的目标、计划和欲望，或者缺乏它们，而被贫穷所束缚，或者被富足所祝福，因为他的目标、计划和欲望，或者缺乏它们，已经被催眠的节奏变得永恒和真实。

Q Is that all you have to say of the connection between hypnotic rhythm and human relationships?

问: 关于催眠节奏和人际关系之间的联系，这就是你要说的全部吗？

A No, I have just begun. Remember while I am talking I am speaking of the influence of hypnotic rhythm in connection with all human relationships. Men who succeed in business do so entirely because of the way they relate themselves to their associates and to others outside of the business.

A 不，我才刚刚开始。记住，当我在讲话的时候，我是在谈论催眠节奏对所有人类关系的影响。在商业领域取得成功的人之所以能够取得成功，完全是因为他们与自己的同事以及商业领域以外的其他人的关系。

Professional men who succeed do so largely because of the manner in which they relate themselves to their clients. It is much more important for the lawyer to know people and to know the laws of nature than it is to know the law. And the doctor is a failure before he starts unless he knows how to relate himself to his patients so as to establish their faith in him.

成功的专业人士之所以能做到这一点，很大程度上是因为他们与客户相处的方式。对于律师来说，认识人和了解自然规律要比了解法律重要得多。医生在开始之前就是一个失败者，除非他知道如何与他的病人建立联系，从而建立他们对他的信任。

Marriage succeeds or fails entirely because of the manner in which the participants relate themselves to one another. Proper relationship in marriage begins with a proper motive for the marriage. Most marriages do not bring happiness because the contracting parties neither understand, nor attempt to understand, the law of hypnotic rhythm, through the operation of which every word they speak, every act in which they engage, and every motive by which they are inspired to deal with each other is picked up and woven into a web that entangles them in controversial misery or gives to them the wings of freedom through which they soar above all forms of unhappiness.

婚姻的成败完全取决于参与者彼此相处的方式。适当的婚姻关系始于适当的婚姻动机。大多数婚姻不会带来幸福，因为缔约双方既不理解，也不试图理解催眠律，通过操作，他们说的每一个字，他们从事的每一个行为，他们被激励去处理对方的每一个动机，被挑选出来，编织成一张网，把他们困在有争议的痛苦之中，或给他们自由的翅膀，通过这张翅膀，他们超越了所有形式的不幸。

Every newly made acquaintanceship between people ripens into friendship and then into spiritual harmony (sometimes called love) or plants a germ of suspicion and doubt which evolves and grows into open rebellion, according to the way in which the participants in the acquaintanceship relate themselves to one another.

人们之间每一次新的相识都会发展成为友谊，然后进入精神和谐(有时称为爱) ，或者根据相识中的参与者彼此之间的关系，培育出怀疑和疑虑的种子，这些怀疑和疑虑会演变成公开的反叛。

Hypnotic rhythm picks up the dominating motives, aims, purposes, and feelings of the contacting minds and weaves these into some degree of faith or fear, love or hatred. After the pattern has taken definite shape, as it does with time, it is forced upon the contacting minds and made a part thereof.

催眠的节奏拾起主导的动机，目的，目的和感情的联系心灵和编织这些到一定程度的信仰或恐惧，爱或仇恨。当模式成为确定的形状之后，就像它随着时间的推移一样，它被强加在接触者的头脑中，并成为其中的一部分。

In this silent way does nature make permanent the dominating factors of every human relationship. In every human relationship the evil motives and the evil deeds of the contacting individuals are coordinated and consolidated into definite form and subtly woven into that all-important human trait known as character. In the same manner, the motives and the deeds of good are consolidated and forced upon the individual. You see, therefore, it is not only one’s deeds but also one’s very thoughts which determine the nature of all human relationships.

在这种无声的方式中，大自然使每一个人类关系永远成为主导因素。在每一种人际关系中，相互联系的个体的邪恶动机和邪恶行为被协调和统一成一种明确的形式，并巧妙地编织进被称为性格的至关重要的人类特征中。同样，善的动机和行为也被巩固并强加于个人。因此，你看，不仅是一个人的行为，也是一个人的思想决定了所有人类关系的本质。

Q You are leading into pretty deep water. Let’s keep near the shore, where I can follow you without fear of getting beyond a safe depth. Go ahead and tell me how this subject of human relationships actually works in the current affairs of a problem-filled world such as we have today.

问: 你现在的处境相当困难。让我们保持靠近海岸，在那里我可以跟随你而不用担心到达一个安全的深度。请继续告诉我这个人际关系的主题实际上是如何在一个充满问题的世界的时事中工作的，就像我们今天这样。

A That is a happy thought. But let me make sure you understand the principles I am telling about, before I try to show you how to apply them in the affairs of life.

A 这是一个令人高兴的想法。但是，在我向你们展示如何在生活中应用这些原则之前，请先让我确保你们明白我所讲的这些原则。

I wish to be sure you understand that the law of hypnotic rhythm is something that no one can control, influence, or evade. But everyone can relate himself to this law so as to benefit by its inexorable operation. Harmonious relationship with the law consists entirely of the individual changing his habits so they represent the circumstances and the things the individual wants and is willing to accept.

我希望你们明白，催眠律是没有人能够控制、影响或逃避的。但是每个人都可以把自己和这个规律联系起来，从而受益于它不可阻挡的运作。与法律的和谐关系完全由个人改变他的习惯所组成，因此他们代表了环境和个人想要并愿意接受的事物。

No one can change the law of hypnotic rhythm any more than one can change the law of gravity, but everyone can change himself. Remember, therefore, in all the discussion of this subject that all human relationships are made and maintained by the habits of the individuals related.

没有人可以改变催眠节律，就像没有人可以改变万有引力一样，但是每个人都可以改变自己。因此，请记住，在所有关于这个主题的讨论中，所有的人际关系都是由相关个体的习惯建立和维持的。

“No one can change the law of hypnotic rhythm any more than one can change the law of gravity, but everyone can change himself.”

“没有人可以改变催眠节律，就像没有人可以改变万有引力一样，但是每个人都可以改变自己。”

Have you ever tried to change someone else and only been frustrated when you realized you were not in control and therefore not succeeding?

你是否曾经试图改变别人，但是当你意识到自己无法控制因而无法成功时，你感到沮丧？

The law of hypnotic rhythm plays only the part of solidifying the factors which constitute human relationships, but it does not create those factors. Before we go further with the discussion of human relationships, I want you to get a clear understanding of the subconscious mind.

催眠律只起到固化构成人际关系的因素的作用，并不产生这些因素。在我们进一步讨论人际关系之前，我希望你们对潜意识有一个清晰的了解。

The term “subconscious mind” represents a hypothetical physical organ which has no actual existence. The mind of man consists of universal energy (some call it Infinite Intelligence) which the individual receives, appropriates, and organizes in definite thought forms through the network of intricate physical apparatus known as a brain.

“潜意识”这个术语代表了一个假想的没有实际存在的物理器官。人类的心智由普遍的能量(有人称之为无限的智慧)组成，个体通过被称为大脑的复杂的物理装置网络，接收、占有并以明确的思想形式组织。

These thought forms are replicas of various stimuli which reach the brain through the five commonly known physical senses and the sixth sense, which is not so well known. When any form of stimuli reaches the brain and takes the definite shape of thought, it is classified and stored away in a group of the brain cells known as the memory group.

这些思维形式是各种刺激的复制品，这些刺激物通过五种常见的物理感官和第六感到达大脑，而第六感并不为人所知。当任何形式的刺激到达大脑并形成明确的思维形态时，它被分类并储存在一组被称为记忆组的脑细胞中。

All thoughts of a similar nature are stored together so that the bringing forth of one leads to easy contact with all its associates. The system is very similar to the modern office filing cabinet, and it is operated in a similar manner.

所有类似性质的思想都被储存在一起，以便一个人的提出能够导致与其所有同伴的容易接触。该系统非常类似于现代办公室文件柜，并以类似的方式操作。

The thought impressions with which one mixes the greatest amount of emotion (or feeling) are the dominating factors of the brain because they are always near the surface— at the top of the filing system, so to speak—where they spring into action voluntarily, the moment an individual neglects to exercise self-discipline. These emotion-laden thoughts are so powerful they often cause an individual to rush into action and indulge in deeds which have not been submitted to or approved by his reasoning faculty. These emotional outbursts usually destroy harmony in all human relationships. The brain often brings together combinations of emotional feeling so powerful they completely set aside the control of the reasoning faculty. On all such occasions human relationships are apt to be lacking in harmony.

将最大量的情绪(或感觉)混合在一起的思想印象是大脑的主导因素，因为它们总是接近表面，也就是说，在归档系统的顶部，当个体忽视自律时，它们就会自动开始行动。这些充满感情的想法是如此强大，以至于常常会导致一个人仓促行动，沉迷于那些没有被他的推理能力所接受或认可的行为。这些情绪的爆发通常会破坏所有人类关系的和谐。大脑经常将强烈的情感组合在一起，以至于完全放弃了对推理能力的控制。在所有这些情况下，人际关系往往缺乏和谐。

Through the operation of the sixth sense, the brain of a human being may contact the filing cabinet of other brains and inspect at will whatever thought impressions are on file there. The condition under which one person may contact and inspect the filing cabinet of another person’s brain is generally known as harmony, but you may better understand what is meant if I say brains attuned to the same rate of thought vibrations can easily and quickly exercise the privilege of entering and inspecting each other’s filing cabinets of thoughts.

通过第六感的运作，人类的大脑可以与其他大脑的文件柜联系，并随意检查文件中的任何想法印象。一个人可以接触和检查另一个人的大脑文件柜的情况通常被称为和谐，但是如果我说与同样的思想振动频率协调的大脑可以轻松快速地行使进入和检查彼此的思想文件柜的特权，你可能会更好地理解这意味着什么。

In addition to receiving organized thoughts from the filing cabinets of other brains through the sixth sense, one can, through this same physical organ, contact and receive information from the universal storehouse known as Infinite Intelligence.

除了通过第六感从其他大脑的文件柜接收有组织的思想之外，人们还可以通过这个同样的物理器官，接触并接收来自被称为无限智慧的宇宙仓库的信息。

All information reaching one’s brain through the sixth sense comes from sources not easily isolated or traced; therefore, this sort of information is generally believed to come from one’s subconscious mind. The sixth sense is the organ of the brain through which one receives all information, all knowledge, all thought impressions which do not come through one or more of the five physical senses.

所有通过第六感到达大脑的信息都来自于不容易分离或追踪的来源; 因此，这种信息通常被认为来自于一个人的潜意识。第六感是大脑的器官，人们通过它接收所有的信息、所有的知识、所有的思想印象，而这些印象并不是通过一种或多种物理感官来获得的。

Now that you understand how the mind operates, you will more easily understand how and why people come to grief through improper human relationships. You will also understand how human relationship may be made to yield riches in their highest form, riches in material, mental, and spiritual estates.

现在你明白了心灵是如何运作的，你就会更容易理解人们是如何以及为什么会因为不正当的人际关系而遭遇不幸。你们也会理解人类关系是如何以最高的形式产生财富的---- 物质财富、精神财富和精神财富。

Moreover, you will understand there can never be happiness except through understanding and application of the right principles of human relationships. You will understand, too, that no individual is an entity unto himself, that completeness of mind can be attained only by harmony of purpose and deed between two or more minds. You will understand why every human being should, of his own choice, become his brother’s keeper in fact as well as in theory.

此外，你会明白，除非通过理解和应用正确的人际关系原则，否则永远不会有幸福。你们也会明白，没有人是自己的实体，只有通过两个或两个以上的头脑之间目的和行动的和谐，才能达到头脑的完整。你会明白为什么每个人都应该，按照他自己的选择，在事实上和理论上成为他兄弟的守护者。

Q What you say may be true, but I still insist that you have me beyond safe depths of thought. Let us get back nearer to the shore, where I can wade in familiar water. We shall go out into the deeper water after we learn to swim well. We started out to discuss the subject of how to profit by adversity, but it seems we have drifted somewhat afield from that subject.

问: 你说的也许是真的，但是我仍然坚持认为你已经超越了我安全的思想深度。让我们回到岸边，在那里我可以涉过熟悉的水。在我们学会游泳之后，我们将到更深的水里去。我们开始讨论如何从逆境中获利的问题，但似乎我们已经偏离了这个主题。

A We have detoured, but we have not drifted. The Devil never drifts. The detour was necessary in order that you might be prepared to understand the most important part of this entire interview.

A 我们绕了路，但没有漂流。魔鬼从不漂泊。为了让你准备好理解整个面试中最重要的部分，绕道是必要的。

We are now ready to get back to the discussion of the subject of adversity. Inasmuch as most adversities grow out of improper relationships between people, it seems important to understand how people may become properly related.

我们现在准备回到关于逆境的讨论上来。由于大多数不幸都是由人与人之间不正当的关系造成的，因此了解人们如何能够正确地建立关系似乎很重要。

Naturally the question arises as to what is a proper relationship between people? The answer is that the proper relationship is one that brings to all connected with it, or affected by it, some form of benefit.

自然而然，问题就来了: 人与人之间的正当关系是什么？答案是，正确的关系是一种给所有与之相关或受其影响的人带来某种形式利益的关系。

“The proper relationship is one that brings to all connected with it, or affected by it, some form of benefit.”

正确的关系是给所有与之相关或受其影响的人带来某种形式利益的关系

Take a moment to inventory your relationships, at home, at work, and at play. List the relationships that seem in need of improvement and keep them in your mind as you continue reading.

花点时间盘点一下你的人际关系，无论是在家里，在工作中，还是在娱乐中。列出那些看起来需要改进的关系，并且在你继续阅读的时候把它们记在脑子里。

Q What, then, is an improper relationship?

问: 那么，什么是不正当的关系？

A Any relationship between people which damages anyone or brings any form of misery or unhappiness to any of the individuals.

人与人之间的任何关系，如果伤害了任何人，或给任何个人带来任何形式的痛苦或不幸。

Q How can improper relationships be corrected?

问: 如何纠正不正当的关系？

A By change of mind of the person causing the improper relationship, or by changing the persons to the relationship. Some minds harmonize naturally while others just as naturally clash. Successful human relationships, to endure as such, must be formed of minds that naturally harmonize, quite aside from the question of having common interests as a means of bringing them into harmony.

通过改变引起不正当关系的人的想法，或者通过改变人的关系。有些思想天生和谐，而有些思想天生冲突。成功的人际关系要持续下去，就必须由自然地协调的思想构成，而不是把拥有共同利益作为使它们和谐相处的手段的问题。

When you speak of business leaders who succeed because “they know how to pick men,” you might more correctly say they succeed because they know how to associate minds which harmonize naturally. Knowing how to pick people successfully for any definite purpose in life is based upon ability to recognize the types of people whose minds naturally harmonize.

当你说商业领袖成功是因为“他们知道如何挑选男人”时，你可能更正确地说他们成功是因为他们知道如何将思想自然地联系起来。知道如何为生活中的任何明确目标成功地挑选人，是基于能够识别那些思想天生和谐的人的能力。

Remember Hill’s definition of the Master Mind: “harmonious coordination of two or more minds working to a definite end.”

记住希尔对大师头脑的定义: “两个或两个以上的头脑协调工作，达到一个明确的目的。”

Q Stay focused on adversity, if you will. If there are possible benefits to be found through adversity, name some of them.

如果你愿意的话，把注意力集中在逆境上。如果在逆境中可以找到一些好处，列举出来。

A Adversity relieves people of vanity and egotism. It discourages selfishness by proving that no one can succeed without the cooperation of others.

逆境能使人摆脱虚荣和自负。它通过证明没有人能够在没有他人合作的情况下取得成功来阻止自私自利。

Adversity forces an individual to test his mental, physical, and spiritual strength; it thus brings him face to face with his weaknesses and gives him the opportunity to bridge them.

逆境迫使一个人去考验他的精神、身体和精神力量; 因此，逆境让他直面自己的弱点，并给他弥合这些弱点的机会。

Adversity forces one to seek ways and means to definite ends by meditation and introspective thought. This often leads to the discovery and use of the sixth sense through which one may communicate with Infinite Intelligence.

逆境迫使人们通过冥想和内省的思考来寻找达到目的的方法和途径。这通常导致了第六感的发现和使用，人们可以通过第六感与无限智慧交流。

Adversity forces one to recognize the need for intelligence not available except from sources outside of one’s own mind.

逆境迫使一个人认识到智力的必要性，这种必要性除了来自自己头脑之外的来源之外是无法获得的。

Adversity breaks old habits of thought and gives one an opportunity to form new habits; therefore, it may serve to break the hold of hypnotic rhythm and change its operation from negative to positive ends.

逆境可以打破旧的思维习惯，给人一个机会形成新的习惯; 因此，逆境可以打破催眠的节奏，将其运作从消极转向积极。

Q What is the greatest benefit one may receive through adversity?

问: 一个人在逆境中能得到的最大好处是什么？

A The greatest benefit of adversity is that it may, and generally does, force one to change one’s thought-habits, thus breaking and redirecting the force of hypnotic rhythm.

A 逆境的最大好处是，它可以，而且通常确实迫使一个人改变自己的思维习惯，从而打破和重新引导催眠节奏的力量。

Q In other words, failure always is a blessing when it forces one to acquire knowledge or to build habits that lead to the achievement of one’s major purpose in life. Is that correct?

换句话说，当失败迫使一个人获得知识或养成习惯，从而实现人生的主要目标时，失败总是一种祝福。是这样吗？

A Yes, and something more! Failure is a blessing when it forces one to depend less upon material forces and more upon spiritual forces.

A 是的，还有更多！当失败迫使一个人减少对物质力量的依赖而更多地依赖于灵性力量时，它就是一种祝福。

Many human beings discover their “other selves,” the forces which operate through the power of thought, only after some catastrophe deprives them of the full and free use of their physical bodies. When a man can no longer use his hands and his feet, he usually begins to use his brain; thus he puts himself in the way of discovering the power of his own mind.

许多人发现了他们的“其他自我” ，这种力量通过思想的力量运作，只有在一些灾难剥夺了他们充分和自由地使用他们的肉体之后。当一个人不能再使用他的手和脚时，他通常开始使用他的大脑，这样他就把自己置于发现自己思想力量的道路上。

The Devil brings in the “other self” here, revealing how we can use our power of thought and our “other selves” to discover our true power and major purpose.

魔鬼把“另一个自我”带到这里，揭示我们如何运用我们的思想力量和“另一个自我”来发现我们真正的力量和主要目的。

Q What benefits may be derived from the loss of material things—money, for example?

问: 失去物质上的东西ーー例如，金钱ーー会带来什么好处？

A The loss of material things may teach many needed lessons, none greater, however, than the truth that man has control over nothing and has no assurance of the permanent use of anything except his own power of thought.

失去物质的东西可以教会我们许多必要的教训，但没有什么比这样一个事实更重要了: 人无法控制任何东西，除了他自己的思想力量之外，他无法保证永久地使用任何东西。

Q I wonder if this is not the greatest benefit available through adversity?

问: 我想知道这是否是逆境带来的最大好处？

A No, the greatest potential benefit of any circumstance which causes one to make a fresh start is that it provides an opportunity to break the grip of hypnotic rhythm and set up a new set of thought-habits. New habits offer the only way out for people who fail. Most people who escape from the negative to the positive operation of the law of hypnotic rhythm do so only because of some form of adversity which forces them to change their thought-habits.

答案是否定的，任何环境促使一个人重新开始的最大潜在好处是，它提供了一个打破催眠节奏的机会，并建立一套新的思维习惯。新的习惯为失败者提供了唯一的出路。大多数人之所以从消极逃避到积极运作的催眠律，只是因为某种形式的逆境迫使他们改变思维习惯。

Q Isn’t adversity apt to break one’s self-reliance and cause one to give up hope?

难道逆境不会打破一个人的自力更生，使他放弃希望吗？

A It has that effect on those whose will power is weak through long established habits of drifting. It has the opposite effect on those who have not been weakened through drifting. The non-drifter meets with temporary defeat and failure, but his reaction to all forms of adversity is positive. He fights instead of giving up, and usually wins.

A 它对那些由于长期形成的漂泊习惯而意志力薄弱的人有这种效果。对于那些没有因漂泊而被削弱的人来说，它有着相反的效果。非漂流者会遭遇暂时的失败和失败，但他对各种形式的逆境的反应是积极的。他不是放弃，而是战斗，通常都会赢。

Life gives no one immunity against adversity, but life gives to everyone the power of positive thought, which is sufficient to master all circumstances of adversity and convert them into benefits. The individual is left with the privilege of using or neglecting to use his prerogative right to think his way through all adversities. Every individual is forced either to use his thought power for the attainment of definite, positive ends, or by neglect or design use this power for the attainment of negative ends. There can be no compromise, no refusal to use the mind.

生活没有给予任何人对逆境的免疫力，但生活给予每个人积极思想的力量，这足以掌握所有逆境的情况，并将其转化为利益。个人被赋予使用或忽略使用他的特权来思考一切逆境的方式。每个人要么被迫使用他的思想力量来达到明确的、积极的目的，要么被忽视或故意使用这种力量来达到消极的目的。没有妥协，没有拒绝使用头脑。

The law of hypnotic rhythm forces every individual to give some degree of use, either negative or positive, to his mind, but it does not influence the individual as to which use he will make of his mind.

催眠节奏法则迫使每个人在某种程度上对自己的思想有所利用，无论是消极的还是积极的，但它不影响个人对自己思想的利用。

“The non-drifter meets with temporary defeat and failure, but his reaction to all forms of adversity is positive. He fights instead of giving up, and usually wins.”

“非漂流者会遭遇暂时的失败和失败，但他对所有形式的逆境的反应都是积极的。他不是放弃，而是战斗，通常都会赢。”

Do you remember a time when you felt like giving up . . . but didn’t? My co-author and I expand this concept in our book Three Feet from Gold, with stories of perseverance and never giving up from over thirty-five of today’s top leaders, non-drifters of our time!

你还记得有一次你想放弃... 但是没有吗？我和我的合著者在我们的书《金子三尺》中扩展了这个概念，讲述了当今35位最高领导人——我们这个时代的非流浪者——坚持不懈、永不放弃的故事！

Q Am I to understand from what you say that every adversity is a blessing?

问: 我是否可以从你所说的话中理解，每一次逆境都是一次祝福？

A No, I did not say that. I said there is the seed of an equivalent advantage in every adversity. I did not say there was the full-blown flower of advantage, just the seed. Usually the seed consists of some form of knowledge, some idea or plan, or some opportunity which would not have been available except through the change of thought-habits forced by the adversity.

A 不，我没有那样说。我说过，在每一个逆境中都有一个同等优势的种子。我并没有说有全盛的花的优势，只是种子。通常，种子包括某种形式的知识、某种想法或计划，或某种机会，这些机会除非在逆境中被迫改变思维习惯，否则是不可能得到的。

Q Are those all the benefits available to human beings through failure?

问: 这些是人类通过失败获得的所有好处吗？

A No, failure is used by nature as a common language in which she chastises people when they neglect to adapt themselves to her laws.

不，失败是大自然使用的一种共同语言，在这种语言中，她谴责那些忽视适应她的法律的人。

For example, the world war was man-made and destructive. Nature planted in the circumstances of the war the seed of an equivalent reprimand in the form of a world depression. The depression was inevitable and inescapable. It followed the war as naturally as day follows night and by the operation of the self-same law, the law of hypnotic rhythm.

例如，世界大战是人为的和具有破坏性的。大自然在战争的环境中播下了以世界大萧条为形式的同等谴责的种子。经济萧条是不可避免的。它遵循着战争就像白天遵循着黑夜一样自然，遵循着自我同一的法则，催眠律。

Q Am I to understand that the law of hypnotic rhythm is the same as that which Ralph Waldo Emerson called the law of compensation?

问: 我是否能够理解催眠节律与拉尔夫·沃尔多·爱默生所称的补偿律是一样的？

A The law of hypnotic rhythm is the law of compensation. It is the power with which nature balances negative and positive forces throughout the universes, in all forms of energy, in all forms of matter, and in all human relationships.

A 催眠律就是补偿律。它是大自然在整个宇宙中，在所有形式的能量中，在所有形式的物质中，以及在所有人类关系中，平衡负面和正面力量的力量。

Q Does the law of hypnotic rhythm operate quickly in all instances? For example, does this law immediately bless one with the benefits of positive application of thoughts, or curse one immediately with the results of negative thoughts?

问: 催眠节律是否在所有情况下都很快起作用？例如，这个法则是否会立即祝福一个人积极应用思想的好处，还是立即诅咒一个人消极思想的结果？

A The law operates definitely but not always swiftly. Both the benefits and the penalties incurred through the law by individuals may be harvested by others, either before or after their death.

A 法律肯定会发挥作用，但不总是迅速发挥作用。个人通过法律获得的利益和受到的惩罚可以由他人在其死亡之前或之后获得。

Observe how this law works by forcing upon one generation of people the effects of both the sins and the virtues of preceding generations. In the operation of all of nature’s laws, the fourth dimension, time, is an inexorable factor. The length of time consumed by nature in the relation of effects to their causes depends, in every instance, on the circumstances at hand. Nature grows a pumpkin in three months. A good size oak tree requires a hundred years. She converts a hen’s egg into a chicken in four weeks, but she requires nine months to convert the egg of a human being into an individual.

观察这个法律是如何运作的，通过强迫一代人接受上一代人的罪恶和美德的影响。在所有自然法则的运作中，第四维度，时间，是一个不可阻挡的因素。在任何情况下，大自然所消耗的时间在结果与其原因之间的关系上取决于当时的情况。大自然三个月就会长出一个南瓜。一棵大小合适的橡树需要一百年的时间。她在四个星期内把一只母鸡的蛋变成一只鸡，但是她需要九个月的时间来把一个人的蛋变成一个个体。

“Life gives no one immunity against adversity, but life gives to everyone the power of positive thought, which is sufficient to master all circumstances of adversity and convert them into benefits.”

“生活并不能使任何人免于逆境，但生活赋予每个人积极思想的力量，这种力量足以掌握逆境中的所有情况，并将其转化为利益。”

Has nature created the current economic turmoil to allow us once again to convert our own personal adversities into benefits?

大自然是否创造了当前的经济动荡，让我们再次将个人逆境转化为利益？





Chapter Twelve

ENVIRONMENT, TIME, HARMONY, AND CAUTION

第十二章环境，时间，和谐和谨慎

Q I NOW HAVE A BETTER UNDERSTANDING of the potentialities of adversity and failure. You may go ahead, now, with your description of the next of the seven principles. What is your next principle?

现在我对逆境和失败的潜力有了更好的理解。现在，你可以继续描述下一个七项原则。你的下一个原则是什么？

A The next principle is environmental influence.

A 下一个原则是环境影响。

Q Go ahead and describe the working principle of environmental influences as a determining factor in human destinies.

请继续描述环境影响作为人类命运决定因素的工作原理。

A Environment consists of all the mental, spiritual, and physical forces which affect and influence human beings.

环境包括一切影响和影响人类的精神、精神和物理力量。

Q What connection, if any, is there between environmental influences and hypnotic rhythm?

问: 环境影响和催眠节律之间有什么联系，如果有的话？

A Hypnotic rhythm solidifies and makes permanent the thought-habits of human beings. Thought-habits are stimulated by environmental influences. In other words, the material on which thoughts are fed comes from one’s environment. Thought-habits are made permanent by hypnotic rhythm.

一种催眠的节奏巩固并使人类的思维习惯永久化。思维习惯受到环境影响的刺激。换句话说，思想所依赖的材料来自于一个人所处的环境。思维习惯是通过催眠的节奏而永久形成的。

Q What is the most important part of one’s environment, the part which determines, more than all others, whether an individual makes positive or negative use of his mind?

问: 一个人的环境中最重要的部分是什么? 它比其他部分更能决定一个人的思想是积极的还是消极的？

A The most important part of one’s environment is that created by his association with others. All people absorb and take over, either consciously or unconsciously, the thought-habits of those with whom they associate closely.

一个人的环境中最重要的部分是他与他人的联系所创造的。所有的人都会有意识或无意识地吸收和接管那些与他们有密切联系的人的思维习惯。

Q Do you mean by this that constant association with a person whose thought-habits are negative influences one to form negative thought-habits?

问: 你的意思是说，与一个思维习惯消极的人经常联系会影响一个人形成消极的思维习惯吗？

A Yes, the law of hypnotic rhythm forces every human being to form thought-habits which harmonize with the dominating influences of his environment, particularly that part of his environment created by his association with other minds.

答: 是的，催眠节奏法则迫使每个人形成思维习惯，这些思维习惯与他所处环境的主要影响相协调，尤其是与他人的联想所创造的那部分环境。

Q Then it is important that one select one’s close associates with great care?

那么，重要的是要小心选择自己的亲密伙伴？

A Yes, one’s intimate associates should be chosen with as much care as one chooses the food with which he feeds his body, with the object always of associating with people whose dominating thoughts are positive, friendly, and harmonious.

答: 是的，一个人的亲密伙伴应该像选择他用来喂养身体的食物一样小心谨慎，选择的目标总是与那些主导思想是积极、友好、和谐的人交往。

Q Which class of associates has the greatest influence upon one?

哪一类律师对一个人的影响最大？

A One’s partner in marriage and in the home and one’s associates in his occupation. After that come close friends and acquaintances. Casual acquaintances and strangers have but little influence on one.

一个人在婚姻和家庭中的伴侣以及在其职业中的同事。在那之后就是亲密的朋友和熟人。一般的熟人和陌生人对一个人的影响很小。

“The material on which thoughts are fed come from one’s environment. Thought-habits are made permanent by hypnotic rhythm.”

思维所依赖的材料来自环境。思维习惯是通过催眠节律而永久形成的

Have you ever felt your attitude or mood become negative just by being in the presence of someone negative? Was it your spouse, child, or business partner? Hill suggests that you need to interject thoughts that are positive, friendly, and harmonious not only to counteract those negative thoughts but also to influence that person into a more positive space. If it is your business partner, evaluate if the relationship is one you want to save . . . or make the decision to move away from the partner’s negativity.

你有没有觉得你的态度或情绪因为面对某个消极的人而变得消极？是你的配偶、孩子还是生意伙伴？希尔建议，你需要插入积极、友好、和谐的想法，这不仅可以抵消消极的想法，还可以影响那个人进入一个更积极的空间。如果是你的生意伙伴，评估一下这段关系是否是你想挽救的... ... 或者决定远离对方的消极态度。

Q Why does one’s partner in marriage have so great an influence upon one’s mind?

问: 为什么婚姻中的伴侣对一个人的思想有如此大的影响？

A Because the relationship of marriage brings people under the influence of spiritual forces of such weight that they become dominating forces of the mind.

因为婚姻的关系使人们受到精神力量的影响，这种精神力量的重量使他们成为支配心灵的力量。

Q How may environmental influences be used to break the grip of hypnotic rhythm?

问: 如何利用环境影响来打破催眠的节奏？

A All influences which establish thought-habits are given permanency through the law of hypnotic rhythm. One may change the influences of his environment so that the dominating influences are either positive or negative, and the law of hypnotic rhythm will make them permanent, unless they are changed through one’s habits of thought.

一切建立思维习惯的影响都是通过催眠节律而持久的。一个人可以改变他周围环境的影响，使得主导的影响要么是积极的，要么是消极的，催眠节律将使这些影响永久存在，除非通过一个人的思维习惯改变它们。

Q Stating this truth in another way, one may submit himself to any environmental influence desired, whether positive or negative, and the law of hypnotic rhythm will make the influence permanent when it assumes the magnitude of thought-habit. Is that the way the law works?

用另一种方式来说明这个事实，一个人可以服从任何环境的影响，无论是积极的还是消极的，催眠节奏法则将使这种影响永久性当它假定思想习惯的重要性。法律就是这么运作的吗？

A That is correct. Be careful of all forces which inspire thought; those are the forces which constitute environment and determine the nature of one’s earthly destiny.

A 是的。小心所有激发思想的力量; 这些力量构成了环境并决定了一个人尘世命运的本质。

Q What class of people controls their environmental influences?

什么阶层的人控制他们的环境影响？

A The non-drifters. All who are victims of the habit of drifting forfeit their power to choose their own environment. They become the victims of every negative influence of their environment.

A 非流浪者。所有习惯于漂流的受害者丧失了选择自己环境的能力。他们成为所处环境的各种负面影响的受害者。

Q Is there no way out for the drifter? Is there no method by which he may submit himself to the influence of a positive environment?

流浪汉没有出路吗？难道没有一种方法可以使他屈服于积极环境的影响吗？

A Yes, there is a way out for drifters. They can stop drifting, take possession of their own minds, and choose an environment which inspires positive thought. This they may accomplish through definiteness of purpose.

A 是的，流浪者是有出路的。他们可以停止漂泊，拥有自己的思想，选择一个能激发积极思想的环境。他们可以通过明确目标来实现这一点。

Q Is that all there is to the act of eliminating the habit of drifting? Is the habit only a state of mind?

问: 这就是消除漂泊习惯的全部行为吗？习惯只是一种精神状态吗？

A Drifting is nothing but a negative state of mind, a state of mind conspicuous by its emptiness of purpose.

漂泊不过是一种消极的精神状态，一种因其目的的空虚而显著的精神状态。

Q What effective procedure may one follow in establishing an environment most helpful in developing and maintaining positive thought-habits?

在建立一个对培养和保持积极的思维习惯最有帮助的环境时，应该遵循哪些有效的步骤？

A The most effective of all environments is that which may be created by a friendly alliance of a group of people who will obligate themselves to assist one another in achieving the object of some definite purpose. This sort of an alliance is known as a Master Mind. Through its operation one may associate himself with carefully chosen individuals each of whom brings to the alliance some knowledge, experience, education, plan, or idea suited to his needs in carrying out the object of his definite purpose.

所有环境中最有效的环境是由一群人组成的友好联盟所创造的环境，这些人有义务互相帮助，以达到某种明确的目的。这种联盟被称为头脑大师。通过它的运作，人们可以把自己与精心挑选的个人联系起来，每个人都为联盟带来一些知识、经验、教育、计划或想法，以适合自己实现其明确目标的需要。

The most successful leaders in all walks of life avail themselves of this sort of made-to-order environmental influence. Outstanding achievement is impossible without the friendly cooperation of others. Stating the truth in another way, successful people must control their environment, thereby insuring themselves against the influence of a negative environment.

各行各业中最成功的领导者都利用这种定制的环境影响。没有他人的友好合作，卓越的成就是不可能的。换句话说，成功人士必须控制他们的环境，从而使自己免受消极环境的影响。

Q What of people whose duty to relatives makes it impossible for them to avoid the influence of a negative environment?

问: 那些对亲属负有责任，不可能避免负面环境影响的人呢？

A No human being owes another any degree of duty which robs him of his privilege of building his thought-habits in a positive environment. On the other hand, every human being is duty bound to himself to remove from his environment every influence which even remotely tends to develop negative thought-habits.

任何人都不欠别人任何程度的责任，这种责任剥夺了他在积极的环境中养成思维习惯的特权。另一方面，每个人都有责任从自己的环境中消除一切影响，哪怕是稍微有可能形成消极的思维习惯。

Q Isn’t this a cold-blooded philosophy?

问: 这不是一种冷血的哲学吗？

A Only the strong survive. No one can be strong without removing himself from all influences which develop negative thought-habits. Negative thought-habits result in the loss of the privilege of self-determination, no matter what or who may cause those habits. Positive thought-habits may be controlled by the individual and made to serve his aims and purposes. Negative thought-habits control the individual and deprive him of the privilege of self-determination.

只有强者才能生存。没有人能够强大，除非他能够摆脱所有导致消极思想习惯的影响。消极的思想习惯会导致失去自决的特权，不管是什么或谁可能导致这些习惯。积极的思维习惯可以被个人所控制，并且服务于他的目标和目的。消极的思想习惯控制着个人，剥夺了他作为自决的特权。

Q I deduce from all you have said that those who control the environmental influences out of which their thought habits are built are masters of their earthly destinies and that all others are mastered by earthly destinies. Is that stating the matter correctly?

问: 我从你们所说的一切推断出，那些控制着环境影响的人，他们的思维习惯就是建立在这种环境影响之上的，他们是自己地球上命运的主人，而其他所有人都被地球上的命运所主宰。这样说对吗？

A Perfectly stated.

一个完美的陈述。

Q What establishes one’s thought-habits?

问: 是什么决定了一个人的思维习惯？

A All habits are established because of inherent or acquired desires, or motives. That is, habits are begun as the result of some form of definite desire.

所有的习惯都是因为内在或后天的欲望或动机而形成的。也就是说，习惯是作为某种形式的明确欲望的结果而开始的。

Q What takes place in the physical brain while one is forming thought-habits?

当一个人形成思维习惯时，他的物理大脑中发生了什么？

A Desires are organized impulses of energy called thoughts. Desires that are mixed with emotional feeling magnetize the brain cells in which they are stored and prepare those cells to be taken over and directed by the law of hypnotic rhythm. When any thought appears in the brain or is created there, and is mixed with keen emotional feeling of desire, the law of hypnotic rhythm begins, at once, to translate it into its physical counterpart. Dominating thoughts, which are acted upon first by the law of hypnotic rhythm, are those with which are mixed the strongest desires and the most intense feelings. Thought-habits are established by the repetition of the same thoughts.

欲望是被称为思想的有组织的能量冲动。混合着情感的欲望磁化了储存它们的脑细胞，并准备这些细胞被催眠节律控制和引导。当任何想法出现在大脑中或在那里被创造出来，并与强烈的欲望情感混合在一起时，催眠律立即开始将其转化为身体上的对应物。支配性的思想，是那些混合着最强烈的欲望和最强烈的情感的思想，它们首先被催眠的节奏法则所支配。思维习惯是通过重复同样的思想而形成的。

Q What are the most impelling basic motives or desires which inspire thought action?

什么是最有感染力的基本动机或欲望，激发思想行动？

A The ten most common motives, those which inspire most of one’s thought-action, are these:

A 最常见的十个动机，激发了人们大部分的思想和行动，是:

• The desire for sex expression and love

•对性表达和爱的渴望

• The desire for physical food

•对物质食物的渴望

• The desire for spiritual, mental, and physical self-expression

•对精神、心理和身体自我表达的渴望

• The desire for perpetuation of life after death

•对死后生命永存的渴望

• The desire for power over others

•对权力凌驾于他人之上的渴望

• The desire for material wealth

•对物质财富的渴望

• The desire for knowledge

•对知识的渴望

• The desire to imitate others

•模仿他人的欲望

• The desire to excel others

•想要超越他人的欲望

• The seven basic fears

•七种基本恐惧

These are the dominating motives which inspire the majority of all human endeavors.

这些都是激发人类大多数努力的主要动机。

Q What about the negative desires such as greed, envy, avarice, jealousy, anger? Are these not expressed more often than any of the positive desires?

那些消极的欲望如贪婪、嫉妒、贪婪、嫉妒、愤怒呢？难道这些不是比任何积极的愿望表达得更频繁吗？

A All negative desires are nothing but frustrations of positive desires. They are inspired by some form of defeat, failure, or neglect by human beings to adapt themselves to nature’s laws in a positive way.

所有消极的欲望只不过是积极欲望的挫折。他们受到人类某种形式的失败、失败或忽视的启发，以积极的方式使自己适应自然法则。

Q That’s a new slant on the subject of negative thoughts. If I correctly understand what you have said, all negative thoughts are inspired by one’s neglect or failure to adapt oneself harmoniously to nature’s laws. Is that correct?

问: 这是关于消极思想的一个新的倾向。如果我正确地理解了你所说的话，所有的消极思想都是由于一个人忽视或未能使自己和谐地适应自然规律而产生的。是这样吗？

A That is exactly correct. Nature will not tolerate idleness or vacuums of any sort. All space must be and is filled with something.

A 完全正确。大自然不会容忍任何形式的懒惰或空虚。所有的空间都必须充满某种东西。

Everything in existence, of both a physical and a spiritual nature, must be and is constantly in motion. The human brain is no exception. It was created to receive, organize, specialize, and express the power of thought. When the individual does not use the brain for the expression of positive, creative thoughts, nature fills the vacuum by forcing the brain to act upon negative thoughts.

一切存在的事物，包括物质的和精神的，都必须不断地运动。人类的大脑也不例外。它的创造是为了接受、组织、专门化和表达思想的力量。当个人没有使用大脑来表达积极的、创造性的想法时，大自然通过迫使大脑对消极的想法采取行动来填补真空。

There can be no idleness in the brain. Understand this principle and you will come into a new and important understanding of the part environmental influences take in the lives of human beings.

大脑中不可能有懒惰。理解这个原则，你就会对环境影响在人类生活中所起的作用有一个全新而重要的认识。

You will better understand, also, how the law of hypnotic rhythm operates, it being the law which keeps everything and everyone constantly moving through some form of expression of either negative or positive principles.

你也会更好地理解催眠律是如何运作的，催眠律就是让一切事物和每个人通过某种形式表达积极或消极的原则而不断移动的律。

“Nature will not tolerate idleness or vacuums of any sort. All space must be and is filled with something . . . When the individual does not use the brain for the expression of positive, creative thoughts, nature fills the vacuum by forcing the brain to act upon negative thoughts.”

“大自然不会容忍任何形式的懒惰或空虚。所有的空间都必须并且充满了某些东西... ... 当个体不用大脑来表达积极的、创造性的思想时，大自然就会通过迫使大脑对消极的思想采取行动来填补空白。”

I find this so true particularly when I think of children who have too much idle time on their hands. Don Green, CEO of the Napoleon Hill Foundation, remembers, “As young people we were constantly kept busy with the admonition that idleness was the devil’s workshop.” Interesting parallel, don’t you think?

当我想到那些有太多闲暇时间的孩子时，我发现这一点尤其正确。拿破仑 · 希尔基金会的首席执行官唐 · 格林回忆道: “年轻人总是告诫我们，懒惰是魔鬼的工作间，让我们忙得团团转。”有趣的类比，你不觉得吗？

Nature is not interested in morals as such. She is not interested in right and wrong. She is not interested in justice and injustice. She is interested only in forcing everything to express action according to its nature!

大自然对道德本身并不感兴趣。她对是非不感兴趣。她对正义和不公正不感兴趣。她感兴趣的只是迫使一切按照其本质来表达行动！

Q That is an enlightening interpretation of nature’s ways. To whom may I turn for corroboration of your claims?

问: 这是对自然规律的一种有启发性的解释。我可以向谁求证你的说法呢？

A To men of science, to the philosophers, to all accurate thinkers. Lastly, to the physical manifestations of nature herself.

A 献给科学家，献给哲学家，献给所有精确的思想家，最后，献给自然本身的物质表现。
