Nature has no such thing as dead matter. Every atom of matter is constantly in a state of motion. All energy is constantly in motion. There are no dead voids anywhere. Time and space are literally manifestations of motion of such swiftness that it cannot be measured by human beings.

自然界没有死物质这种东西。物质中的每个原子都在不断地处于运动状态。所有的能量都在不断地运动。任何地方都没有死亡的空隙。时间和空间从字面意义上来说就是快速运动的表现，人类是无法测量的。

Q Alas, one is forced to the conclusion, from what you say, that the sources of dependable knowledge are shockingly limited.

唉，人们不得不从你的话中得出这样的结论: 可靠的知识来源是极其有限的。

A The developed sources of knowledge are limited. Every normal adult human brain is a potential gateway to all the knowledge there is throughout the universes. Every normal adult brain has within its mechanism the possibility of direct communication with Infinite Intelligence, wherein exists all the knowledge that is or can ever be.

A 已开发的知识来源有限。每一个正常的成年人的大脑都是通向遍布宇宙的所有知识的潜在门户。每一个正常成年人的大脑都有可能与无限智慧进行直接交流，在这种交流中存在着所有现存的或可能存在的知识。

Q Your statement leads me to believe that human beings may become all they have attributed to what they call God. Is that what you mean?

问: 你的陈述让我相信，人类可能会成为他们所认为的上帝的一切。你是这个意思吗？

A Through the law of evolution the human brain is being perfected to communicate at will with Infinite Intelligence. The perfection will come through organized development of the brain, through its adaptation to nature’s laws. Time is the factor which will bring perfection.

通过进化的规律，人类的大脑正在完善，可以随意与无限智慧进行交流。完美将来自大脑的有组织的发展，通过它对自然规律的适应。时间是带来完美的因素。

Q What causes cycles of recurring events, such as epidemics of disease, business depressions, wars, and crime waves?

什么导致循环事件的周期性发生，比如疾病流行、商业萧条、战争和犯罪浪潮？

A All such epidemics in which great numbers of people are similarly affected are caused by the law of hypnotic rhythm, through which nature consolidates thoughts of a similar nature and causes those thoughts to be expressed through mass action.

所有这样的流行病，其中大量的人类受到类似的影响，都是由催眠节律引起的，通过催眠节律，大自然巩固了类似性质的思想，并使这些思想通过群体行动表达出来。

Q Then the Great Depression was put into motion because great numbers of people were influenced to release thoughts of fear. Is that correct?

问: 然后大萧条开始了，因为很多人受到影响，去释放恐惧的想法。是这样吗？

A Perfectly. Millions of people were endeavoring to get something for nothing, through stock gambling. When they suddenly discovered they had gotten nothing for something, they became frightened, rushed to their banks to draw out their balances, and the panic was on. Through mass thought of millions of minds, all thinking in terms of fear of poverty, the depression was prolonged over a period of years.

A 完美。数以百万计的人正在通过股票赌博，努力不劳而获。当他们突然发现他们没有得到任何东西，他们变得害怕，冲向他们的银行提取他们的余额，恐慌继续。通过对数以百万计的头脑的广泛思考，所有的头脑都以对贫穷的恐惧来思考，经济萧条延续了数年之久。

The current economic turmoil in the United States and throughout the world was put into motion in a similar fashion. Millions were endeavoring to get something for nothing, through real estate (no-money-down deals, sub-prime mortgages, and valuation bubbles) as well as the financial markets. When everything started to collapse, they became frightened and the panic was on once again. By changing the thoughts of these millions from fear back to focus on fundamentally sound financial principles, can we stabilize the economy? Napoleon Hill’s philosophy can show us the way. The choice is ours.

目前美国和全世界的经济动荡也是以类似的方式发生的。数百万人正在努力通过房地产(无首付交易、次级抵押贷款和估值泡沫)以及金融市场免费获得一些东西。当一切开始崩溃的时候，他们变得害怕起来，恐慌再次出现。通过将数百万人的思想从恐惧转回到关注基本健全的金融原则，我们能够稳定经济吗？拿破仑 · 希尔的哲学可以为我们指明道路。这是我们的选择。

Q From what you say, I deduce that nature consolidates the dominating thoughts of people and expresses these thoughts through some form of mass action, such as business depressions, business booms, and so on. Is that correct?

问: 根据你所说的，我推断大自然巩固了人们的主导思想，并通过某种形式的群体行动来表达这些思想，比如商业萧条、商业繁荣等等。是这样吗？

A You have the right idea.

A 你的想法是对的。

Q Let us now take up the next of the seven principles. Go ahead and describe it.

现在让我们接下来讨论七条原则中的下一条。请继续描述它。

A The next principle is time, the fourth dimension.

A 下一个原则是时间，第四个维度。

Q What relationship is there between time and the operation of the law of hypnotic rhythm?

时间与催眠节律的运作有什么关系？

A Time is the law of hypnotic rhythm. The lapse of time required to give permanency to thought-habits depends upon the object and the nature of the thoughts.

时间是催眠节律。使思维习惯持久所需的时间取决于思维的对象和性质。

Q But I understood you to say that the only enduring thing in nature is change. If that is true, then time is constantly changing, rearranging, and recombining all things, including one’s thought-habits. How, then, could the law of hypnotic rhythm give permanency to one’s thought-habits?

问: 但我明白你的意思，自然界唯一持久的东西就是变化。如果这是真的，那么时间就是在不断地变化，重新安排，重新组合所有的东西，包括一个人的思维习惯。那么，催眠节律怎么能使一个人的思维习惯永久化呢？

A Time divides all thought-habits into two classes, negative thoughts and positive thoughts. One’s individual thoughts are of course constantly changing and being recombined to suit the individual’s desires, but thoughts do not change from negative to positive or vice versa except through voluntary effort on the part of the individual.

时间把所有的思维习惯分为两类: 消极思维和积极思维。一个人的个人思想当然是不断变化和被重新组合以适应个人的欲望，但是思想不会从消极变为积极，反之亦然，除非通过个人的自愿努力。

Time penalizes the individual for all negative thoughts and rewards him for all positive thoughts, according to the nature and purpose of the thoughts. If one’s dominating thoughts are negative, time penalizes the individual by building in his mind the habit of negative thinking and then proceeds to solidify this habit into permanency every second of its existence. Positive thoughts are, likewise, woven by time into permanent habits. The term “permanency,” of course, refers to the natural life of the individual. In the strict sense of the term, nothing is permanent. Time converts thought-habits into what might be called permanency during the life of the individual.

根据思想的本质和目的，时间惩罚所有消极思想的个人，奖励所有积极思想的个人。如果一个人的主导思想是消极的，那么时间通过在他的头脑中建立消极思想的习惯来惩罚个人，然后开始将这个习惯固化为永久性的存在的每一秒。同样，积极的想法也会随着时间的流逝而变成永久的习惯。当然，“永久性”一词指的是个人的自然生命。严格意义上说，没有什么是永恒的。时间将思维习惯转化为个人一生中所谓的永久性。

Q Now I have a better understanding of how time works. What other characteristics has time in connection with the earthly destiny of human beings?

现在我对时间是如何运作的有了更好的理解。与人类的尘世命运有关的时间还有什么其他特征？

A Time is nature’s seasoning influence through which human experience may be ripened into wisdom. People are not born with wisdom, but they are born with the capacity to think, and they may, through the lapse of time, think their way into wisdom.

时间是自然的调味影响，通过它，人类的经验可以成熟为智慧。人并非生来就有智慧，但他们生来就有思考的能力，随着时间的推移，他们可以通过思考获得智慧。

“People are not born with wisdom, but they are born with the capacity to think, and they may, through the lapse of time, think their way into wisdom.”

“人不是生来就有智慧，而是生来就有思考的能力，随着时间的推移，他们可以通过思考获得智慧。”

I find this one of the most profound statements in this entire book. By using our ability to think and analyzing our experiences in life, whether successes or failures, we can gain wisdom. Can it actually be that simple?

我发现这是整本书中最深刻的陈述之一。通过运用我们思考和分析生活经历的能力，无论是成功还是失败，我们都可以获得智慧。事情真的能这么简单吗？

Q Do youths ever possess wisdom?

问: 年轻人有过智慧吗？

A Only in very elementary matters. Wisdom comes only through the lapse of time. It cannot be inherited and it cannot be imparted from one person to another except through the lapse of time.

A 只有在非常基本的事情上。智慧只有在时间的流逝中才会显现。它不能继承，也不能从一个人传给另一个人，除非经过时间的推移。

Q Does the lapse of time force an individual to acquire wisdom?

时间的流逝是否会迫使一个人获得智慧？

A No! Wisdom comes only to non-drifters who form positive thought-habits as a dominating force in their lives. Drifters and those whose dominating thoughts are negative never acquire wisdom except of a very elementary nature.

A 不！只有那些形成积极思想习惯并在生活中占据主导地位的非漂泊者才会有智慧。流浪者和那些占主导地位的思想是消极的人，除非具有非常基本的本性，否则他们永远不会获得智慧。

Q From what you say, I infer that time is the friend of the person who trains his mind to follow positive thought-habits and the enemy of the person who drifts into negative thought-habits. Is that correct?

从你所说的，我推断，时间是那些训练自己的思维去追随积极思维习惯的人的朋友，也是那些陷入消极思维习惯的人的敌人。是这样吗？

A That is precisely true. All people can be classified as drifters and non-drifters. Drifters are always at the mercy of the non-drifters, and time makes this relationship permanent.

A 那完全正确。所有的人都可以分为流浪者和非流浪者。流浪者总是受不流浪者的摆布，而时间使这种关系永久存在。

Q Do you mean that if I drift along through life, without definite aim or purpose, the non-drifter may become my master, and time only serves to give the non-drifter a stronger and more permanent grip upon me?

你的意思是说，如果我在生活中随波逐流，没有明确的目标或目的，非漂泊者可能会成为我的主人，而时间只会给予非漂泊者一个更强大和更持久的抓地力？

A That is stating the truth exactly.

A 那正在准确地陈述事实。

“Wisdom comes only to non-drifters who form positive thought-habits as a dominating force in their lives.”

“只有那些形成积极思维习惯的非漂泊者才有智慧，他们在生活中占据主导地位。”

Again I am forced to think about our children. With so much negativity around us due to terrorism and financial strife, what is going to be the long-term impact on our children? We must envelop our children in positive experiences in order to generate positive thoughts in their minds.

我不得不再一次为我们的孩子着想。恐怖主义和金融冲突给我们带来了如此多的负面影响，对我们的孩子将会产生什么样的长期影响？我们必须让我们的孩子身处积极的经历中，以便在他们的头脑中产生积极的想法。

Q What is wisdom?

什么是智慧？

A Wisdom is the ability to relate yourself to nature’s laws so as to make them serve you, and the ability to relate yourself to other people so as to gain their harmonious, willing cooperation in helping you to make life yield whatever you demand of it.

智慧就是将自己与自然法则联系起来，让它们为你服务的能力，以及将自己与他人联系起来，从而获得他们和谐、愿意合作的能力，帮助你让生活产生你所需要的任何东西。

Q Then accumulated knowledge is not wisdom?

那么积累的知识不就是智慧吗？

A Great heavens, no! If knowledge were wisdom, the achievements of science would not have been converted into implements of destruction.

天哪，不！如果知识是智慧，那么科学的成就就不会变成毁灭的工具。

Q What is needed to convert knowledge into wisdom?

问: 将知识转化为智慧需要什么？

A Time plus the desire for wisdom. Wisdom is never thrust upon one. It is acquired, if at all, by positive thinking, through voluntary effort!

时间加上对智慧的渴望。智慧永远不会强加于人。它是通过积极的思考，通过自愿的努力而获得的！

Q Is it safe for all people to have knowledge?

问: 所有人都有知识是安全的吗？

A It is never safe for anyone to have extensive knowledge without wisdom.

A 对任何人来说，没有智慧的博学永远不会安全。

Q What is the age at which most people who acquire wisdom begin to acquire it?

大多数获得智慧的人在什么年龄开始获得智慧？

A The majority of people who acquire wisdom do so after they have passed the age of forty. Prior to that time the majority of people are too busy gathering knowledge and organizing it into plans to spend any effort seeking wisdom.

大多数获得智慧的人都是在四十岁以后才获得智慧。在此之前，大多数人都忙于收集知识并将其组织成计划，而不是花费任何精力去寻求智慧。

Q What circumstance of life is most apt to lead one to acquire wisdom?

什么样的生活环境最容易使人获得智慧？

A Adversity and failure. These are nature’s universal languages through which she imparts wisdom to those who are ready to receive it.

逆境与失败。这些是大自然的宇宙语言，她通过这些语言将智慧传授给那些准备接受智慧的人。

Q Do adversity and failure always bring wisdom?

问: 逆境和失败总是带来智慧吗？

A No, only to those who are ready for wisdom and have voluntarily sought it.

答: 不，只有那些准备好接受智慧并自愿寻求智慧的人才可以。

Q What determines one’s readiness to receive wisdom?

是什么决定了一个人愿意接受智慧？

A Time and the nature of one’s thought-habits.

一个人思维习惯的时间和性质。

Q Is newly acquired knowledge the same as time-tested knowledge?

新获得的知识和经过时间考验的知识是一样的吗？

A No, knowledge tested through the lapse of time always is superior to that which has been newly acquired. Time gives to knowledge definiteness in both quality and quantity, and dependability. One never can be sure of knowledge that has not been tested.

不，通过时间的流逝测试的知识总是优于新学到的知识。时间赋予知识质量和数量的确定性和可靠性。没有经过检验的知识是永远无法确定的。

Q What is dependable knowledge?

什么是可靠的知识？

A It is knowledge which harmonizes with natural law, which means that it is based upon positive thought.

它是与自然规律相协调的知识，这意味着它是建立在积极的思想之上的。

Q Does time modify and alter the values of knowledge?

时间会改变和改变知识的价值吗？

A Yes, time modifies and alters all values. That which is accurate knowledge today may become null and void tomorrow because of time’s rearrangement of facts and values. Time modifies all human relationships for better or for worse, depending upon the policy through which people relate themselves to one another.

答: 是的，时间会修改和改变所有的价值观。由于时间对事实和价值的重新安排，今天正确的知识明天可能会变得无效。时间改变了所有的人际关系，无论是好是坏，这取决于人们相互联系的政策。

In the realm of thought there is a time when it is proper to sow the seeds of thought, and there is a proper time to reap the harvest of those thoughts, the same as there is a time to sow and a time to reap from the soil of the earth. Without the proper measurement of time between the sowing and the reaping, nature modifies or withholds the rewards of the sowing.

在思想的领域里，有一个适当的时间播下思想的种子，有一个适当的时间收获这些思想的收获，就像有一个播种的时间和一个从大地的土壤收获的时间一样。如果没有对播种和收获之间的时间进行适当的计算，大自然就会改变或抑制播种的回报。

Q Go ahead, now, and describe the last two of the seven principles.

继续，现在，描述七个原则中的最后两个。

A The next principle is harmony.

A 下一个原则是和谐。

Throughout nature one may find evidences that all natural law moves in an orderly manner, through the law of harmony. Through the operation of this law nature forces everything within the range of a given environment to become harmoniously related. Understand this truth and you will catch a new and a more intriguing vision of the power of environment. You will understand why association with negative minds is fatal to those seeking self-determination.

人们可以在自然界中找到证据，证明所有的自然规律都是通过和谐的规律有序地运行着的。通过这个法则的运作，大自然迫使特定环境范围内的一切事物和谐地联系在一起。了解这个事实，你就会对环境的力量有一个新的、更有趣的认识。你会明白为什么与消极思想的联系对那些寻求自决的人来说是致命的。

Q Do you mean that nature voluntarily forces human beings to harmonize with the influences of their environment?

问: 你的意思是大自然自愿迫使人类与环境的影响和谐相处吗？

A Yes, that is true. The law of hypnotic rhythm forces upon every living thing the dominating influences of the environment in which it exists.

A 是的，这是真的。催眠节律强迫每一个生物受其所处环境的支配性影响。

Q If nature forces human beings to take on the nature of the environment in which they live, what means of escape are available to people who find themselves in an environment of poverty and failure but desire to escape?

问: 如果大自然迫使人类接受他们所生活的环境的自然属性，那些发现自己处于贫穷和失败的环境中却渴望逃离的人们有什么办法可以逃离呢？

A They must change their environment or remain poverty-stricken. Nature permits no one to escape the influences of his environment.

他们必须改变自己的环境，否则就会继续贫穷下去。大自然不允许任何人逃避环境的影响。

However, nature, in her abundance of wisdom, has given to every normal human being the privilege of establishing his own mental, spiritual, and physical environment, but once he establishes it he must become a part of it. This is the inexorable working of the law of harmony.

然而，大自然，以其丰富的智慧，赋予了每一个正常人建立自己的精神、精神和物理环境的特权，但是一旦他建立了它，他就必须成为它的一部分。这是和谐规律发挥作用的必然要求。

Q In a business association, for example, who establishes the dominating influence that determines the rhythm of the environment?

例如，在一个商业协会中，谁建立了决定环境节奏的主导影响力？

A The individual or individuals who think and act with definiteness of purpose.

有明确目标的个人或个人的思考和行动。

Q Is it as simple as that?

问: 就这么简单吗？

A Yes, definiteness of purpose is the starting point from which an individual may establish his own environment.

答: 是的，明确目标是个人建立自己环境的出发点。

Q I do not seem to follow your reasoning. The entire world is torn with warfare and business depressions and other forms of strife which represent about everything except harmony. Nature does not seem to be forcing people to harmonize with one another. How do you explain this inconsistency?

问: 我似乎不明白你的理由。整个世界被战争、商业萧条和其他形式的冲突所撕裂，这些冲突除了和谐之外，代表着一切。大自然似乎并没有强迫人们彼此和谐相处。你如何解释这种不一致性？

As in Hill’s day, there seems to be little harmony in our world today. When you think of the current economy, the natural disasters, the military conflicts, the human devastation from disease and hunger, does harmony seem even attainable? Hill would say, yes, even in the face of the horrible conditions of his time. While you and I may not be in control of harmony in our world, we can create harmony in our homes.

就像希尔时代一样，今天的世界似乎缺乏和谐。当你想到当前的经济，自然灾害，军事冲突，疾病和饥饿造成的人类破坏，和谐是否看起来可以实现？希尔会说，是的，即使面对他那个时代可怕的环境。虽然你和我可能无法控制我们这个世界的和谐，但我们可以在家庭中创造和谐。

A There is no inconsistency. The dominating influences of the world are, as you say, negative. Very well, nature is forcing human beings to harmonize with the dominating influences of the world environment.

A 没有不一致之处。正如你所说，这个世界的主要影响是负面的。很好，大自然正在迫使人类与世界环境的主导影响相协调。

Manifestations of harmony may be either positive or negative. For example, a group of men in prison may, and they generally do, think and act in a negative manner, but nature sees to it that the dominating influence of the prison is impressed upon every individual in it. A group of poverty-stricken people in a tenement house may fight among themselves and apparently resist all forms of harmony, but nature forces each of them to become a part of the dominating influence of the house in which they live.

和谐的表现可以是积极的，也可以是消极的。例如，一群被关在监狱里的人，他们通常会以消极的方式思考和行动，但是大自然注意到监狱的主导影响会影响到监狱里的每一个人。一群生活在廉租房里的贫困人口可能相互争斗，显然抵制一切形式的和谐，但是大自然迫使他们每个人都成为他们所居住的房子的主导影响力的一部分。

Harmony, in the sense it is here used, means that nature relates everything throughout the universes to every other thing of a similar nature. Negative influences are forced into association with one another, no matter where they may be. Positive influences are just as definitely forced into association with one another.

和谐，在这里使用的意义上，意味着自然将遍布宇宙的一切与其他具有相似性质的事物联系起来。负面影响被迫相互联系，不管他们可能在哪里。积极的影响力绝对是被迫与其他人建立联系的。

Q I am beginning to see why successful business leaders are so careful in the choice of their business associates. Men who succeed in any calling usually establish their own environment by surrounding themselves with people who think and act in terms of success. Is that the idea?

问: 我开始明白为什么成功的商业领袖在选择商业伙伴时如此谨慎。在任何职业中成功的男人通常会通过与那些以成功为思想和行为准则的人相处来建立他们自己的环境。这就是你的想法吗？

A That is the idea exactly. Observe, with profit, that the one thing all successful men insist upon is harmony among their business associates. Another trait of successful people is that they move with definiteness of purpose and insist upon their associates doing the same. Understand these two truths and you understand the major difference between a Henry Ford and a day laborer.

A 这正是我的想法。要注意，有利可图的是，所有成功人士都坚持的一件事就是与他们的商业伙伴保持和谐。成功人士的另一个特征是，他们行动时目标明确，并坚持让同事也这样做。理解这两个事实，你就会明白亨利 · 福特和临时工的主要区别。

So the principle of harmony is a benefit to us when we surround ourselves with other successful people. Think of the people you work with. Are they supporting you . . . or holding you back?

所以当我们和其他成功人士在一起时，和谐的原则对我们是有益的。想想你的同事。他们是在支持你... 还是在拖你的后腿？

Q Now tell me about the last of the seven principles.

现在告诉我七条原则中的最后一条。

A The last principle is caution.

A 最后一个原则是谨慎。

Next to the habit of drifting, the most dangerous human trait is the lack of caution.

除了随波逐流的习惯之外，人类最危险的特点就是缺乏谨慎。

People drift into all sorts of hazardous circumstances because they do not exercise caution by planning the moves they make. The drifter always moves without exercising caution. He acts first and thinks later, if at all. He does not choose his friends. He drifts along and allows people to attach themselves to him on their own terms. He does not choose an occupation. He drifts through school and is glad to get the first job that will give him food and clothing. He invites people to cheat him at trade by neglecting to inform himself of the rules of trade. He invites illness by neglecting to inform himself of the rules of sound health. He invites poverty by neglecting to protect himself against the environmental influences of the poverty-stricken. He invites failure at every step he takes by neglecting to exercise the caution to observe what causes people to fail. He invites fear in all its forms by his lack of caution in examining the causes of fear. He fails in marriage because he neglects to use caution in his choice of a mate, and he uses still less caution in his methods of relating himself to her after marriage. He loses his friends or converts them into enemies by his lack of caution in relating himself to them on the proper basis.

人们之所以会陷入各种各样的危险境地，是因为他们没有对自己的行动进行谨慎的规划。那个流浪汉总是不加小心地移动。他先行动，后思考，如果有的话。他没有选择朋友。他随波逐流，允许人们按照自己的方式依附于他。他没有选择职业。他在学校里四处漂泊，很高兴找到了第一份工作，这份工作可以给他吃的，给他穿的。他让人们在交易中欺骗他，因为他忽略了交易规则。他因忽略了健康的规则而招致疾病。他通过忽视保护自己免受贫困人口的环境影响而招致贫困。他每走一步都招致失败，因为他忽略了谨慎地观察是什么导致了人们的失败。他在审查恐惧的原因时缺乏谨慎，从而引起各种形式的恐惧。他在婚姻中失败是因为他在选择伴侣时忽略了谨慎，而且他在婚后与她联系的方法上更不谨慎。他失去了他的朋友，或者把他们变成敌人，因为他在适当的基础上与他们联系时缺乏谨慎。

“Next to the habit of drifting, the most dangerous human trait is the lack of caution.”

“除了漂泊不定的习惯之外，人类最危险的特点是缺乏谨慎。”

Q Are all people lacking in caution?

问: 是不是所有的人都缺乏谨慎？

A No, only those who have acquired the habit of drifting. The non-drifter always uses caution. He carefully thinks his plans through before he begins them. He makes allowances for the human frailties of his associates and plans ahead to bridge them.

A 不，只有那些养成了随波逐流的习惯的人。非流浪汉总是谨慎行事。他在开始计划之前仔细考虑了一番。他体谅他的同事们的人性弱点，并计划提前弥合这些弱点。

If he sends a messenger on an important mission, he sends someone else to make sure the messenger does not neglect his mission. Then he checks on both of them to be sure his wishes have been fulfilled. He takes nothing for granted where caution provides a way to insure his success.

如果他派遣一个信使去执行一个重要的任务，他会派遣另外一个人去确保信使不会忽视他的任务。然后他检查他们两个，以确保他的愿望已经实现。他不认为任何事情都是理所当然的，谨慎是他成功的保证。

Q Isn’t over-caution as detrimental as lack of caution?

过分谨慎不是和缺乏谨慎一样有害吗？

A There is no such thing as over-caution. What you call “over-caution” is an expression of fear. Fear and caution are two entirely different things.

A 没有过分谨慎这回事。你所说的“过分谨慎”是恐惧的表现。恐惧和谨慎是完全不同的两件事。

Q Don’t people mistake fear for over-caution?

难道人们不会把恐惧误认为过分谨慎吗？

A Yes, that does sometimes happen, but the majority of people create for themselves far more disastrous hazards by total lack of the habit of caution than by over-caution.

答: 是的，这种情况有时确实会发生，但是大多数人完全没有谨慎的习惯，而不是过分谨慎，这会给自己造成更多灾难性的危险。

Q In what way may caution be used most advantageously?

在什么方面可以最有利地使用警告？

A In the selection of one’s associates and in one’s method of relating oneself to associates. The reason for this is obvious. One’s associates constitute the most important part of one’s environment, and environmental influences determine whether one forms the habit of drifting or becomes a non-drifter. The person who exercises due caution in the choice of associates never allows himself to be closely associated with any person who does not bring to him, through the association, some definite mental, spiritual, or economic benefit.

在选择同事和与同事交往的方法中。原因显而易见。一个人的同伴构成了他所处环境的最重要部分，环境的影响决定了一个人是否养成了漂流的习惯，还是成为了一个非漂流者。在选择合作伙伴时保持应有的谨慎的人决不允许自己与任何不通过合作给他带来某种明确的精神、精神或经济利益的人密切联系。

Q Isn’t that method of choosing associates selfish?

这种选择同事的方法不是很自私吗？

A It is sensible and leads to self-determination. It is the desire of every normal person to find material success and happiness.

A 这是明智的，并且会导致自决。寻找物质上的成功和幸福是每个正常人的愿望。

Nothing contributes more to one’s success and happiness than carefully chosen associates. Caution in the selection of associates becomes, therefore, the duty of every person who wishes to become happy and successful. The drifter allows his closest associates to attach themselves to him on their own terms. The non-drifter carefully selects his associates and allows no one to become closely associated with him unless that person contributes some form of helpful influence or bestows some definite benefit.

对于一个人的成功和幸福来说，没有什么比精心挑选的伙伴更重要的了。因此，谨慎选择合伙人成为每个希望变得快乐和成功的人的责任。流浪汉允许他最亲密的伙伴依附于他自己的条件。非流浪汉仔细地挑选他的同伴，不允许任何人与他有密切的联系，除非那个人贡献某种形式的有益影响或给予某种确定的利益。

Q It never occurred to me that caution in the selection of friends had so definite a bearing on one’s success or failure. Do all successful people exercise caution in the selection of all their associates, whether in business, social, or professional relationships?

我从来没有想到，在选择朋友时的谨慎会对一个人的成功或失败产生如此明确的影响。是否所有的成功人士在选择他们的同事时都会小心谨慎，无论是在商业、社交还是职业关系中？

A Without the exercise of caution in the choice of all associates, no one may be certain of success in any calling. On the other hand, lack of exercise of caution brings almost certain defeat in whatever one undertakes.

在选择合作伙伴时，如果不小心谨慎，没有人能够确保在任何事情上取得成功。另一方面，缺乏谨慎几乎肯定会导致一个人在任何事情上的失败。

Do you have a hard time saying “no” to people? This chapter makes you realize that using caution in selecting your associates and learning to say “no” more often may speed you on your path to success.

你是否很难拒绝别人？这一章让你意识到，在选择你的同事和学会说“不”更经常地谨慎可能会加速你的成功之路。

SUMMARY

摘要

THREE THINGS connected with my interview with the Devil interest me most. These three factors interest me because they have been the most important influences in my own life, a fact which any reader of my story can easily discern. The three important factors are the habit of drifting, the law of hypnotic rhythm through which all habits are made permanent, and the element of time.

我对魔鬼的采访有三件事最感兴趣。这三个因素使我感兴趣，因为它们对我自己的生活产生了最重要的影响，任何读过我的故事的人都很容易看出这一点。这三个重要因素分别是漂泊的习惯、使习惯永久化的催眠律和时间因素。

Here is a trio of forces which hold inviolate the destinies of all men. The three take on a new and more important meaning when they are grouped and studied as a combined force. It takes but little imagination and scarcely any understanding of natural laws for one to see that most of the difficulties in which people find themselves are of their own making. Moreover, difficulties seldom are the outgrowth of immediate circumstances. They are generally the climax of a series of circumstances which have been consolidated through the habit of drifting and with the aid of time.

这里有三种力量，它们决定着所有人的命运。当这三种力量作为一种联合的力量进行组合和研究时，它们就具有了新的、更为重要的意义。人们几乎不需要什么想象力和对自然法则的任何理解就可以看出，人们所面临的大多数困难都是他们自己造成的。此外，困难很少是眼前环境的结果。它们通常是一系列情况的高潮，这些情况通过随波逐流的习惯和时间的帮助而得到巩固。

“Most of the difficulties in which people find themselves are of their own making.”

“人们发现自己面临的大多数困难都是自己造成的。”

Many people today have a victim mentality which they use as an excuse to not take responsibility for their own lives.

今天许多人有一种受害者心态，他们以此为借口不对自己的生活负责。

Samuel Insull did not lose his $4 billion industrial empire as the result of the depression. He began losing it long before the depression when he became the victim of a group of women who flattered him into turning his talents from public utilities to grand opera. If ever a man in a high position in the financial world went down because of the power of drifting, hypnotic rhythm, and time, that man was Samuel Insull. I am writing from accurate knowledge of Mr. Insull and the cause of his troubles dating from the time that I served with him during the World War to the time of his ill-advised attempt to run away from himself.

塞缪尔并没有因为大萧条而失去他价值40亿美元的工业帝国。早在大萧条之前，他就已经开始失去理智，当时他成了一群女人的牺牲品，这些女人奉承他，把他的才华从公共事业转向了大歌剧。如果说在金融界有一个身居高位的人因为漂泊、催眠般的节奏和时间的力量而走下坡路，那么这个人就是塞缪尔 · 英萨尔。我写这封信是出于对因苏尔先生的准确了解，以及从我在第二次世界大战期间与他一起服役到他不明智地试图逃离自己的那段时间，他遇到麻烦的原因。

Samuel Insull moved from England to the U.S. in 1881 to become the private secretary of Thomas Edison and rose to become president of the Chicago Edison Co. in 1892. By 1907 he had taken control of Chicago’s transit system. By 1912 he was operating several hundred power plants. He vigorously promoted the stock of his holding companies. When they collapsed in 1932, he fled to Europe; extradited in 1934, he was tried three times for fraud, violation of bankruptcy laws, and embezzlement, but was acquitted each time. Hill gives us an inside look at the other reasons for his collapse and fall from grace. Today you instantly know the name Edison . . . but probably do not recognize Insull.

1881年，塞缪尔 · 英萨尔从英国移居美国，成为托马斯 · 爱迪生的私人秘书，并于1892年升任芝加哥爱迪生公司总裁。到1907年，他已经控制了芝加哥的交通系统。到1912年，他已经经营了几百家发电厂。他大力宣传他的控股公司的股票。当他们在1932年分崩离析时，他逃往欧洲; 1934年被引渡回国，他因欺诈、违反破产法和挪用公款三次受审，但每次都被无罪释放。希尔给了我们一个内部的原因，他崩溃和失宠的其他原因。今天你立刻知道了爱迪生这个名字... ... 但是可能不认识因苏尔。

Henry Ford went through the same depression that swept Mr. Insull under, but Ford came out on top without a scratch. Do you want to know the reason? I’ll tell you. Ford has the habit of not drifting on any subject. Time is Ford’s friend because he has formed the habit of using it in a positive, constructive manner, with the aid of thoughts of his own making, woven into plans of his own creation.

亨利 · 福特经历了横扫英萨尔先生的同样的抑郁症，但是福特却毫发无伤地拔得头筹。你想知道原因吗？我来告诉你。福特有一个习惯，就是不在任何问题上绕圈子。时间是福特的朋友，因为他已经养成了积极、有建设性地利用时间的习惯，借助于他自己创造的思想，编织成他自己创造的计划。

Take any circumstance you wish, measure it with reference to its relationship to the habit of drifting, hypnotic rhythm, and time, and you may ascertain accurately the cause of all success and all failure.

采取任何你希望的情况，衡量它与习惯的关系，催眠的节奏，和时间，你可以确定所有成功和所有失败的原因。

Franklin D. Roosevelt went into office with a bang during his first term. He had but one major purpose in mind and that was very definite. It was to stop the stampede of fear and start people to thinking and talking in terms of business recovery instead of business depression.

富兰克林·德拉诺·罗斯福在他的第一个任期内轰轰烈烈地上任。他心里只有一个主要的目的，那就是非常明确的。这是为了阻止恐慌的蔓延，让人们开始从商业复苏而不是商业萧条的角度思考和讨论。

In carrying out that purpose, there was no drifting. The forces of the entire nation were consolidated and moved as one to help carry out the President’s definite purpose. For the first time in the history of America, the newspapers of all political leanings, the churches of all denominations, the people of all races and colors, and the political organizations of all brands united themselves into one stupendous power for the sole purpose of helping the President restore faith and normal business relationships in the country.

为了达到这个目的，我们没有漂泊不定。整个国家的力量得到了巩固，并作为一个整体进行调动，以帮助实现总统的明确目标。美国历史上第一次，所有政治倾向的报纸、所有教派的教会、所有种族和肤色的人民以及所有品牌的政治组织联合成一个巨大的力量，唯一的目的就是帮助总统恢复信仰和正常的商业关系。

In a conference held between the President and a group of emergency advisers a few days after he went into office, I asked him what was his major problem. He replied, “It is not a question of majors and minors; we have but one problem and that is to stop fear and supplant it with faith.”

在总统上任后的几天里，我在总统和一组紧急顾问之间举行的一次会议上问他，他的主要问题是什么。他回答说: “这不是专业和未成年人的问题，我们只有一个问题，那就是停止恐惧，用信心取而代之。”

Before the end of his first year in office, the President had stopped fear and supplanted it by faith, and the nation was slowly but surely on the way out of the jungle of depression. By the end of his first term—mark well the element of lapse of time—the President had so effectively consolidated the forces of American business and private life that he had an entire nation in back of him, ready, willing, and enthusiastically desirous of following his lead no matter which way he went.

在他执政的第一年结束之前，总统已经停止了恐惧并用信仰取代了它，整个国家缓慢但坚定地走出了萧条的丛林。在他的第一个任期结束时——这很好地标志着时间的流逝——总统有效地巩固了美国商业和私人生活的力量，以至于整个国家都支持他，随时准备、愿意和热情地追随他的领导，不管他走哪条路。

These are facts well known to everyone who reads newspapers or listens to the radio.

这些事实对每个读报纸或听广播的人来说都是众所周知的。

Like all of us, Napoleon Hill lived in a political environment that affected everyone. We often think of ourselves as “victims” of the media or the political system or other outside forces. Hill is showing us how to rise above victimhood— another of the Devil’s tools—and take responsibility for all our choices.

和我们所有人一样，拿破仑 · 希尔生活的政治环境影响着每一个人。我们常常认为自己是媒体、政治制度或其他外部力量的“受害者”。希尔正在向我们展示如何超越受害者的心态ーー这也是魔鬼的另一个工具ーー并为我们的所有选择承担责任。

Then came another presidential election and the opportunity for the people to express their faith in their leader. They expressed it in a landslide without precedent in American politics, and the President went into office a second time with an almost unanimous electorate vote with only two states meekly dissenting.

然后又是一次总统选举，人民有机会表达他们对领导人的信任。他们以美国政治史上前所未有的压倒性优势表达了这一观点，总统第二次就职时几乎全票通过，只有两个州表示了温顺的反对。

Now observe how the Wheel of Life began to reverse itself and turn back in the other direction. The President changed his policy from definiteness of purpose to indefiniteness and drifting.

现在来看看生命之轮是如何开始自我反转并朝着另一个方向回转的。总统改变了他的政策，从目标的确定变成了不确定和游移不定。

His change of policy split the powerful labor group and turned more than half of it against him. It split the almost-solid following he held in both houses of Congress, and more important than all this, it split the American people into “pro” and “anti” groups with the result that about all the President had left of his original political assets was his million-dollar smile and his ready handshake—obviously not enough to enable him to regain the power he once wielded in American life.

他的政策改变分裂了强大的劳工团体，使其中一半以上的人反对他。它分裂了他在国会参众两院几乎牢不可破的支持者，更重要的是，它把美国人民分成了“支持”和“反对”两派，结果，这位总统最初的政治资产只剩下他那百万美元的微笑和随时可以握手——显然不足以让他重新获得他曾经在美国生活中掌握的权力。

Here, then, we have an excellent example of a man who skyrocketed to great power through definiteness of purpose and belly-flopped to the starting point by his habit of drifting. In both his rise and his fall can be seen clearly the operation of the principles of drifting and non-drifting reaching a climax through the power of hypnotic rhythm and time.

在这里，我们有一个很好的例子，一个人通过明确的目标飞速发展成为一个强大的力量，但是由于他的漂泊不定的习惯而跌落到了起点。在他的兴衰中，都可以清楚地看到通过催眠的节奏和时间的力量，漂移和不漂移原则的运作达到了一个高潮。

“Here, then, we have an excellent example of a man who skyrocketed to great power through definiteness of purpose and belly-flopped to the starting point by his habit of drifting.”

“这里，我们有一个很好的例子，说明一个人凭借明确的目标而一飞冲天，凭借漂泊不定的习惯跌到了起点。”

Take a moment to think of other people, in the public eye or in your circle of influence, who achieved great success only to lose it later because of drifting.

花点时间想想其他人，无论是在公众眼里还是在你的影响力圈子里，他们取得了巨大的成功，但后来却因为漂泊而失去了。

All my life the Devil had a dramatic story to tell of his dealings with me. He saw me drift in and out of scores of business opportunities for which many would have given a king’s ransom. He saw me drifting in my policy of relating myself to others, particularly in my lack of caution in business dealings.

在我的一生中，魔鬼有一个戏剧性的故事来讲述他与我的交易。他看到我在数十个商业机会中徘徊，许多人愿意为此付出巨大的代价。他看到我在处理人际关系的政策上有些飘忽不定，特别是在商业交往中缺乏谨慎。

The circumstance which saved me from fatal control of the law of hypnotic rhythm was the definiteness of purpose with which, at long last, I dedicated my entire life to the organization of a philosophy of individual achievement. I drifted at one time or another on all my minor whims and endeavors, but my drifting was offset by my major purpose, which was sufficient to restore my courage and start me once more in the quest of knowledge every time I was defeated in connection with my minor aims.

把我从催眠律法的致命控制中解救出来的环境是明确的目标，最后，我终于把我的整个生命奉献给了个人成就的哲学的组织。我偶尔会因为一些小小的兴趣和努力而漂泊不定，但是我的漂泊被我的主要目标所抵消，每当我因为一些小目标而失败时，这些目标就足以让我恢复勇气，再次开始我对知识的追求。

I learned something of the hazardous nature of the habit of drifting while engaged in analyzing more than 25,000 people in connection with the organization of the Law of Success. These analyses showed that only two out of every 100 have a definite major aim in life. The other 98 were caught by the habit of drifting. It seems more than a coincidence that my analyses clearly corroborated the Devil’s claim that he controls 98 out of every 100 people because of their habit of drifting.

在对25000多人进行与成功法则的组织有关的分析时，我学到了一些漂泊习惯的危险本质。这些分析表明，每100个人中只有两个人有明确的人生目标。其余的98只被漂流的习惯困住了。这似乎不仅仅是一个巧合，我的分析清楚地证实了魔鬼的说法，他控制98% 的人，因为他们的习惯漂泊。

Looking back over my own career, I can see clearly that I could have avoided the majority of the temporary defeats with which I met if I had been definitely following a plan for the attainment of my major purpose in life.

回顾我自己的职业生涯，我可以清楚地看到，如果我明确地按照一个计划来实现我人生的主要目标，我本可以避免大多数我遇到的暂时性失败。

From my experience in having analyzed the problems of more than 5,000 families, I know, definitely, that the majority of married people who get out of harmony with each other do so because of the accumulation of a great number of little circumstances in their married relationship which could have been cleared up and disposed of as they arose if there had been a definite policy to do so. They do not live their married life with definiteness of purpose.

从我分析了5000多个家庭的问题的经验来看，我确切地知道，大多数已婚人士之所以彼此不和谐，是因为他们的婚姻关系中积累了大量的小环境，如果有明确的政策的话，这些环境本来可以在出现时得到清理和处理。他们的婚姻生活没有明确的目标。

So the story has gone, all back down the ages. The man with the most definite plan and purpose and the most power rides on to victory. The others scurry for cover and get crushed under the heels of those who are more determined.

所以这个故事已经过去了，都是很久以前的事了。有最明确的计划、目标和最强大的力量的人骑向胜利。其他人急忙寻找掩护，被那些更有决心的人踩在脚下。

The answer is not hard to find. There is no use looking toward high heaven for it. For my part I would prefer to seek the answer from the Devil, for he would tell me quickly enough that victory goes to the people who know what they want and are determined to have it. They have mastered the habit of drifting. They have definite policies, definite plans, and definite objectives. Their opposition, which may outnumber them very greatly, has no chance against them because the opposition has no plan, no purpose, no policy except that of drifting along, hoping that something may turn up to help them. In those three brief sentences you have the sum and the substance of the difference between success and failure, power and lack of it.

答案不难找到。指望高高的天堂是没有用的。就我而言，我宁愿从魔鬼那里寻求答案，因为他会很快告诉我，胜利属于那些知道自己想要什么并决心拥有它的人们。他们已经掌握了随波逐流的习惯。他们有明确的方针、明确的计划和明确的目标。他们的反对派人数可能远远超过他们，因为反对派没有计划，没有目的，没有政策，只是随波逐流，希望有什么东西能帮助他们。在这三个简短的句子中，你可以总结出成功与失败、力量与缺乏之间的区别。

We come, now, near to the end of our visit through this book. If we were to try to state in one brief sentence the most important part of that which I have tried to convey through the book, it would be something like this:

现在，通过这本书，我们的访问接近尾声。如果我们试着用一个简短的句子来陈述我试图通过这本书来传达的最重要的部分，大概是这样的:

One’s dominating desires can be crystallized into their physical equivalents through definiteness of purpose backed by definiteness of plans, with the aid of nature’s law of hypnotic rhythm and time!

一个人支配性的欲望可以通过明确的目的和明确的计划，借助于催眠节奏和时间的自然法则，结晶成他们的物理等价物！

There you have the positive phase of the philosophy of individual achievement I have tried to describe through this book, brought down to an irreducible minimum of brevity and simplicity. If you expand the philosophy for the purpose of adapting it to the circumstances of life, you find that it is as broad as life itself, that it covers all human relationships, all human thoughts, aims, and desires.

这就是我试图通过这本书描述的个人成就哲学的积极阶段，它将简洁简洁降到了不可或缺的最低限度。如果你为了适应生活环境而扩展哲学，你会发现它和生活本身一样广泛，它涵盖了所有的人际关系，所有的人类思想、目标和欲望。

So here we are, at the end of the strangest of all the thousands of interviews I have had with the great and the near-great, over a period of fifty years of labor, in my search for the truths of life that lead to happiness and economic security.

因此，在我五十年的劳动生涯中，我与伟大的和近乎伟大的人物进行了数以千计的访谈，寻找能够带来幸福和经济安全的生活真理，最后我们来到了这里，这是最奇怪的访谈。

How strange, indeed, that after having had active cooperation from such men as Carnegie, Edison, and Ford, I should have been compelled, finally, to go to the Devil for a working knowledge of the greatest of all the principles uncovered in my quest for truth. How strange that I was forced to experience poverty and failure and adversity in a hundred forms before being given the privilege of understanding and using a law of nature which softens the thrust of these wicked weapons or wipes them out altogether. But the strangest of all this dramatic experience which life has provided me is the simplicity of the law through which, if I had understood it, I could have transmuted my desires into substantial form without having to undergo so many years of hardship and misery.

多么奇怪啊，在得到卡内基、爱迪生和福特这些人的积极合作之后，我最终还是被迫去魔鬼那里寻找我在追求真理过程中所发现的最伟大的原则的工作知识。奇怪的是，我被迫经历一百种形式的贫穷、失败和逆境，然后才被赋予理解和运用自然法则的特权，这种法则软化了这些邪恶武器的力量，或者将它们全部消灭。但是生活给予我的这些戏剧性的经历中最奇怪的是法律的简单性，如果我理解了它，我就可以把我的欲望变成实体形式，而不必经历这么多年的苦难和痛苦。

I find now, at the end of my interview with the Devil, that I had been carrying in my own pockets the matches with which the fires of adversity were being touched off. And I find, too, that the water with which those fires were finally extinguished was at my command in great abundance.

现在，在我与魔鬼的会谈结束时，我发现我自己的口袋里装着火柴，正是用这些火柴点燃了逆境之火。我还发现，那些最终被扑灭的大火所依赖的水源，是我大量支配的。

I searched for the philosopher’s lodestone with which failure may be converted into success, only to learn that both success and failure are the results of day-to-day evolutionary forces through which dominating thoughts are pieced together bit by bit and woven into the things we want or the things we do not want, according to the nature of those thoughts.

我寻找哲学家的磁石，失败可以转化为成功，结果却发现，成功和失败都是日常进化力量的结果，通过这些力量，主导思想被一点一点地拼凑起来，根据这些思想的本质，编织成我们想要的东西或我们不想要的东西。

How unfortunate that I did not understand this truth from the time that I reached the age of reason, for if I had understood it then I might have been able to go around some of the hurdles I have been forced to jump as I walked through “The Valley of the Shadow” of life.

当我到了理智的年龄时，我不理解这个真理是多么不幸，因为如果我理解了它，那么我可能就能够绕过我在穿越生命的“阴影之谷”时被迫跨越的一些障碍。

The story of my interview with the Devil is now in your hands. The benefits you will receive from it will be in exact proportion to the thought it inspires in you. To benefit from reading the interview, you need not agree with every portion of it.

我与魔鬼会面的故事现在就在你们手中。你将从中得到的好处将与它在你身上激发的思想成正比。为了从阅读面试中获益，你不需要对面试的每一部分都表示赞同。

You have only to think and to reach your own conclusions concerning every part of it. How reasonable that is. You are the judge and the jury and the attorney for both the prosecution and the defense. If you do not win your case, the loss and the cause thereof will be yours!

你只需要思考并且得出你自己关于它的每一部分的结论。这是多么合理啊。你既是法官，也是陪审团，还是控方和辩方的律师。如果你没有赢得官司，损失和原因将是你的！

—NAPOLEON HILL

ー napoleon HILL

“One’s dominating desires can be crystallized into their physical equivalents through definiteness of purpose backed by definiteness of plans, with the aid of nature’s law of hypnotic rhythm and time!”

“一个人支配性的欲望可以通过明确的目标和明确的计划，借助于催眠律和时间的自然法则，结晶成他们的物理等价物! ”

Napoleon Hill wanted to share this message with the world in the 1930s, but instead it was hidden away in a vault, to be finally uncovered and shared with you now in 2011— for a reason. Will you . . .

上世纪30年代，拿破仑 · 希尔(Napoleon Hill)曾想与世界分享这一信息，但它却被藏在一个保险库里，最终在2011年被发现，并与你分享——这是有原因的。你愿意..。

•意识到你自己的口袋里装着用来点燃逆境之火的火柴，并且发现，用来最终扑灭这些火焰的水也是大量由你自己掌控的？然后:

• Find your definiteness of purpose?

•找到你的明确目标？

• Create a definite plan?

•制定一个明确的计划？

• Engage the aid of nature’s law of hypnotic rhythm?

•利用催眠节律的自然法则？

• And use the asset of time to assist you in reaching your greatest success?

•利用时间的资产来帮助你获得最大的成功？

AFTERWORD

后记

WHETHER YOU HAVE READ this entire book or only a few of its pages before turning to this afterword, you will have realized that if the historical names, dates, and events in this book were replaced by those of our current times, little has changed. From Hill’s description of media propaganda, the conditioning that children receive in school, the fear-based teachings preached by religions, people’s poor diet and health habits, to the challenging economic climate, little seems to have shifted in our collective consciousness and therefore in our collective experience.

不管你是读完了这本书还是只读了其中的几页，在翻到这篇后记之前，你都会意识到，如果这本书中的历史名称、日期和事件被我们当前时代的名称、日期和事件所取代，那么几乎没有什么变化。从希尔对媒体宣传的描述、儿童在学校接受的教育、宗教宣扬的以恐惧为基础的教育、人们不良的饮食和健康习惯，到充满挑战的经济气候，我们的集体意识似乎几乎没有改变，因此也没有改变我们的集体经验。

The good news is that it is never too late for a new beginning, for a renaissance in consciousness. As Mr. Hill reminds us, “I have also discovered that there comes with every experience of temporary defeat, and every failure and every form of adversity, the seed of an equivalent benefit.” Our path is seemingly composed of a polarity of both failure and success. A lighter way of putting it might be that Hill’s principles for living teach us “how to fail successfully.” This is a paradox understood by the spiritually mature, those whom he describes as having risen above the “hypnotic rhythm” and discovered their “other self,” which can also be identified as the Self of the self, the Higher Self, or the Authentic Self.

好消息是，对于一个新的开始，一个意识的复兴，永远不会太晚。正如希尔先生提醒我们的那样，“我还发现，每一次暂时失败的经历，每一次失败和每一种形式的逆境，都是获得同等收益的种子。”我们的道路似乎是由失败和成功的极性组成的。一种更轻松的说法可能是，希尔的生活原则教我们“如何成功地失败”这是一个悖论，被精神上成熟的人所理解，他们被描述为已经超越了“催眠的节奏” ，发现了他们的“其他的自我” ，这也可以被认定为自我的自我，更高的自我，或真实的自我。

It is encouraging that many of today’s spiritual, philosophical, self-help, and even scientific authors share Hill’s view of what he calls “definiteness of purpose,” or, in current parlance, “intention setting.” When it is our intention to wake up from the “hypnotic rhythm” of living—what the Hindus call delusion and the Buddhists call illusion—individual and collective consciousness expands. We, along with our global family, benefit.

令人鼓舞的是，今天许多精神上的、哲学上的、自助的、甚至科学上的作者都赞同希尔对他所说的“明确目标”的看法，或者用现在的说法，“意图设定”当我们打算从生活的“催眠节奏”(印度教徒称之为妄想，佛教徒称之为幻觉)中醒来时，个人和集体意识就会扩大。我们，连同我们的全球大家庭，都从中受益。

Hill’s integrity shines through his descriptions of what it means to manifest success. In fact, he unhesitatingly announces that “any man can avail himself of the benefits of his ‘other self’” as long as he is not “steeped in greed.” This spiritually dignified statement elevates success to a matter of consciousness—that is, success does not necessarily mean that “he who has the most toys wins.” Hill thus eliminates confusing spiritual awakening with the capacity to manifest things in one’s life, for there is never enough of “more.”

希尔的正直在他对成功意味着什么的描述中熠熠生辉。事实上，他毫不犹豫地宣布，“任何人都可以利用他的‘他我’的好处” ，只要他不“沉浸在贪婪之中”这种精神上高贵的说法将成功提升到一个意识层面的问题ーー也就是说，成功并不一定意味着“拥有最多玩具的人就是赢家”希尔因此消除了混乱的精神觉醒与能力，以彰显的东西在一个人的生活，因为从来没有足够的“更多”

We are also taught the importance of awareness, of mindfulness, an activity of consciousness abhorred by Hill’s Devil, who delights in using people’s lack of thinking for themselves to his advantage. Consciously observing the mind and its capacities is to look at it with respect, compassion, gratitude, for it is God’s gift to us. Mind not only forms our inner landscape; it creates our outer circumstances. Let us not fight with the mind; let us appreciate its nuances, its intuitions, its utmost capacities with the understanding that mind is the key to being self-directed, self-empowered, self-confident.

我们也被教导意识的重要性，正念，一种被希尔的魔鬼憎恶的意识活动，他喜欢利用人们缺乏思考来为自己谋利。有意识地观察心灵及其能力，就是以尊重、同情和感激的心态来看待它，因为它是上帝赐予我们的礼物。思想不仅形成了我们的内心世界，它还创造了我们的外部环境。让我们不要与心灵作斗争; 让我们欣赏它的细微差别、它的直觉和它最大的能力，并且理解心灵是自我导向、自我授权和自信的关键。

Next to “drifting,” the most dangerous human trait Hill describes is the “lack of caution,” or what we might call a lack of discernment. Discernment is a relative of wisdom, which causes us to think of the repercussions before we take action, as well as to honestly observe the results of our choice-making. Thus we may create our own path to freedom.

除了“随波逐流” ，希尔描述的最危险的人类特征是“缺乏谨慎” ，或者我们可以称之为缺乏洞察力。洞察力是智慧的相对，它使我们在采取行动之前想到后果，并且诚实地观察我们做出选择的结果。因此，我们可以创造自己的自由之路。

In the minds of his modern-day readers, Hill's teachings are most often associated with prosperity, which translates as money in one’s individual coffers. But truth be told, he has shared with the world his wisdom of “how-to-live principles,” beginning with one’s interior being, one’s inner state of consciousness, inviting us to give outer expression to our highest potential not only for our own benefit, but for all humankind.

在现代读者的心目中，希尔的教义最常与富裕联系在一起，也就是个人金库中的金钱。但是说实话，他已经向世界分享了他的“如何生活的原则”的智慧，从一个人的内在存在，一个人的内在意识状态开始，邀请我们把我们最大的潜能表达出来，不仅是为了我们自己的利益，也是为了全人类。

I wish to add that it was a wisdom-guided choice on the part of the Napoleon Hill Foundation to entrust this precious manuscript to the able hands of Sharon Lechter. Her many years of deeply studying Napoleon Hill’s truth principles, and more importantly her practice of them, have made her a perfect candidate to now offer this manuscript to the world.

我想补充一点，拿破仑 · 希尔基金会将这份珍贵的手稿委托给莎朗 · 莱切特，这是一个明智的选择。她多年来深入研究拿破仑 · 希尔的真理原则，更重要的是她对这些原则的实践，使她成为现在向世界提供这份手稿的完美人选。

May all Hill’s readers break free from conditional belief systems and live life in all of its richness, its exquisite beauty and joy, freely delivering their gifts, talents, and skills on this planet we all call home. Peace and richest blessings to you!

希望所有希尔的读者都能从条件信仰体系中解放出来，生活在这个我们称之为家的星球上，享受它所有的丰富、精致的美丽和快乐，自由地传递他们的天赋、才能和技能。祝你平安、幸福！

—MICHAEL BERNARD BECKWITH

ー michael BERNARD BECKWITH

MICHAEL BERNARD BECKWITH is the author of Spiritual Liberation: Fulfilling Your Soul’s Potential, and was featured in The Secret. He is the founder of the Agape International Spiritual Center and the co-founder of the Association for Global New Thought, and the Season for Nonviolence.

迈克尔 · 伯纳德 · 贝克维斯是《精神解放: 发挥你灵魂的潜能》一书的作者，并在《秘密》一书中有特写。他是爱加倍国际精神中心的创始人，也是全球新思想协会和非暴力季节的共同创始人。

IN REFLECTION

反思

THROUGHOUT NAPOLEON HILL’S WRITINGS, there is a strong spirituality present, informing his methods and his morality. In many places in the present book, Outwitting the Devil, this religious foundation for his belief system is perhaps at its most explicit.

在拿破仑 · 希尔的作品中，有一种强烈的灵性存在，为他的方法和道德提供信息。在本书《战胜心魔许多地方，他的信仰体系的这种宗教基础也许是最明确的。

Some of his statements about evil and fear, about “indefiniteness” and “drifting,” derive from an American religious tradition that dates back, at least, to the Transcendentalism of Ralph Waldo Emerson in the mid-nineteenth century. Currents in American spirituality in Hill’s day (during the writing of this book in the late 1930s) included Norman Vincent Peale, Emmett Fox, and, in popular inspirational fiction, Lloyd C. Douglas. The very personal Christian evangelism of Aimee Semple McPherson and Billy Sunday were also still omnipresent in the media and public consciousness of the era.

他的一些关于邪恶和恐惧，关于“不确定性”和“漂泊不定”的论述来源于美国的宗教传统，至少可以追溯到19世纪中叶的超验主义拉尔夫·沃尔多·爱默生。希尔时代(在20世纪30年代写这本书的时候)美国精神的潮流包括诺曼 · 文森特 · 皮尔，埃米特 · 福克斯，以及流行励志小说中的劳埃德 · 道格拉斯。艾梅 · 森普尔 · 麦克弗森和比利 · 桑迪非常个人化的基督教布道在那个时代的媒体和公众意识中仍然无处不在。

For Hill, however, the stature of some of the titans of industry and finance of the time achieved a kind of religious validation and served to inspire his own thought and action, and he urged others to look to these men—and all were men—as models of successful moral behavior that yielded personal success as well as general good.

然而，对希尔来说，当时一些工业和金融巨头的地位获得了某种宗教认可，激发了他自己的思想和行动，他敦促其他人把这些人ーー而且他们都是男人ーー作为成功的道德行为的典范，既带来个人的成功，也带来普遍的好处。

The Great Depression was, for Napoleon Hill, in great measure a moral failure. What would he say about our current crises in financial markets—the near collapse of the banking system in 2008 and the subsequent severe recession that has affected the lives of everyone who will pick up this book in 2011 and beyond?

对拿破仑 · 希尔来说，大萧条在很大程度上是道德上的失败。对于我们当前的金融市场危机——2008年银行体系几近崩溃，以及随后出现的严重衰退，影响了2011年及以后每个人的生活——他会说些什么呢？

His pantheon included Carnegie (of course), Edison, Ford, and Rockefeller. Each of these tycoons has been subsequently analyzed and reanalyzed by historians, economists, and biographers and their personal flaws placed in the glare of public scrutiny. To Hill, they were not historical figures but contemporary leaders on the world stage—as were Adolf Hitler and Benito Mussolini, Franklin Roosevelt and Winston Churchill. He did not critique Rockefeller’s ruthless competitiveness, and he was probably unaware at the time of Ford’s anti-Semitism.

他的万神殿包括卡内基(当然) ，爱迪生，福特和洛克菲勒。历史学家、经济学家和传记作家随后对这些大亨及其个人缺陷进行了分析和重新分析，并将其置于公众密切关注之下。在希尔看来，他们不是历史人物，而是当代世界舞台上的领导人---- 就像阿道夫 · 希特勒和贝尼托·墨索里尼、富兰克林·德拉诺·罗斯福和温斯顿·丘吉尔一样。他没有批评洛克菲勒无情的竞争力，而且在福特的反犹太主义时期，他可能也不知道这一点。

For Hill, American society and the free market system held the best hope for the world as it teetered on the brink of conflagration—and even with the evident imperfections of his native country (what he saw as its susceptibility to the Devil’s machinations), there was nothing on earth that could compare with it.

在希尔看来，当世界濒临战火的边缘时，美国社会和自由市场体系为世界带来了最大的希望。即使他的祖国有明显的不完美之处(他认为美国容易受到魔鬼阴谋的影响) ，世界上也没有任何东西可以与之相比。

For individuals who made the personal choice to succeed in life, who resisted the temptations and weaknesses of irreligion and sought, instead, the help of God (called by various names in the book), there was no limit to how far they might go. Limits were self-imposed, or imposed by the negative outside force of evil, personified by the Devil.

对于那些个人选择在生活中获得成功，抵制不信教的诱惑和软弱，寻求上帝的帮助(书中有各种各样的称呼)的人来说，他们可以走多远是没有限制的。限制是自我强加的，或者是被邪恶的外部消极力量强加的，被魔鬼拟人化了。

So what is Hill’s religion? Frankly, that is not important to me. As much as I have been influenced by Napoleon Hill’s philosophy and fascinated by his life, it has never mattered to me what church he attended or whether he attended any church at all. More important is the question: What is he teaching us today about the role of faith in our lives?

那么，希尔的宗教是什么呢？坦白说，这对我来说并不重要。尽管我深受拿破仑 · 希尔哲学的影响，对他的生活着迷，但他去过哪个教堂，或者他是否去过任何教堂，对我来说都无关紧要。更重要的是这个问题: 今天他教给我们什么关于信仰在我们生活中的作用？

The answer to that question is for you to decide. I think it is a foundational issue that affects every line he writes. After all, he chose to frame this book in the classical genre of the philosophical dialogue, and he sets up a sparring match with the most vivid anti-religious figure in all of literature (from the Bible, through Milton, through C.S. Lewis). And I continue to be fascinated by this choice for it allows Hill to express—in a very readable style—his own deeply held beliefs and theories about human behavior. It holds profound lessons for us all.

这个问题的答案是由你来决定。我认为这是一个基础性的问题，影响着他写的每一行。毕竟，他选择将这本书框架在经典的哲学对话体裁中，并且与所有文学作品中最生动的反宗教人物(从圣经，到弥尔顿，再到 c.s. 刘易斯)进行了一场辩论赛。我仍然对这种选择很感兴趣，因为它使希尔能够以非常可读的方式表达他自己对人类行为深信不疑的信念和理论。它对我们所有人都有深刻的教训。

As you go forward in your life and find obstacles in your way, it may serve you to review Hill’s seven principles for Outwitting the Devil in your life.

当你在人生的道路上前进，发现前进道路上的障碍时，你可以回顾一下希尔为你人生的战胜心魔几个月提出的7条原则。

• Definiteness of purpose

•目标明确

• Mastery over self

•掌控自我

• Learning from adversity

‧从逆境中学习

• Controlling environmental influence (associations)

‧控制环境影响(协会)

• Time (giving permanency to positive, rather than negative thought-habits and developing wisdom)

•时间(给予积极而非消极的思维习惯以永久性，并培养智慧)

• Harmony (acting with definiteness of purpose to become the dominating influence in your own mental, spiritual, and physical environment)

•和谐(带着明确的目标行动，在你自己的精神、精神和物理环境中成为主导影响力)

• Caution (thinking through your plan before you act)

•谨慎(在行动前仔细考虑你的计划)

In reviewing these seven principles, you may identify and reveal what is holding you back from achieving your greatest success.

在回顾这七条原则时，你可能会发现并揭示阻碍你获得最大成功的因素。

It was a profound blessing to me to have the Napoleon Hill Foundation entrust this manuscript to my hands—a manuscript that was hidden and locked away for over seventy years (either by his wife or the Devil himself . . . you decide). They say when a student is ready, the teacher will appear. Is it possible that Think and Grow Rich was the right message during the Great Depression and that Outwitting the Devil is the right message for our current times? I believe we see God’s hand at work, not the Devil’s. I believe Outwitting the Devil was not published until God felt it was the right message at the right time . . . now for us in 2011. It has definitely made a huge impact in my life and I hope that you will find value in it for your life.

拿破仑 · 希尔基金会把这份手稿委托给我，这对我来说是一个深刻的祝福ーー这份手稿被藏了超过70年(要么是他的妻子，要么是魔鬼本人... ... 你自己决定)。他们说当一个学生准备好了，老师就会出现。有没有可能思考致富是大萧条时期的正确信息，战胜心魔是当今时代的正确信息？我相信我们看到的是上帝的手在工作，而不是魔鬼的手。我相信，直到2011年，上帝觉得战胜心魔在正确的时间传达了正确的信息，我们才得以出版。它无疑对我的生活产生了巨大的影响，我希望你能从中找到生活的价值。

May Napoleon Hill’s words bring you
hope, courage, and, most of all,
definiteness of purpose for your life . . .
Be blessed.

愿拿破仑 · 希尔的话给你带来希望、勇气，最重要的是，给你的生活带来明确的目标... ... 祝福你。

—SHARON LECHTER

ー sharon LECHTER

About the Authors

关于作者

NAPOLEON HILL
1883–1970

拿破仑 · 希尔1883-1970

NAPOLEON HILL WAS BORN IN 1883 in the remote mountains of Wise County, Virginia. He was born into poverty, and his mother died when he was nine years old. One year later his father remarried, and his stepmother became a source of inspiration for the young boy.

拿破仑 · 希尔1883年出生于弗吉尼亚州怀斯县的偏远山区。他出身贫寒，母亲在他九岁时就去世了。一年后，他的父亲再婚了，他的继母成为这个年轻男孩灵感的源泉。

With the influence of his stepmother, Hill became a newspaper reporter while in his teens. His writings got the attention of Robert L. Taylor, former governor of Tennessee and later a United States senator. Taylor owned Bob Taylor’s Magazine and employed the young Hill to write success stories. At the time, Hill was enrolled at Georgetown University Law School.

在继母的影响下，希尔在十几岁时成为了一名报社记者。他的著作引起了 Robert l. Taylor 的注意，Robert l. Taylor 是前田纳西州州长列表，后来成为美国参议员。泰勒拥有鲍勃 · 泰勒的杂志，并雇佣年轻的希尔写成功的故事。当时，希尔被乔治城大学法学院录取。

In 1908 Hill was assigned to interview Andrew Carnegie and a three-hour interview became one that lasted three days. While Hill did the interviewing, Carnegie sold him on the idea of organizing the world’s first philosophy of personal achievement, based on the principles of success.

1908年，希尔被指派采访安德鲁 · 卡内基，三个小时的采访持续了三天。当希尔接受采访时，卡内基向他推销了一个想法，那就是以成功的原则为基础，组织世界上第一个个人成就哲学。

Carnegie provided Hill with introductions to giants of the time including Henry Ford, Thomas A. Edison, and John D. Rockefeller. Hill was to spend twenty years interviewing, studying, and writing about successful individuals.

卡内基为希尔介绍了当时的一些大人物，包括亨利 · 福特、爱迪生和约翰·戴维森·洛克菲勒。希尔花了二十年时间采访、研究和写作成功人士。

It would be twenty years after Hill interviewed Andrew Carnegie before he wrote the eight-volume Law of Success in 1928. He was to write many best sellers in his lifetime. In 1937 Hill wrote Think and Grow Rich, which became the best-selling self-help book of all time and continues today to sell millions of copies all over the world. Little wonder that Hill was often introduced as Miracle Man—Maker of Millionaires.

在希尔采访安德鲁 · 卡内基20年后，他于1928年写下了八卷本的《成功法则》。他一生中写了许多畅销书。1937年，希尔写了《思考致富》一书，成为有史以来最畅销的自助书，至今仍在全世界销售数百万册。难怪希尔经常被称为创造奇迹的人ーー百万富翁的制造者。

About the Authors

关于作者

SHARON LECHTER

莎伦 · 莱切特

A LIFE-LONG EDUCATION ADVOCATE, Sharon Lechter is the founder of Pay Your Family First, a financial education organization. Sharon serves as a national spokesperson for the National CPA Financial Literacy Commission. In 2008 Sharon was appointed to the first President’s Advisory Council on Financial Literacy, serving both Presidents Bush and Obama.

莎伦 · 莱切特是一位生活长期教育的倡导者，她是一家金融教育机构“支付你的家庭第一”的创始人。沙龙是全国注册会计师金融扫盲委员会的全国发言人。2008年，沙龙被任命为第一任总统金融扫盲顾问委员会成员，为布什总统和奥巴马总统服务。

Sharon is an entrepreneur, author, philanthropist, educator, international speaker, licensed CPA, and mother. She has been a pioneer in developing new technologies, programs, and products to bring education into children’s lives in ways that are innovative, challenging, and fun. Her financial literacy board game, ThriveTime for Teens, an innovative and experiential life and money reality game, has gained recognition with coveted awards including the GOLD Mom’s Choice Award, Creative Child Magazine’s 2010 Game of The Year, Dr. Toy’s Best Vacation Product, and a five-star rating from WTS Toy Reviews. Sharon is recognized as an expert on the topics of financial education for children, personal finance, and entrepreneurship.

莎朗是一位企业家、作家、慈善家、教育家、国际演讲家、注册会计师和母亲。她一直是开发新技术、新项目和新产品的先驱，以创新、富有挑战性和趣味性的方式将教育带入儿童生活。她的理财知识棋盘游戏《青少年的繁华时光》是一款创新的体验式生活和货币现实游戏，获得了众多奖项的认可，包括金妈妈选择奖、创意儿童杂志2010年度游戏、玩具博士的最佳度假产品以及 WTS 玩具评论的五星评级。莎伦是公认的儿童金融教育、个人理财和创业方面的专家。

Sharon authored the national best seller Three Feet from Gold in cooperation with the Napoleon Hill Foundation and Greg Reid. Sharon is also known world-wide as the co-author of the international #1 New York Times best seller Rich Dad Poor Dad and fourteen other books in the Rich Dad series.

沙龙与拿破仑 · 希尔基金会和格雷格 · 里德合作，撰写了全国畅销书《距离金子三英尺》。作为《纽约时报》国际畅销书排行第一的《富爸爸》和《富爸爸》系列的另外十四本书的合著者，莎朗也是闻名世界的。

A committed philanthropist, Sharon also gives back to world communities as both a volunteer and benefactor. Sharon serves on the national boards of the Women Presidents’ Organization, and Child-help, a national organization founded to prevent and treat child abuse.

作为一个坚定的慈善家，沙龙还以志愿者和捐助者的身份回馈世界社区。沙龙是妇女总统组织和儿童帮助组织的全国委员会成员，这是一个旨在预防和治疗虐待儿童行为的全国性组织。

• Advance the concept of private enterprise offered under the American System

推进美国制度下提供的私营企业概念

•强调诚实、道德和正直作为美国精神基石的重要性

• Aid in the development of individuals to help them reach their own potential

* 帮助个人发展，帮助他们实现自己的潜力

• Overcome the self-imposed limitations of fear, doubt and procrastination

•克服恐惧、怀疑和拖延的自我限制

• Help people rise from poverty, physical handicaps, and other disadvantages to high positions, wealth and acquire the true riches of life

激励个人激励自己取得高成就
